00099 static void bochs_port_e9_flush() {
00100         if (!bochs_port_e9_line.empty()) {
00101                 LOG_MSG("Bochs port E9h: %s",bochs_port_e9_line.c_str());
00102                 bochs_port_e9_line.clear();
00103         }
00104 }
00105 
00106 void bochs_port_e9_write(Bitu port,Bitu val,Bitu /*iolen*/) {
00107         if (val == '\n' || val == '\r') {
00108                 bochs_port_e9_flush();
00109         }
00110         else {
00111                 bochs_port_e9_line += (char)val;
00112                 if (bochs_port_e9_line.length() >= 256)
00113                         bochs_port_e9_flush();
00114         }
00115 }

00125 Bitu ROMBIOS_MinAllocatedLoc() {
00126         Bitu r = rombios_alloc.getMinAddress();
00127 
00128         if (r > (0x100000 - rombios_minimum_size))
00129                 r = (0x100000 - rombios_minimum_size);
00130 
00131         return r & ~0xFFF;
00132 }
00133 
00134 void ROMBIOS_FreeUnusedMinToLoc(Bitu phys) {
00135         Bitu new_phys;
00136 
00137         if (rombios_minimum_location & 0xFFF) E_Exit("ROMBIOS: FreeUnusedMinToLoc minimum location not page aligned");
00138 
00139         phys &= ~0xFFFUL;
00140         new_phys = rombios_alloc.freeUnusedMinToLoc(phys) & (~0xFFFUL);
00141         assert(new_phys >= phys);
00142         if (phys < new_phys) MEM_unmap_physmem(phys,new_phys-1);
00143         rombios_minimum_location = new_phys;
00144         ROMBIOS_SanityCheck();
00145         ROMBIOS_DumpMemory();
00146 }

00161 static uint32_t dosbox_int_regsel = 0;
00162 static bool dosbox_int_error = false;

00167 struct dosbox_int_saved_state {
00168     unsigned char   dosbox_int_register_shf;
00169     uint32_t        dosbox_int_register;
00170     unsigned char   dosbox_int_regsel_shf;
00171     uint32_t        dosbox_int_regsel;
00172     bool            dosbox_int_error;
00173     bool            dosbox_int_busy;
00174 };
00175 
00176 #define DOSBOX_INT_SAVED_STATE_MAX      4
00177 
00178 struct dosbox_int_saved_state       dosbox_int_saved[DOSBOX_INT_SAVED_STATE_MAX];
00179 int                                 dosbox_int_saved_sp = -1;
00180 
00181 /* for use with interrupt handlers in DOS/Windows that need to save IG state
00182  * to ensure that IG state is restored on return in order to not interfere
00183  * with anything userspace is doing (as an alternative to wrapping all access
00184  * in CLI/STI or PUSHF/CLI/POPF) */
00185 bool dosbox_int_push_save_state(void) {
00186 
00187     if (dosbox_int_saved_sp >= (DOSBOX_INT_SAVED_STATE_MAX-1))
00188         return false;
00189 
00190     struct dosbox_int_saved_state *ss = &dosbox_int_saved[++dosbox_int_saved_sp];
00191 
00192     ss->dosbox_int_register_shf =       dosbox_int_register_shf;
00193     ss->dosbox_int_register =           dosbox_int_register;
00194     ss->dosbox_int_regsel_shf =         dosbox_int_regsel_shf;
00195     ss->dosbox_int_regsel =             dosbox_int_regsel;
00196     ss->dosbox_int_error =              dosbox_int_error;
00197     ss->dosbox_int_busy =               dosbox_int_busy;
00198     return true;
00199 }
00200 
00201 bool dosbox_int_pop_save_state(void) {
00202     if (dosbox_int_saved_sp < 0)
00203         return false;
00204 
00205     struct dosbox_int_saved_state *ss = &dosbox_int_saved[dosbox_int_saved_sp--];
00206 
00207     dosbox_int_register_shf =           ss->dosbox_int_register_shf;
00208     dosbox_int_register =               ss->dosbox_int_register;
00209     dosbox_int_regsel_shf =             ss->dosbox_int_regsel_shf;
00210     dosbox_int_regsel =                 ss->dosbox_int_regsel;
00211     dosbox_int_error =                  ss->dosbox_int_error;
00212     dosbox_int_busy =                   ss->dosbox_int_busy;
00213     return true;
00214 }
00215 
00216 bool dosbox_int_discard_save_state(void) {
00217     if (dosbox_int_saved_sp < 0)
00218         return false;
00219 
00220     dosbox_int_saved_sp--;
00221     return true;
00222 }

00224 extern bool user_cursor_locked;
00225 extern int user_cursor_x,user_cursor_y;
00226 extern int user_cursor_sw,user_cursor_sh;

00228 static std::string dosbox_int_debug_out;

00230 /* read triggered, update the regsel */
00231 void dosbox_integration_trigger_read() {
00232         dosbox_int_error = false;
00233 
00234         switch (dosbox_int_regsel) {
00235                 case 0: /* Identification */
00236                         dosbox_int_register = 0xD05B0740;
00237                         break;
00238                 case 1: /* test */
00239                         break;
00240                 case 2: /* version string */
00241                         if (dosbox_int_ver_read == NULL)
00242                                 dosbox_int_ver_read = dosbox_int_version;
00243 
00244                         dosbox_int_register = 0;
00245                         for (Bitu i=0;i < 4;i++) {
00246                                 if (*dosbox_int_ver_read == 0) {
00247                                         dosbox_int_ver_read = dosbox_int_version;
00248                                         break;
00249                                 }
00250 
00251                                 dosbox_int_register += ((uint32_t)((unsigned char)(*dosbox_int_ver_read++))) << (uint32_t)(i * 8);
00252                         }
00253                         break;
00254                 case 3: /* version number */
00255                         dosbox_int_register = (0x01U/*major*/) + (0x00U/*minor*/ << 8U) + (0x00U/*subver*/ << 16U) + (0x01U/*bump*/ << 24U);
00256                         break;
00257 
00258 //              case 0x804200: /* keyboard input injection -- not supposed to read */
00259 //                      break;
00260 
00261                 case 0x804201: /* keyboard status */
00262                         uint32_t Keyb_ig_status();
00263                         dosbox_int_register = Keyb_ig_status();
00264                         break;
00265 
00266         case 0x434D54: /* read user mouse status */
00267             dosbox_int_register =
00268                 (user_cursor_locked ? (1UL << 0UL) : 0UL);      /* bit 0 = mouse capture lock */
00269             break;
00270 
00271         case 0x434D55: /* read user mouse cursor position */
00272             dosbox_int_register = ((user_cursor_y & 0xFFFFUL) << 16UL) | (user_cursor_x & 0xFFFFUL);
00273             break;
00274 
00275         case 0x434D56: { /* read user mouse cursor position (normalized for Windows 3.x) */
00276             signed long long x = ((signed long long)user_cursor_x << 16LL) / (signed long long)(user_cursor_sw-1);
00277             signed long long y = ((signed long long)user_cursor_y << 16LL) / (signed long long)(user_cursor_sh-1);
00278             if (x < 0x0000LL) x = 0x0000LL;
00279             if (x > 0xFFFFLL) x = 0xFFFFLL;
00280             if (y < 0x0000LL) y = 0x0000LL;
00281             if (y > 0xFFFFLL) y = 0xFFFFLL;
00282             dosbox_int_register = ((unsigned int)y << 16UL) | (unsigned int)x;
00283             } break;
00284 
00285                 case 0xC54010: /* Screenshot/capture trigger */
00286                         /* TODO: This should also be hidden behind an enable switch, so that rogue DOS development
00287                          *       can't retaliate if the user wants to capture video or screenshots. */
00288 #if (C_SSHOT)
00289                         extern Bitu CaptureState;
00290                         dosbox_int_register = 0x00000000; // available
00291                         if (CaptureState & CAPTURE_IMAGE)
00292                                 dosbox_int_register |= 1 << 0; // Image capture is in progress
00293                         if (CaptureState & CAPTURE_VIDEO)
00294                                 dosbox_int_register |= 1 << 1; // Video capture is in progress
00295                         if (CaptureState & CAPTURE_WAVE)
00296                                 dosbox_int_register |= 1 << 2; // WAVE capture is in progress
00297 #else
00298                         dosbox_int_register = 0xC0000000; // not available (bit 31 set), not enabled (bit 30 set)
00299 #endif
00300                         break;
00301 
00302                 case 0xAA55BB66UL: /* interface reset result */
00303                         break;
00304 
00305                 default:
00306                         dosbox_int_register = 0xAA55AA55;
00307                         dosbox_int_error = true;
00308                         break;
00309         };
00310 
00311         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBox integration read 0x%08lx got 0x%08lx (err=%u)\n",
00312                 (unsigned long)dosbox_int_regsel,
00313                 (unsigned long)dosbox_int_register,
00314                 dosbox_int_error?1:0);
00315 }

00317 unsigned int mouse_notify_mode = 0;
00318 // 0 = off
00319 // 1 = trigger as PS/2 mouse interrupt
00320 
00321 /* write triggered */
00322 void dosbox_integration_trigger_write() {
00323         dosbox_int_error = false;
00324 
00325         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBox integration write 0x%08lx val 0x%08lx\n",
00326                 (unsigned long)dosbox_int_regsel,
00327                 (unsigned long)dosbox_int_register);
00328 
00329         switch (dosbox_int_regsel) {
00330                 case 1: /* test */
00331                         break;
00332 
00333                 case 2: /* version string */
00334                         dosbox_int_ver_read = NULL;
00335                         break;
00336 
00337                 case 0xDEB0: /* debug output (to log) */
00338                         for (unsigned int b=0;b < 4;b++) {
00339                                 unsigned char c = (unsigned char)(dosbox_int_register >> (b * 8U));
00340                                 if (c == '\n' || dosbox_int_debug_out.length() >= 200) {
00341                                         LOG_MSG("Client debug message: %s\n",dosbox_int_debug_out.c_str());
00342                                         dosbox_int_debug_out.clear();
00343                                 }
00344                                 else if (c != 0) {
00345                                         dosbox_int_debug_out += ((char)c);
00346                                 }
00347                                 else {
00348                                         break;
00349                                 }
00350                         }
00351                         dosbox_int_register = 0;
00352                         break;
00353 
00354                 case 0xDEB1: /* debug output clear */
00355                         dosbox_int_debug_out.clear();
00356                         break;
00357 
00358                 case 0x52434D: /* release mouse capture 'MCR' */
00359             void GFX_ReleaseMouse(void);
00360             GFX_ReleaseMouse();
00361             break;
00362 
00363                 case 0x804200: /* keyboard input injection */
00364                         void Mouse_ButtonPressed(Bit8u button);
00365                         void Mouse_ButtonReleased(Bit8u button);
00366             void pc98_keyboard_send(const unsigned char b);
00367             void Mouse_CursorMoved(float xrel,float yrel,float x,float y,bool emulate);
00368                         void KEYBOARD_AUX_Event(float x,float y,Bitu buttons,int scrollwheel);
00369                         void KEYBOARD_AddBuffer(Bit16u data);
00370 
00371                         switch ((dosbox_int_register>>8)&0xFF) {
00372                                 case 0x00: // keyboard
00373                     if (IS_PC98_ARCH)
00374                         pc98_keyboard_send(dosbox_int_register&0xFF);
00375                     else
00376                                         KEYBOARD_AddBuffer(dosbox_int_register&0xFF);
00377                                         break;
00378                                 case 0x01: // AUX
00379                     if (!IS_PC98_ARCH)
00380                                         KEYBOARD_AddBuffer((dosbox_int_register&0xFF)|0x100/*AUX*/);
00381                     else   // no such interface in PC-98 mode
00382                         dosbox_int_error = true;
00383                     break;
00384                                 case 0x08: // mouse button injection
00385                                         if (dosbox_int_register&0x80) Mouse_ButtonPressed(dosbox_int_register&0x7F);
00386                                         else Mouse_ButtonReleased(dosbox_int_register&0x7F);
00387                                         break;
00388                                 case 0x09: // mouse movement injection (X)
00389                                         Mouse_CursorMoved(((dosbox_int_register>>16UL) / 256.0f) - 1.0f,0,0,0,true);
00390                                         break;
00391                                 case 0x0A: // mouse movement injection (Y)
00392                                         Mouse_CursorMoved(0,((dosbox_int_register>>16UL) / 256.0f) - 1.0f,0,0,true);
00393                                         break;
00394                                 case 0x0B: // mouse scrollwheel injection
00395                                         // TODO
00396                                         break;
00397                                 default:
00398                                         dosbox_int_error = true;
00399                                         break;
00400                         }
00401                         break;
00402 
00403 //              case 0x804201: /* keyboard status do not write */
00404 //                      break;
00405 
00406         /* this command is used to enable notification of mouse movement over the windows even if the mouse isn't captured */
00407         case 0x434D55: /* read user mouse cursor position */
00408         case 0x434D56: /* read user mouse cursor position (normalized for Windows 3.x) */
00409             mouse_notify_mode = dosbox_int_register & 0xFF;
00410             LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Mouse notify mode=%u",mouse_notify_mode);
00411             break;
00412  
00413                 case 0xC54010: /* Screenshot/capture trigger */
00414 #if (C_SSHOT)
00415                         void CAPTURE_ScreenShotEvent(bool pressed);
00416                         void CAPTURE_VideoEvent(bool pressed);
00417 #endif
00418                         void CAPTURE_WaveEvent(bool pressed);
00419 
00420                         /* TODO: It would be wise to grant/deny access to this register through another dosbox.conf option
00421                          *       so that rogue DOS development cannot shit-spam the capture folder */
00422 #if (C_SSHOT)
00423                         if (dosbox_int_register & 1)
00424                                 CAPTURE_ScreenShotEvent(true);
00425                         if (dosbox_int_register & 2)
00426                                 CAPTURE_VideoEvent(true);
00427 #endif
00428                         if (dosbox_int_register & 4)
00429                                 CAPTURE_WaveEvent(true);
00430                         break;
00431 
00432                 default:
00433                         dosbox_int_register = 0x55AA55AA;
00434                         dosbox_int_error = true;
00435                         break;
00436         };
00437 }
00438 
00439 /* PORT 0x28: Index
00440  *      0x29: Data
00441  *      0x2A: Status(R) or Command(W)
00442  *      0x2B: Not yet assigned
00443  *
00444  *      Registers are 32-bit wide. I/O to index and data rotate through the
00445  *      bytes of the register depending on I/O length, meaning that one 32-bit
00446  *      I/O read will read the entire register, while four 8-bit reads will
00447  *      read one byte out of 4. */
00448 
00449 static Bitu dosbox_integration_port00_index_r(Bitu port,Bitu iolen) {
00450         Bitu retb = 0;
00451         Bitu ret = 0;
00452 
00453     while (iolen > 0) {
00454         ret += ((dosbox_int_regsel >> (dosbox_int_regsel_shf * 8)) & 0xFFU) << (retb * 8);
00455         if ((++dosbox_int_regsel_shf) >= 4) dosbox_int_regsel_shf = 0;
00456         iolen--;
00457         retb++;
00458     }
00459 
00460     return ret;
00461 }
00462 
00463 static void dosbox_integration_port00_index_w(Bitu port,Bitu val,Bitu iolen) {
00464         uint32_t msk;
00465 
00466     while (iolen > 0) {
00467         msk = 0xFFU << (dosbox_int_regsel_shf * 8);
00468         dosbox_int_regsel = (dosbox_int_regsel & ~msk) + ((val & 0xFF) << (dosbox_int_regsel_shf * 8));
00469         if ((++dosbox_int_regsel_shf) >= 4) dosbox_int_regsel_shf = 0;
00470         val >>= 8U;
00471         iolen--;
00472     }
00473 }
00474 
00475 static Bitu dosbox_integration_port01_data_r(Bitu port,Bitu iolen) {
00476         Bitu retb = 0;
00477         Bitu ret = 0;
00478 
00479     while (iolen > 0) {
00480         if (dosbox_int_register_shf == 0) dosbox_integration_trigger_read();
00481         ret += ((dosbox_int_register >> (dosbox_int_register_shf * 8)) & 0xFFU) << (retb * 8);
00482         if ((++dosbox_int_register_shf) >= 4) dosbox_int_register_shf = 0;
00483         iolen--;
00484         retb++;
00485     }
00486 
00487     return ret;
00488 }
00489 
00490 static void dosbox_integration_port01_data_w(Bitu port,Bitu val,Bitu iolen) {
00491         uint32_t msk;
00492 
00493     while (iolen > 0) {
00494         msk = 0xFFU << (dosbox_int_register_shf * 8);
00495         dosbox_int_register = (dosbox_int_register & ~msk) + ((val & 0xFF) << (dosbox_int_register_shf * 8));
00496         if ((++dosbox_int_register_shf) >= 4) dosbox_int_register_shf = 0;
00497         if (dosbox_int_register_shf == 0) dosbox_integration_trigger_write();
00498         val >>= 8U;
00499         iolen--;
00500     }
00501 }
00502 
00503 static Bitu dosbox_integration_port02_status_r(Bitu port,Bitu iolen) {
00504         /* status */
00505     /* 7:6 = regsel byte index
00506      * 5:4 = register byte index
00507      * 3:2 = reserved
00508      *   1 = error
00509      *   0 = busy */
00510     return (dosbox_int_regsel_shf << 6) + (dosbox_int_register_shf << 4) +
00511         (dosbox_int_error ? 2 : 0) + (dosbox_int_busy ? 1 : 0);
00512 }
00513 
00514 static void dosbox_integration_port02_command_w(Bitu port,Bitu val,Bitu iolen) {
00515     switch (val) {
00516         case 0x00: /* reset latch */
00517             dosbox_int_register_shf = 0;
00518             dosbox_int_regsel_shf = 0;
00519             break;
00520         case 0x01: /* flush write */
00521             if (dosbox_int_register_shf != 0) {
00522                 dosbox_integration_trigger_write();
00523                 dosbox_int_register_shf = 0;
00524             }
00525             break;
00526         case 0x20: /* push state */
00527             if (dosbox_int_push_save_state()) {
00528                 dosbox_int_register_shf = 0;
00529                 dosbox_int_regsel_shf = 0;
00530                 dosbox_int_error = false;
00531                 dosbox_int_busy = false;
00532                 dosbox_int_regsel = 0xAA55BB66;
00533                 dosbox_int_register = 0xD05B0C5;
00534                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG state saved");
00535             }
00536             else {
00537                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG unable to push state, stack overflow");
00538                 dosbox_int_error = true;
00539             }
00540             break;
00541         case 0x21: /* pop state */
00542             if (dosbox_int_pop_save_state()) {
00543                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG state restored");
00544             }
00545             else {
00546                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG unable to pop state, stack underflow");
00547                 dosbox_int_error = true;
00548             }
00549             break;
00550         case 0x22: /* discard state */
00551             if (dosbox_int_discard_save_state()) {
00552                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG state discarded");
00553             }
00554             else {
00555                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBOX IG unable to discard state, stack underflow");
00556                 dosbox_int_error = true;
00557             }
00558             break;
00559         case 0x23: /* discard all state */
00560             while (dosbox_int_discard_save_state());
00561             break;
00562         case 0xFE: /* clear error */
00563             dosbox_int_error = false;
00564             break;
00565         case 0xFF: /* reset interface */
00566             dosbox_int_busy = false;
00567             dosbox_int_error = false;
00568             dosbox_int_regsel = 0xAA55BB66;
00569             dosbox_int_register = 0xD05B0C5;
00570             break;
00571         default:
00572             dosbox_int_error = true;
00573             break;
00574     }
00575 }

00579     dosbox_integration_port01_data_r,

00581     NULL

00647 unsigned int APMBIOS_connected_already_err() {

00649                 case APMBIOS_CONNECT_REAL:      return 0x02;
00650                 case APMBIOS_CONNECT_PROT16:    return 0x05;

00657 ISAPnPDevice::ISAPnPDevice() {
00658         CSN = 0;
00659         logical_device = 0;
00660         memset(ident,0,sizeof(ident));
00661         ident_bp = 0;
00662         ident_2nd = 0;
00663         resource_data_len = 0;
00664         resource_data_pos = 0;
00665     resource_data = NULL;
00666     resource_ident = 0;
00667         alloc_res = NULL;
00668         alloc_write = 0;
00669         alloc_sz = 0;
00670 }
00671 
00672 bool ISAPnPDevice::alloc(size_t sz) {
00673         if (sz == alloc_sz)
00674                 return true;
00675 
00676         if (alloc_res == resource_data) {
00677                 resource_data_len = 0;
00678                 resource_data_pos = 0;
00679                 resource_data = NULL;
00680         }
00681         if (alloc_res != NULL)
00682                 delete[] alloc_res;
00683 
00684         alloc_res = NULL;
00685         alloc_write = 0;
00686         alloc_sz = 0;
00687 
00688         if (sz == 0)
00689                 return true;
00690         if (sz > 65536)
00691                 return false;
00692 
00693         alloc_res = new unsigned char[sz];
00694         if (alloc_res == NULL) return false;
00695         memset(alloc_res,0xFF,sz);
00696         alloc_sz = sz;
00697         return true;
00698 }
00699 
00700 ISAPnPDevice::~ISAPnPDevice() {
00701         alloc(0);
00702 }
00703 
00704 void ISAPnPDevice::begin_write_res() {
00705         if (alloc_res == NULL) return;
00706 
00707         resource_data_pos = 0;
00708         resource_data_len = 0;
00709         resource_data = NULL;
00710         alloc_write = 0;
00711 }
00712 
00713 void ISAPnPDevice::write_byte(const unsigned char c) {
00714         if (alloc_res == NULL || alloc_write >= alloc_sz) return;
00715         alloc_res[alloc_write++] = c;
00716 }
00717 
00718 void ISAPnPDevice::write_begin_SMALLTAG(const ISAPnPDevice::SmallTags stag,unsigned char len) {
00719         if (len >= 8 || (unsigned int)stag >= 0x10) return;
00720         write_byte(((unsigned char)stag << 3) + len);
00721 }
00722 
00723 void ISAPnPDevice::write_begin_LARGETAG(const ISAPnPDevice::LargeTags stag,unsigned int len) {
00724         if (len >= 4096) return;
00725         write_byte(0x80 + ((unsigned char)stag));
00726         write_byte(len & 0xFF);
00727         write_byte(len >> 8);
00728 }
00729 
00730 void ISAPnPDevice::write_Device_ID(const char c1,const char c2,const char c3,const char c4,const char c5,const char c6,const char c7) {
00731         write_byte((((unsigned char)c1 & 0x1FU) << 2) + (((unsigned char)c2 & 0x18U) >> 3));
00732         write_byte((((unsigned char)c2 & 0x07U) << 5) + (((unsigned char)c3 & 0x1FU)     ));
00733         write_byte((((unsigned char)c4 & 0x0FU) << 4) + (((unsigned char)c5 & 0x0FU)     ));
00734         write_byte((((unsigned char)c6 & 0x0FU) << 4) + (((unsigned char)c7 & 0x0FU)     ));
00735 }
00736 
00737 void ISAPnPDevice::write_Logical_Device_ID(const char c1,const char c2,const char c3,const char c4,const char c5,const char c6,const char c7) {
00738         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::LogicalDeviceID,5);
00739         write_Device_ID(c1,c2,c3,c4,c5,c6,c7);
00740         write_byte(0x00);
00741 }
00742 
00743 void ISAPnPDevice::write_Compatible_Device_ID(const char c1,const char c2,const char c3,const char c4,const char c5,const char c6,const char c7) {
00744         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::CompatibleDeviceID,4);
00745         write_Device_ID(c1,c2,c3,c4,c5,c6,c7);
00746 }
00747 
00748 void ISAPnPDevice::write_IRQ_Format(const uint16_t IRQ_mask,const unsigned char IRQ_signal_type) {
00749         bool write_irq_info = (IRQ_signal_type != 0);
00750 
00751         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::IRQFormat,write_irq_info?3:2);
00752         write_byte(IRQ_mask & 0xFF);
00753         write_byte(IRQ_mask >> 8);
00754         if (write_irq_info) write_byte(((unsigned char)IRQ_signal_type & 0x0F));
00755 }
00756 
00757 void ISAPnPDevice::write_DMA_Format(const uint8_t DMA_mask,const unsigned char transfer_type_preference,const bool is_bus_master,const bool byte_mode,const bool word_mode,const unsigned char speed_supported) {
00758         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::DMAFormat,2);
00759         write_byte(DMA_mask);
00760         write_byte(
00761                 (transfer_type_preference & 0x03) |
00762                 (is_bus_master ? 0x04 : 0x00) |
00763                 (byte_mode ? 0x08 : 0x00) |
00764                 (word_mode ? 0x10 : 0x00) |
00765                 ((speed_supported & 3) << 5));
00766 }
00767 
00768 void ISAPnPDevice::write_IO_Port(const uint16_t min_port,const uint16_t max_port,const uint8_t count,const uint8_t alignment,const bool full16bitdecode) {
00769         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::IOPortDescriptor,7);
00770         write_byte((full16bitdecode ? 0x01 : 0x00));
00771         write_byte(min_port & 0xFF);
00772         write_byte(min_port >> 8);
00773         write_byte(max_port & 0xFF);
00774         write_byte(max_port >> 8);
00775         write_byte(alignment);
00776         write_byte(count);
00777 }
00778 
00779 void ISAPnPDevice::write_Dependent_Function_Start(const ISAPnPDevice::DependentFunctionConfig cfg,const bool force) {
00780         bool write_cfg_byte = force || (cfg != ISAPnPDevice::DependentFunctionConfig::AcceptableDependentConfiguration);
00781 
00782         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::StartDependentFunctions,write_cfg_byte ? 1 : 0);
00783         if (write_cfg_byte) write_byte((unsigned char)cfg);
00784 }
00785 
00786 void ISAPnPDevice::write_End_Dependent_Functions() {
00787         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::EndDependentFunctions,0);
00788 }
00789 
00790 void ISAPnPDevice::write_nstring(const char *str,const size_t l) {
00791         if (alloc_res == NULL || alloc_write >= alloc_sz) return;
00792 
00793         while (*str != 0 && alloc_write < alloc_sz)
00794                 alloc_res[alloc_write++] = *str++;
00795 }
00796 
00797 void ISAPnPDevice::write_Identifier_String(const char *str) {
00798         const size_t l = strlen(str);
00799         if (l > 4096) return;
00800 
00801         write_begin_LARGETAG(LargeTags::IdentifierStringANSI,l);
00802         if (l != 0) write_nstring(str,l);
00803 }
00804 
00805 void ISAPnPDevice::write_ISAPnP_version(unsigned char major,unsigned char minor,unsigned char vendor) {
00806         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::PlugAndPlayVersionNumber,2);
00807         write_byte((major << 4) + minor);
00808         write_byte(vendor);
00809 }
00810 
00811 void ISAPnPDevice::write_END() {
00812         unsigned char sum = 0;
00813         size_t i;
00814 
00815         write_begin_SMALLTAG(SmallTags::EndTag,/*length*/1);
00816 
00817         for (i=0;i < alloc_write;i++) sum += alloc_res[i];
00818         write_byte((0x100 - sum) & 0xFF);
00819 }
00820 
00821 void ISAPnPDevice::end_write_res() {
00822         if (alloc_res == NULL) return;
00823 
00824         write_END();
00825 
00826         if (alloc_write >= alloc_sz) LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_WARN)("ISA PNP generation overflow");
00827 
00828         resource_data_pos = 0;
00829         resource_data_len = alloc_sz; // the device usually has a reason for allocating the fixed size it does
00830         resource_data = alloc_res;
00831         alloc_write = 0;
00832 }

00839         ident_2nd = 0;
00840         resource_data_pos = 0;
00841         resource_ident = 0;
00842 }

00846         
00847 void ISAPnPDevice::checksum_ident() {
00848         unsigned char checksum = 0x6a,bit;
00849         int i,j;
00850 
00851         for (i=0;i < 8;i++) {
00852                 for (j=0;j < 8;j++) {
00853                         bit = (ident[i] >> j) & 1;
00854                         checksum = ((((checksum ^ (checksum >> 1)) & 1) ^ bit) << 7) | (checksum >> 1);
00855                 }
00856         }
00857 
00858         ident[8] = checksum;
00859 }

00862         resource_ident = 0;
00863 }

00887 class ISAPnPIntegrationDevice : public ISAPnPDevice {

00893                         host_writed(ident+0,ISAPNP_ID('D','O','S',0x1,0x2,0x3,0x4)); /* DOS1234 test device */

00901 class ISAPNP_SysDevNode {
00902 public:
00903         ISAPNP_SysDevNode(const unsigned char *ir,int len,bool already_alloc=false) {
00904                 if (already_alloc) {
00905                         raw = (unsigned char*)ir;
00906                         raw_len = len;
00907                         own = false;
00908                 }
00909                 else {
00910                         if (len > 65535) E_Exit("ISAPNP_SysDevNode data too long");
00911                         raw = new unsigned char[len+1];
00912                         if (ir == NULL) E_Exit("ISAPNP_SysDevNode cannot allocate buffer");
00913                         memcpy(raw,ir,len);
00914                         raw_len = len;
00915                         raw[len] = 0;
00916                         own = true;
00917                 }
00918         }
00919         virtual ~ISAPNP_SysDevNode() {
00920                 if (own) delete[] raw;
00921         }
00922 public:
00923         unsigned char*          raw;
00924         int                     raw_len;
00925         bool                    own;
00926 };

00937                 ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[i] = NULL;
00938         }

00941         ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount=0;
00942 }

00949                         delete ISA_PNP_devs[i];
00950                         ISA_PNP_devs[i] = NULL;
00951                 }
00952         }
00953         for (i=0;i < MAX_ISA_PNP_SYSDEVNODES;i++) {
00954                 if (ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[i] != NULL) delete ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[i];
00955                 ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[i] = NULL;

00959         ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount=0;
00960 }

00962 void ISA_PNP_devreg(ISAPnPDevice *x) {
00963         if (ISA_PNP_devnext < MAX_ISA_PNP_DEVICES) {
00964                 if (ISA_PNP_WPORT_BIOS == 0) ISA_PNP_WPORT_BIOS = ISA_PNP_WPORT;
00965                 ISA_PNP_devs[ISA_PNP_devnext++] = x;
00966                 x->CSN = ISA_PNP_devnext;
00967         }
00968 }
00969 
00970 static Bitu isapnp_read_port(Bitu port,Bitu /*iolen*/) {
00971         Bitu ret=0xff;
00972 
00973         switch (ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR) {
00974                 case 0x01:      /* serial isolation */
00975                            if (ISA_PNP_selected && ISA_PNP_selected->CSN == 0) {
00976                                    if (ISA_PNP_selected->ident_bp < 72) {
00977                                            if (ISA_PNP_selected->ident[ISA_PNP_selected->ident_bp>>3] & (1 << (ISA_PNP_selected->ident_bp&7)))
00978                                                    ret = ISA_PNP_selected->ident_2nd ? 0xAA : 0x55;
00979                                            else
00980                                                    ret = 0xFF;
00981 
00982                                            if (++ISA_PNP_selected->ident_2nd >= 2) {
00983                                                    ISA_PNP_selected->ident_2nd = 0;
00984                                                    ISA_PNP_selected->ident_bp++;
00985                                            }
00986                                    }
00987                            }
00988                            else {
00989                                    ret = 0xFF;
00990                            }
00991                            break;
00992                 case 0x04:      /* read resource data */
00993                            if (ISA_PNP_selected) {
00994                                    if (ISA_PNP_selected->resource_ident < 9)
00995                                            ret = ISA_PNP_selected->ident[ISA_PNP_selected->resource_ident++];                      
00996                                    else {
00997                                            /* real-world hardware testing shows that devices act as if there was some fixed block of ROM,
00998                                             * that repeats every 128, 256, 512, or 1024 bytes if you just blindly read from this port. */
00999                                            if (ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_pos < ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_len)
01000                                                    ret = ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data[ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_pos++];
01001 
01002                                            /* that means that if you read enough bytes the ROM loops back to returning the ident */
01003                                            if (ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_pos >= ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_len) {
01004                                                    ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_pos = 0;
01005                                                    ISA_PNP_selected->resource_ident = 0;
01006                                            }
01007                                    }
01008                            }
01009                            break;
01010                 case 0x05:      /* read resource status */
01011                            if (ISA_PNP_selected) {
01012                                    /* real-world hardware testing shows that devices act as if there was some fixed block of ROM,
01013                                     * that repeats every 128, 256, 512, or 1024 bytes if you just blindly read from this port.
01014                                     * therefore, there's always a byte to return. */
01015                                    ret = 0x01;  /* TODO: simulate hardware slowness */
01016                            }
01017                            break;
01018                 case 0x06:      /* card select number */
01019                            if (ISA_PNP_selected) ret = ISA_PNP_selected->CSN;
01020                            break;
01021                 case 0x07:      /* logical device number */
01022                            if (ISA_PNP_selected) ret = ISA_PNP_selected->logical_device;
01023                            break;
01024                 default:        /* pass the rest down to the class */
01025                            if (ISA_PNP_selected) ret = ISA_PNP_selected->read(ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR);
01026                            break;
01027         }
01028 
01029 //      if (1) LOG_MSG("PnP read(%02X) = %02X\n",ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR,ret);
01030         return ret;
01031 }
01032 
01033 void isapnp_write_port(Bitu port,Bitu val,Bitu /*iolen*/) {
01034         Bitu i;
01035 
01036         if (port == 0x279) {
01037 //              if (1) LOG_MSG("PnP addr(%02X)\n",val);
01038                 if (val == isa_pnp_init_keystring[ISA_PNP_KEYMATCH]) {
01039                         if (++ISA_PNP_KEYMATCH == 32) {
01040 //                              LOG_MSG("ISA PnP key -> going to sleep\n");
01041                                 ISA_PNP_CUR_STATE = ISA_PNP_SLEEP;
01042                                 ISA_PNP_KEYMATCH = 0;
01043                                 for (i=0;i < MAX_ISA_PNP_DEVICES;i++) {
01044                                         if (ISA_PNP_devs[i] != NULL) {
01045                                                 ISA_PNP_devs[i]->on_pnp_key();
01046                                         }
01047                                 }
01048                         }
01049                 }
01050                 else {
01051                         ISA_PNP_KEYMATCH = 0;
01052                 }
01053 
01054                 ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR = val;
01055         }
01056         else if (port == 0xA79) {
01057 //              if (1) LOG_MSG("PnP write(%02X) = %02X\n",ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR,val);
01058                 switch (ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR) {
01059                         case 0x00: {    /* RD_DATA */
01060                                 unsigned int np = ((val & 0xFF) << 2) | 3;
01061                                 if (np != ISA_PNP_WPORT) {
01062                                         if (ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT != NULL) {
01063                                                 ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT = NULL;
01064                                                 delete ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT;
01065                                         }
01066 
01067                                         if (np >= 0x200 && np <= 0x3FF) { /* allowable port I/O range according to spec */
01068                                                 LOG_MSG("PNP OS changed I/O read port to 0x%03X (from 0x%03X)\n",np,ISA_PNP_WPORT);
01069 
01070                                                 ISA_PNP_WPORT = np;
01071                                                 ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT = new IO_ReadHandleObject;
01072                                                 ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT->Install(ISA_PNP_WPORT,isapnp_read_port,IO_MB);
01073                                         }
01074                                         else {
01075                                                 LOG_MSG("PNP OS I/O read port disabled\n");
01076 
01077                                                 ISA_PNP_WPORT = 0;
01078                                         }
01079 
01080                                         if (ISA_PNP_selected != NULL) {
01081                                                 ISA_PNP_selected->ident_bp = 0;
01082                                                 ISA_PNP_selected->ident_2nd = 0;
01083                                                 ISA_PNP_selected->resource_data_pos = 0;
01084                                         }
01085                                 }
01086                         } break;
01087                         case 0x02:      /* config control */
01088                                    if (val & 4) {
01089                                            /* ALL CARDS RESET CSN to 0 */
01090                                            for (i=0;i < MAX_ISA_PNP_DEVICES;i++) {
01091                                                    if (ISA_PNP_devs[i] != NULL) {
01092                                                            ISA_PNP_devs[i]->CSN = 0;
01093                                                    }
01094                                            }
01095                                    }
01096                                    if (val & 2) ISA_PNP_CUR_STATE = ISA_PNP_WAIT_FOR_KEY;
01097                                    if ((val & 1) && ISA_PNP_selected) ISA_PNP_selected->config(val);
01098                                    for (i=0;i < MAX_ISA_PNP_DEVICES;i++) {
01099                                            if (ISA_PNP_devs[i] != NULL) {
01100                                                    ISA_PNP_devs[i]->ident_bp = 0;
01101                                                    ISA_PNP_devs[i]->ident_2nd = 0;
01102                                                    ISA_PNP_devs[i]->resource_data_pos = 0;
01103                                            }
01104                                    }
01105                                    break;
01106                         case 0x03: {    /* wake[CSN] */
01107                                 ISA_PNP_selected = NULL;
01108                                 for (i=0;ISA_PNP_selected == NULL && i < MAX_ISA_PNP_DEVICES;i++) {
01109                                         if (ISA_PNP_devs[i] == NULL)
01110                                                 continue;
01111                                         if (ISA_PNP_devs[i]->CSN == val) {
01112                                                 ISA_PNP_selected = ISA_PNP_devs[i];
01113                                                 ISA_PNP_selected->wakecsn(val);
01114                                         }
01115                                 }
01116                                 if (val == 0)
01117                                         ISA_PNP_CUR_STATE = ISA_PNP_ISOLATE;
01118                                 else
01119                                         ISA_PNP_CUR_STATE = ISA_PNP_CONFIG;
01120                                 } break;
01121                         case 0x06:      /* card select number */
01122                                 if (ISA_PNP_selected) ISA_PNP_selected->CSN = val;
01123                                 break;
01124                         case 0x07:      /* logical device number */
01125                                 if (ISA_PNP_selected) ISA_PNP_selected->select_logical_device(val);
01126                                 break;
01127                         default:        /* pass the rest down to the class */
01128                                 if (ISA_PNP_selected) ISA_PNP_selected->write(ISA_PNP_CUR_ADDR,val);
01129                                 break;
01130                 }
01131         }
01132 }
01133 
01134 static Bitu INT15_Handler(void);
01135 
01136 // FIXME: This initializes both APM BIOS and ISA PNP emulation!
01137 //        Need to separate APM BIOS init from ISA PNP init from ISA PNP BIOS init!
01138 //        It might also be appropriate to move this into the BIOS init sequence.
01139 void ISAPNP_Cfg_Reset(Section *sec) {
01140         Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("cpu"));
01141 
01142         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Initializing ISA PnP emulation");
01143 
01144         enable_integration_device = section->Get_bool("integration device");
01145     enable_integration_device_pnp = section->Get_bool("integration device pnp");
01146         ISAPNPBIOS = section->Get_bool("isapnpbios");
01147         APMBIOS = section->Get_bool("apmbios");
01148         APMBIOS_pnp = section->Get_bool("apmbios pnp");
01149         APMBIOS_allow_realmode = section->Get_bool("apmbios allow realmode");
01150         APMBIOS_allow_prot16 = section->Get_bool("apmbios allow 16-bit protected mode");
01151         APMBIOS_allow_prot32 = section->Get_bool("apmbios allow 32-bit protected mode");
01152 
01153         std::string apmbiosver = section->Get_string("apmbios version");
01154 
01155         if (apmbiosver == "1.0")
01156                 APM_BIOS_minor_version = 0;
01157         else if (apmbiosver == "1.1")
01158                 APM_BIOS_minor_version = 1;
01159         else if (apmbiosver == "1.2")
01160                 APM_BIOS_minor_version = 2;
01161         else//auto
01162                 APM_BIOS_minor_version = 2;
01163 
01164     /* PC-98 does not have APM.
01165      * I *think* it has Plug & Play, but probably different from ISA PnP and specific to the C-Bus interface,
01166      * which I have no information on at this time --J.C. */
01167     if (IS_PC98_ARCH)
01168         return;
01169 
01170         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("APM BIOS allow: real=%u pm16=%u pm32=%u version=1.%u",
01171                 APMBIOS_allow_realmode,
01172                 APMBIOS_allow_prot16,
01173                 APMBIOS_allow_prot32,
01174                 APM_BIOS_minor_version);
01175 
01176         if (APMBIOS && (APMBIOS_allow_prot16 || APMBIOS_allow_prot32) && INT15_apm_pmentry == 0) {
01177                 Bitu cb,base;
01178 
01179                 /* NTS: This is... kind of a terrible hack. It basically tricks Windows into executing our
01180                  *      INT 15h handler as if the APM entry point. Except that instead of an actual INT 15h
01181                  *      triggering the callback, a FAR CALL triggers the callback instead (CB_RETF not CB_IRET). */
01182                 /* TODO: We should really consider moving the APM BIOS code in INT15_Handler() out into it's
01183                  *       own function, then having the INT15_Handler() call it as well as directing this callback
01184                  *       directly to it. If you think about it, this hack also lets the "APM entry point" invoke
01185                  *       other arbitrary INT 15h calls which is not valid. */
01186 
01187                 cb = CALLBACK_Allocate();
01188                 INT15_apm_pmentry = CALLBACK_RealPointer(cb);
01189                 LOG_MSG("Allocated APM BIOS pm entry point at %04x:%04x\n",INT15_apm_pmentry>>16,INT15_apm_pmentry&0xFFFF);
01190                 CALLBACK_Setup(cb,INT15_Handler,CB_RETF,"APM BIOS protected mode entry point");
01191 
01192         /* NTS: Actually INT15_Handler is written to act like an interrupt (IRETF) type callback.
01193          *      Prior versions hacked this into something that responds by CB_RETF, however some
01194          *      poking around reveals that CALLBACK_SCF and friends still assume an interrupt
01195          *      stack, thus, the cause of random crashes in Windows was simply that we were
01196          *      flipping flag bits in the middle of the return address on the stack. The other
01197          *      source of random crashes is that the CF/ZF manipulation in INT 15h wasn't making
01198          *      it's way back to Windows, meaning that when APM BIOS emulation intended to return
01199          *      an error (by setting CF), Windows didn't get the memo (CF wasn't set on return)
01200          *      and acted as if the call succeeded, or worse, CF happened to be set on entry and
01201          *      was never cleared by APM BIOS emulation.
01202          *
01203          *      So what we need is:
01204          *
01205          *      PUSHF           ; put flags in right place
01206          *      PUSH    BP      ; dummy FAR pointer
01207          *      PUSH    BP      ; again
01208          *      <callback>
01209          *      POP     BP      ; drop it
01210          *      POP     BP      ; drop it
01211          *      POPF
01212          *      RETF
01213          *
01214          *      Then CALLBACK_SCF can work normally this way.
01215          *
01216          * NTS: We *still* need to separate APM BIOS calls from the general INT 15H emulation though... */
01217         base = Real2Phys(INT15_apm_pmentry);
01218         LOG_MSG("Writing code to %05x\n",(unsigned int)base);
01219 
01220         phys_writeb(base+0x00,0x9C);                             /* pushf */
01221         phys_writeb(base+0x01,0x55);                             /* push (e)bp */
01222         phys_writeb(base+0x02,0x55);                             /* push (e)bp */
01223 
01224         phys_writeb(base+0x03,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                             //GRP 4
01225         phys_writeb(base+0x04,(Bit8u)0x38);                                             //Extra Callback instruction
01226         phys_writew(base+0x05,(Bit16u)cb);                              //The immediate word
01227 
01228         phys_writeb(base+0x07,0x5D);                             /* pop (e)bp */
01229         phys_writeb(base+0x08,0x5D);                             /* pop (e)bp */
01230         phys_writeb(base+0x09,0x9D);                             /* popf */
01231         phys_writeb(base+0x0A,0xCB);                             /* retf */
01232     }
01233 }
01234 
01235 void ISAPNP_Cfg_Init() {
01236         AddVMEventFunction(VM_EVENT_RESET,AddVMEventFunctionFuncPair(ISAPNP_Cfg_Reset));
01237 }
01238 
01239 /* the PnP callback registered two entry points. One for real, one for protected mode. */
01240 static Bitu PNPentry_real,PNPentry_prot;
01241 
01242 static bool ISAPNP_Verify_BiosSelector(Bitu seg) {
01243         if (!cpu.pmode || (reg_flags & FLAG_VM)) {
01244                 return (seg == 0xF000);
01245         } else if (seg == 0)
01246                 return 0;
01247         else {
01248 #if 1
01249                 /* FIXME: Always return true. But figure out how to ask DOSBox the linear->phys
01250                           mapping to determine whether the segment's base address maps to 0xF0000.
01251                           In the meantime disabling this check makes PnP BIOS emulation work with
01252                           Windows 95 OSR2 which appears to give us a segment mapped to a virtual
01253                           address rather than linearly mapped to 0xF0000 as Windows 95 original
01254                           did. */
01255                 return true;
01256 #else
01257                 Descriptor desc;
01258                 cpu.gdt.GetDescriptor(seg,desc);
01259 
01260                 /* TODO: Check desc.Type() to make sure it's a writeable data segment */
01261                 return (desc.GetBase() == 0xF0000);
01262 #endif
01263         }
01264 }
01265 
01266 static bool ISAPNP_CPU_ProtMode() {
01267         if (!cpu.pmode || (reg_flags & FLAG_VM))
01268                 return 0;
01269 
01270         return 1;
01271 }
01272 
01273 static Bitu ISAPNP_xlate_address(Bitu far_ptr) {
01274         if (!cpu.pmode || (reg_flags & FLAG_VM))
01275                 return Real2Phys(far_ptr);
01276         else {
01277                 Descriptor desc;
01278                 cpu.gdt.GetDescriptor(far_ptr >> 16,desc);
01279 
01280                 /* TODO: Check desc.Type() to make sure it's a writeable data segment */
01281                 return (desc.GetBase() + (far_ptr & 0xFFFF));
01282         }
01283 }
