01536 bool ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(const unsigned char *raw,Bitu len,bool already) {
01537         if (ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount >= MAX_ISA_PNP_SYSDEVNODES)
01538                 return false;
01539 
01540         ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount] = new ISAPNP_SysDevNode(raw,len,already);
01541         if (ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount] == NULL)
01542                 return false;
01543         
01544         ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount++;
01545         if (ISAPNP_SysDevNodeLargest < (len+3))
01546                 ISAPNP_SysDevNodeLargest = len+3;
01547 
01548         return true;
01549 }
01550 
01551 /* ISA PnP function calls have their parameters stored on the stack "C" __cdecl style. Parameters
01552  * are either int, long, or FAR pointers. Like __cdecl an assembly language implementation pushes
01553  * the function arguments on the stack BACKWARDS */
01554 static Bitu ISAPNP_Handler(bool protmode /* called from protected mode interface == true */) {
01555         Bitu arg;
01556         Bitu func,BiosSelector;
01557 
01558         /* I like how the ISA PnP spec says that the 16-bit entry points (real and protected) are given 16-bit data segments
01559          * which implies that all segments involved might as well be 16-bit.
01560          *
01561          * Right?
01562          *
01563          * Well, guess what Windows 95 gives us when calling this entry point:
01564          *
01565          *     Segment SS = DS = 0x30  base=0 limit=0xFFFFFFFF
01566          *       SS:SP = 0x30:0xC138BADF or something like that from within BIOS.VXD
01567          *
01568          * Yeah... for a 16-bit code segment call. Right. Typical Microsoft. >:(
01569          *
01570          * This might also explain why my early experiments with Bochs always had the perpetual
01571          * APM BIOS that never worked but was always detected.
01572          *
01573          * ------------------------------------------------------------------------
01574          * Windows 95 OSR2:
01575          *
01576          * Windows 95 OSR2 however uses a 16-bit stack (where the stack segment is based somewhere
01577          * around 0xC1xxxxxx), all we have to do to correctly access it is work through the page tables.
01578          * This is within spec, but now Microsoft sends us a data segment that is based at virtual address
01579          * 0xC2xxxxxx, which is why I had to disable the "verify selector" routine */
01580         arg = SegPhys(ss) + (reg_esp&cpu.stack.mask) + (2*2); /* entry point (real and protected) is 16-bit, expected to RETF (skip CS:IP) */
01581 
01582         if (protmode != ISAPNP_CPU_ProtMode()) {
01583                 //LOG_MSG("ISA PnP %s entry point called from %s. On real BIOSes this would CRASH\n",protmode ? "Protected mode" : "Real mode",
01584                 //      ISAPNP_CPU_ProtMode() ? "Protected mode" : "Real mode");
01585                 reg_ax = 0x84;/* BAD_PARAMETER */
01586                 return 0;
01587         }
01588 
01589         func = mem_readw(arg);
01590 //      LOG_MSG("PnP prot=%u DS=%04x (base=0x%08lx) SS:ESP=%04x:%04x (base=0x%08lx phys=0x%08lx) function=0x%04x\n",
01591 //              (unsigned int)protmode,(unsigned int)SegValue(ds),(unsigned long)SegPhys(ds),
01592 //              (unsigned int)SegValue(ss),(unsigned int)reg_esp,(unsigned long)SegPhys(ss),
01593 //              (unsigned long)arg,(unsigned int)func);
01594 
01595         /* every function takes the form
01596          *
01597          * int __cdecl FAR (*entrypoint)(int Function...);
01598          *
01599          * so the first argument on the stack is an int that we read to determine what the caller is asking
01600          *
01601          * Dont forget in the real-mode world:
01602          *    sizeof(int) == 16 bits
01603          *    sizeof(long) == 32 bits
01604          */    
01605         switch (func) {
01606                 case 0: {               /* Get Number of System Nodes */
01607                         /* int __cdecl FAR (*entrypoint)(int Function,unsigned char FAR *NumNodes,unsigned int FAR *NodeSize,unsigned int BiosSelector);
01608                          *                               ^ +0         ^ +2                        ^ +6                       ^ +10                       = 12 */
01609                         Bitu NumNodes_ptr = mem_readd(arg+2);
01610                         Bitu NodeSize_ptr = mem_readd(arg+6);
01611                         BiosSelector = mem_readw(arg+10);
01612 
01613                         if (!ISAPNP_Verify_BiosSelector(BiosSelector))
01614                                 goto badBiosSelector;
01615 
01616                         if (NumNodes_ptr != 0) mem_writeb(ISAPNP_xlate_address(NumNodes_ptr),ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount);
01617                         if (NodeSize_ptr != 0) mem_writew(ISAPNP_xlate_address(NodeSize_ptr),ISAPNP_SysDevNodeLargest);
01618 
01619                         reg_ax = 0x00;/* SUCCESS */
01620                 } break;
01621                 case 1: {               /* Get System Device Node */
01622                         /* int __cdecl FAR (*entrypoint)(int Function,unsigned char FAR *Node,struct DEV_NODE FAR *devNodeBuffer,unsigned int Control,unsigned int BiosSelector);
01623                          *                               ^ +0         ^ +2                    ^ +6                               ^ +10                ^ +12                       = 14 */
01624                         Bitu Node_ptr = mem_readd(arg+2);
01625                         Bitu devNodeBuffer_ptr = mem_readd(arg+6);
01626                         Bitu Control = mem_readw(arg+10);
01627                         BiosSelector = mem_readw(arg+12);
01628                         unsigned char Node;
01629                         Bitu i=0;
01630 
01631                         if (!ISAPNP_Verify_BiosSelector(BiosSelector))
01632                                 goto badBiosSelector;
01633 
01634                         /* control bits 0-1 must be '01' or '10' but not '00' or '11' */
01635                         if (Control == 0 || (Control&3) == 3) {
01636                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP Get System Device Node: Invalid Control value 0x%04x\n",(int)Control);
01637                                 reg_ax = 0x84;/* BAD_PARAMETER */
01638                                 break;
01639                         }
01640 
01641                         devNodeBuffer_ptr = ISAPNP_xlate_address(devNodeBuffer_ptr);
01642                         Node_ptr = ISAPNP_xlate_address(Node_ptr);
01643                         Node = mem_readb(Node_ptr);
01644                         if (Node >= ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount) {
01645                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP Get System Device Node: Invalid Node 0x%02x (max 0x%04x)\n",(int)Node,(int)ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount);
01646                                 reg_ax = 0x84;/* BAD_PARAMETER */
01647                                 break;
01648                         }
01649 
01650                         ISAPNP_SysDevNode *nd = ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[Node];
01651 
01652                         mem_writew(devNodeBuffer_ptr+0,nd->raw_len+3); /* Length */
01653                         mem_writeb(devNodeBuffer_ptr+2,Node); /* on most PnP BIOS implementations I've seen "handle" is set to the same value as Node */
01654                         for (i=0;i < (Bitu)nd->raw_len;i++)
01655                                 mem_writeb(devNodeBuffer_ptr+i+3,nd->raw[i]);
01656 
01657 //                      LOG_MSG("ISAPNP OS asked for Node 0x%02x\n",Node);
01658 
01659                         if (++Node >= ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount) Node = 0xFF; /* no more nodes */
01660                         mem_writeb(Node_ptr,Node);
01661 
01662                         reg_ax = 0x00;/* SUCCESS */
01663                 } break;
01664                 case 4: {               /* Send Message */
01665                         /* int __cdecl FAR (*entrypoint)(int Function,unsigned int Message,unsigned int BiosSelector);
01666                          *                               ^ +0         ^ +2                 ^ +4                        = 6 */
01667                         Bitu Message = mem_readw(arg+2);
01668                         BiosSelector = mem_readw(arg+4);
01669 
01670                         if (!ISAPNP_Verify_BiosSelector(BiosSelector))
01671                                 goto badBiosSelector;
01672 
01673                         switch (Message) {
01674                                 case 0x41:      /* POWER_OFF */
01675                                         LOG_MSG("Plug & Play OS requested power off.\n");
01676                                         throw 1;        /* NTS: Based on the Reboot handler code, causes DOSBox to cleanly shutdown and exit */
01677                                         reg_ax = 0;
01678                                         break;
01679                                 case 0x42:      /* PNP_OS_ACTIVE */
01680                                         LOG_MSG("Plug & Play OS reports itself active\n");
01681                                         reg_ax = 0;
01682                                         break;
01683                                 case 0x43:      /* PNP_OS_INACTIVE */
01684                                         LOG_MSG("Plug & Play OS reports itself inactive\n");
01685                                         reg_ax = 0;
01686                                         break;
01687                                 default:
01688                                         LOG_MSG("Unknown ISA PnP message 0x%04x\n",(int)Message);
01689                                         reg_ax = 0x82;/* FUNCTION_NOT_SUPPORTED */
01690                                         break;
01691                         }
01692                 } break;
01693                 case 0x40: {            /* Get PnP ISA configuration */
01694                         /* int __cdecl FAR (*entrypoint)(int Function,unsigned char far *struct,unsigned int BiosSelector);
01695                          *                               ^ +0         ^ +2                      ^ +6                        = 8 */
01696                         Bitu struct_ptr = mem_readd(arg+2);
01697                         BiosSelector = mem_readw(arg+6);
01698 
01699                         if (!ISAPNP_Verify_BiosSelector(BiosSelector))
01700                                 goto badBiosSelector;
01701 
01702                         /* struct isapnp_pnp_isa_cfg {
01703                                  uint8_t        revision;
01704                                  uint8_t        total_csn;
01705                                  uint16_t       isa_pnp_port;
01706                                  uint16_t       reserved;
01707                          }; */
01708 
01709                         if (struct_ptr != 0) {
01710                                 Bitu ph = ISAPNP_xlate_address(struct_ptr);
01711                                 mem_writeb(ph+0,0x01);          /* ->revision = 0x01 */
01712                                 mem_writeb(ph+1,ISA_PNP_devnext); /* ->total_csn */
01713                                 mem_writew(ph+2,ISA_PNP_WPORT_BIOS);    /* ->isa_pnp_port */
01714                                 mem_writew(ph+4,0);             /* ->reserved */
01715                         }
01716 
01717                         reg_ax = 0x00;/* SUCCESS */
01718                 } break;
01719                 default:
01720                         //LOG_MSG("Unsupported ISA PnP function 0x%04x\n",func);
01721                         reg_ax = 0x82;/* FUNCTION_NOT_SUPPORTED */
01722                         break;
01723         };
01724 
01725         return 0;
01726 badBiosSelector:
01727         /* return an error. remind the user (possible developer) how lucky he is, a real
01728          * BIOS implementation would CRASH when misused like this */
01729         LOG_MSG("ISA PnP function 0x%04x called with incorrect BiosSelector parameter 0x%04x\n",(int)func,(int)BiosSelector);
01730         LOG_MSG(" > STACK %04X %04X %04X %04X %04X %04X %04X %04X\n",
01731                 mem_readw(arg),         mem_readw(arg+2),       mem_readw(arg+4),       mem_readw(arg+6),
01732                 mem_readw(arg+8),       mem_readw(arg+10),      mem_readw(arg+12),      mem_readw(arg+14));
01733 
01734         reg_ax = 0x84;/* BAD_PARAMETER */
01735         return 0;
01736 }
01737 
01738 static Bitu ISAPNP_Handler_PM(void) {
01739         return ISAPNP_Handler(true);
01740 }
01741 
01742 static Bitu ISAPNP_Handler_RM(void) {
01743         return ISAPNP_Handler(false);
01744 }
01745 
01746 static Bitu INT70_Handler(void) {
01747         /* Acknowledge irq with cmos */
01748         IO_Write(0x70,0xc);
01749         IO_Read(0x71);
01750         if (mem_readb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE)) {
01751                 Bit32u count=mem_readd(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT);
01752                 if (count>997) {
01753                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT,count-997);
01754                 } else {
01755                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT,0);
01756                         PhysPt where=Real2Phys(mem_readd(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_POINTER));
01757                         mem_writeb(where,mem_readb(where)|0x80);
01758                         mem_writeb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE,0);
01759                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_POINTER,RealMake(0,BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_TEMP));
01760                         IO_Write(0x70,0xb);
01761                         IO_Write(0x71,IO_Read(0x71)&~0x40);
01762                 }
01763         } 
01764         /* Signal EOI to both pics */
01765         IO_Write(0xa0,0x20);
01766         IO_Write(0x20,0x20);
01767         return 0;
01768 }
01769 
01770 CALLBACK_HandlerObject* tandy_DAC_callback[2];
01771 static struct {
01772         Bit16u port;
01773         Bit8u irq;
01774         Bit8u dma;
01775 } tandy_sb;
01776 static struct {
01777         Bit16u port;
01778         Bit8u irq;
01779         Bit8u dma;
01780 } tandy_dac;
01781 
01782 static bool Tandy_InitializeSB() {
01783         /* see if soundblaster module available and at what port/IRQ/DMA */
01784         Bitu sbport, sbirq, sbdma;
01785         if (SB_Get_Address(sbport, sbirq, sbdma)) {
01786                 tandy_sb.port=(Bit16u)(sbport&0xffff);
01787                 tandy_sb.irq =(Bit8u)(sbirq&0xff);
01788                 tandy_sb.dma =(Bit8u)(sbdma&0xff);
01789                 return true;
01790         } else {
01791                 /* no soundblaster accessible, disable Tandy DAC */
01792                 tandy_sb.port=0;
01793                 return false;
01794         }
01795 }
01796 
01797 static bool Tandy_InitializeTS() {
01798         /* see if Tandy DAC module available and at what port/IRQ/DMA */
01799         Bitu tsport, tsirq, tsdma;
01800         if (TS_Get_Address(tsport, tsirq, tsdma)) {
01801                 tandy_dac.port=(Bit16u)(tsport&0xffff);
01802                 tandy_dac.irq =(Bit8u)(tsirq&0xff);
01803                 tandy_dac.dma =(Bit8u)(tsdma&0xff);
01804                 return true;
01805         } else {
01806                 /* no Tandy DAC accessible */
01807                 tandy_dac.port=0;
01808                 return false;
01809         }
01810 }
01811 
01812 /* check if Tandy DAC is still playing */
01813 static bool Tandy_TransferInProgress(void) {
01814         if (real_readw(0x40,0xd0)) return true;                 /* not yet done */
01815         if (real_readb(0x40,0xd4)==0xff) return false;  /* still in init-state */
01816 
01817         Bit8u tandy_dma = 1;
01818         if (tandy_sb.port) tandy_dma = tandy_sb.dma;
01819         else if (tandy_dac.port) tandy_dma = tandy_dac.dma;
01820 
01821         IO_Write(0x0c,0x00);
01822         Bit16u datalen=(Bit8u)(IO_ReadB(tandy_dma*2+1)&0xff);
01823         datalen|=(IO_ReadB(tandy_dma*2+1)<<8);
01824         if (datalen==0xffff) return false;      /* no DMA transfer */
01825         else if ((datalen<0x10) && (real_readb(0x40,0xd4)==0x0f) && (real_readw(0x40,0xd2)==0x1c)) {
01826                 /* stop already requested */
01827                 return false;
01828         }
01829         return true;
01830 }
01831 
01832 static void Tandy_SetupTransfer(PhysPt bufpt,bool isplayback) {
01833         Bitu length=real_readw(0x40,0xd0);
01834         if (length==0) return;  /* nothing to do... */
01835 
01836         if ((tandy_sb.port==0) && (tandy_dac.port==0)) return;
01837 
01838         Bit8u tandy_irq = 7;
01839         if (tandy_sb.port) tandy_irq = tandy_sb.irq;
01840         else if (tandy_dac.port) tandy_irq = tandy_dac.irq;
01841         Bit8u tandy_irq_vector = tandy_irq;
01842         if (tandy_irq_vector<8) tandy_irq_vector += 8;
01843         else tandy_irq_vector += (0x70-8);
01844 
01845         /* revector IRQ-handler if necessary */
01846         RealPt current_irq=RealGetVec(tandy_irq_vector);
01847         if (current_irq!=tandy_DAC_callback[0]->Get_RealPointer()) {
01848                 real_writed(0x40,0xd6,current_irq);
01849                 RealSetVec(tandy_irq_vector,tandy_DAC_callback[0]->Get_RealPointer());
01850         }
01851 
01852         Bit8u tandy_dma = 1;
01853         if (tandy_sb.port) tandy_dma = tandy_sb.dma;
01854         else if (tandy_dac.port) tandy_dma = tandy_dac.dma;
01855 
01856         if (tandy_sb.port) {
01857                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0xd0);                               /* stop DMA transfer */
01858                 IO_Write(0x21,IO_Read(0x21)&(~(1<<tandy_irq))); /* unmask IRQ */
01859                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0xd1);                               /* turn speaker on */
01860         } else {
01861                 IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0x60);  /* disable DAC */
01862                 IO_Write(0x21,IO_Read(0x21)&(~(1<<tandy_irq)));                 /* unmask IRQ */
01863         }
01864 
01865         IO_Write(0x0a,0x04|tandy_dma);  /* mask DMA channel */
01866         IO_Write(0x0c,0x00);                    /* clear DMA flipflop */
01867         if (isplayback) IO_Write(0x0b,0x48|tandy_dma);
01868         else IO_Write(0x0b,0x44|tandy_dma);
01869         /* set physical address of buffer */
01870         Bit8u bufpage=(Bit8u)((bufpt>>16)&0xff);
01871         IO_Write(tandy_dma*2,(Bit8u)(bufpt&0xff));
01872         IO_Write(tandy_dma*2,(Bit8u)((bufpt>>8)&0xff));
01873         switch (tandy_dma) {
01874                 case 0: IO_Write(0x87,bufpage); break;
01875                 case 1: IO_Write(0x83,bufpage); break;
01876                 case 2: IO_Write(0x81,bufpage); break;
01877                 case 3: IO_Write(0x82,bufpage); break;
01878         }
01879         real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,bufpage);
01880 
01881         /* calculate transfer size (respects segment boundaries) */
01882         Bit32u tlength=length;
01883         if (tlength+(bufpt&0xffff)>0x10000) tlength=0x10000-(bufpt&0xffff);
01884         real_writew(0x40,0xd0,(Bit16u)(length-tlength));        /* remaining buffer length */
01885         tlength--;
01886 
01887         /* set transfer size */
01888         IO_Write(tandy_dma*2+1,(Bit8u)(tlength&0xff));
01889         IO_Write(tandy_dma*2+1,(Bit8u)((tlength>>8)&0xff));
01890 
01891         Bit16u delay=(Bit16u)(real_readw(0x40,0xd2)&0xfff);
01892         Bit8u amplitude=(Bit8u)((real_readw(0x40,0xd2)>>13)&0x7);
01893         if (tandy_sb.port) {
01894                 IO_Write(0x0a,tandy_dma);       /* enable DMA channel */
01895                 /* set frequency */
01896                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0x40);
01897                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,256-delay*100/358);
01898                 /* set playback type to 8bit */
01899                 if (isplayback) IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0x14);
01900                 else IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0x24);
01901                 /* set transfer size */
01902                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,(Bit8u)(tlength&0xff));
01903                 IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,(Bit8u)((tlength>>8)&0xff));
01904         } else {
01905                 if (isplayback) IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,(IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0x7c) | 0x03);
01906                 else IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,(IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0x7c) | 0x02);
01907                 IO_Write(tandy_dac.port+2,(Bit8u)(delay&0xff));
01908                 IO_Write(tandy_dac.port+3,(Bit8u)(((delay>>8)&0xf) | (amplitude<<5)));
01909                 if (isplayback) IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,(IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0x7c) | 0x1f);
01910                 else IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,(IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0x7c) | 0x1e);
01911                 IO_Write(0x0a,tandy_dma);       /* enable DMA channel */
01912         }
01913 
01914         if (!isplayback) {
01915                 /* mark transfer as recording operation */
01916                 real_writew(0x40,0xd2,(Bit16u)(delay|0x1000));
01917         }
01918 }
01919 
01920 static Bitu IRQ_TandyDAC(void) {
01921         if (tandy_dac.port) {
01922                 IO_Read(tandy_dac.port);
01923         }
01924         if (real_readw(0x40,0xd0)) {    /* play/record next buffer */
01925                 /* acknowledge IRQ */
01926                 IO_Write(0x20,0x20);
01927                 if (tandy_sb.port) {
01928                         IO_Read(tandy_sb.port+0xe);
01929                 }
01930 
01931                 /* buffer starts at the next page */
01932                 Bit8u npage=real_readb(0x40,0xd4)+1;
01933                 real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,npage);
01934 
01935                 Bitu rb=real_readb(0x40,0xd3);
01936                 if (rb&0x10) {
01937                         /* start recording */
01938                         real_writeb(0x40,0xd3,rb&0xef);
01939                         Tandy_SetupTransfer(npage<<16,false);
01940                 } else {
01941                         /* start playback */
01942                         Tandy_SetupTransfer(npage<<16,true);
01943                 }
01944         } else {        /* playing/recording is finished */
01945                 Bit8u tandy_irq = 7;
01946                 if (tandy_sb.port) tandy_irq = tandy_sb.irq;
01947                 else if (tandy_dac.port) tandy_irq = tandy_dac.irq;
01948                 Bit8u tandy_irq_vector = tandy_irq;
01949                 if (tandy_irq_vector<8) tandy_irq_vector += 8;
01950                 else tandy_irq_vector += (0x70-8);
01951 
01952                 RealSetVec(tandy_irq_vector,real_readd(0x40,0xd6));
01953 
01954                 /* turn off speaker and acknowledge soundblaster IRQ */
01955                 if (tandy_sb.port) {
01956                         IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0xd3);
01957                         IO_Read(tandy_sb.port+0xe);
01958                 }
01959 
01960                 /* issue BIOS tandy sound device busy callout */
01961                 SegSet16(cs, RealSeg(tandy_DAC_callback[1]->Get_RealPointer()));
01962                 reg_ip = RealOff(tandy_DAC_callback[1]->Get_RealPointer());
01963         }
01964         return CBRET_NONE;
01965 }
01966 
01967 static void TandyDAC_Handler(Bit8u tfunction) {
01968         if ((!tandy_sb.port) && (!tandy_dac.port)) return;
01969         switch (tfunction) {
01970         case 0x81:      /* Tandy sound system check */
01971                 if (tandy_dac.port) {
01972                         reg_ax=tandy_dac.port;
01973                 } else {
01974                         reg_ax=0xc4;
01975                 }
01976                 CALLBACK_SCF(Tandy_TransferInProgress());
01977                 break;
01978         case 0x82:      /* Tandy sound system start recording */
01979         case 0x83:      /* Tandy sound system start playback */
01980                 if (Tandy_TransferInProgress()) {
01981                         /* cannot play yet as the last transfer isn't finished yet */
01982                         reg_ah=0x00;
01983                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
01984                         break;
01985                 }
01986                 /* store buffer length */
01987                 real_writew(0x40,0xd0,reg_cx);
01988                 /* store delay and volume */
01989                 real_writew(0x40,0xd2,(reg_dx&0xfff)|((reg_al&7)<<13));
01990                 Tandy_SetupTransfer(PhysMake(SegValue(es),reg_bx),reg_ah==0x83);
01991                 reg_ah=0x00;
01992                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
01993                 break;
01994         case 0x84:      /* Tandy sound system stop playing */
01995                 reg_ah=0x00;
01996 
01997                 /* setup for a small buffer with silence */
01998                 real_writew(0x40,0xd0,0x0a);
01999                 real_writew(0x40,0xd2,0x1c);
02000                 Tandy_SetupTransfer(PhysMake(0xf000,0xa084),true);
02001                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02002                 break;
02003         case 0x85:      /* Tandy sound system reset */
02004                 if (tandy_dac.port) {
02005                         IO_Write(tandy_dac.port,(Bit8u)(IO_Read(tandy_dac.port)&0xe0));
02006                 }
02007                 reg_ah=0x00;
02008                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02009                 break;
02010         }
02011 }
02012 
02013 extern bool date_host_forced;
02014 static Bit8u ReadCmosByte (Bitu index) {
02015         IO_Write(0x70, index);
02016         return IO_Read(0x71);
02017 }
02018 
02019 static void WriteCmosByte (Bitu index, Bitu val) {
02020         IO_Write(0x70, index);
02021         IO_Write(0x71, val);
02022 }
02023 
02024 static bool RtcUpdateDone () {
02025         while ((ReadCmosByte(0x0a) & 0x80) != 0) CALLBACK_Idle();
02026         return true;                    // cannot fail in DOSbox
02027 }
02028 
02029 static void InitRtc () {
02030         WriteCmosByte(0x0a, 0x26);              // default value (32768Hz, 1024Hz)
02031 
02032         // leave bits 6 (pirq), 5 (airq), 0 (dst) untouched
02033         // reset bits 7 (freeze), 4 (uirq), 3 (sqw), 2 (bcd)
02034         // set bit 1 (24h)
02035         WriteCmosByte(0x0b, (ReadCmosByte(0x0b) & 0x61) | 0x02);
02036 
02037         ReadCmosByte(0x0c);                             // clear any bits set
02038 }
02039 
02040 static Bitu INT1A_Handler(void) {
02041         CALLBACK_SIF(true);
02042         switch (reg_ah) {
02043         case 0x00:      /* Get System time */
02044                 {
02045                         Bit32u ticks=mem_readd(BIOS_TIMER);
02046                         reg_al=mem_readb(BIOS_24_HOURS_FLAG);
02047                         mem_writeb(BIOS_24_HOURS_FLAG,0); // reset the "flag"
02048                         reg_cx=(Bit16u)(ticks >> 16);
02049                         reg_dx=(Bit16u)(ticks & 0xffff);
02050                         break;
02051                 }
02052         case 0x01:      /* Set System time */
02053                 mem_writed(BIOS_TIMER,(reg_cx<<16)|reg_dx);
02054                 break;
02055         case 0x02:      /* GET REAL-TIME CLOCK TIME (AT,XT286,PS) */
02056                 if(date_host_forced) {
02057                         InitRtc();                                                      // make sure BCD and no am/pm
02058                         if (RtcUpdateDone()) {                          // make sure it's safe to read
02059                                 reg_ch = ReadCmosByte(0x04);    // hours
02060                                 reg_cl = ReadCmosByte(0x02);    // minutes
02061                                 reg_dh = ReadCmosByte(0x00);    // seconds
02062                                 reg_dl = ReadCmosByte(0x0b) & 0x01;     // daylight saving time
02063                         }
02064                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02065                         break;
02066                 }
02067                 IO_Write(0x70,0x04);            //Hours
02068                 reg_ch=IO_Read(0x71);
02069                 IO_Write(0x70,0x02);            //Minutes
02070                 reg_cl=IO_Read(0x71);
02071                 IO_Write(0x70,0x00);            //Seconds
02072                 reg_dh=IO_Read(0x71);
02073                 reg_dl=0;                       //Daylight saving disabled
02074                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02075                 break;
02076         case 0x03:      // set RTC time
02077                 if(date_host_forced) {
02078                         InitRtc();                                                      // make sure BCD and no am/pm
02079                         WriteCmosByte(0x0b, ReadCmosByte(0x0b) | 0x80);         // prohibit updates
02080                         WriteCmosByte(0x04, reg_ch);            // hours
02081                         WriteCmosByte(0x02, reg_cl);            // minutes
02082                         WriteCmosByte(0x00, reg_dh);            // seconds
02083                         WriteCmosByte(0x0b, (ReadCmosByte(0x0b) & 0x7e) | (reg_dh & 0x01));     // dst + implicitly allow updates
02084                 }
02085                 break;
02086         case 0x04:      /* GET REAL-TIME ClOCK DATE  (AT,XT286,PS) */
02087                 if(date_host_forced) {
02088                         InitRtc();                                                      // make sure BCD and no am/pm
02089                         if (RtcUpdateDone()) {                          // make sure it's safe to read
02090                                 reg_ch = ReadCmosByte(0x32);    // century
02091                                 reg_cl = ReadCmosByte(0x09);    // year
02092                                 reg_dh = ReadCmosByte(0x08);    // month
02093                                 reg_dl = ReadCmosByte(0x07);    // day
02094                         }
02095                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02096                         break;
02097                 }
02098                 IO_Write(0x70,0x32);            //Centuries
02099                 reg_ch=IO_Read(0x71);
02100                 IO_Write(0x70,0x09);            //Years
02101                 reg_cl=IO_Read(0x71);
02102                 IO_Write(0x70,0x08);            //Months
02103                 reg_dh=IO_Read(0x71);
02104                 IO_Write(0x70,0x07);            //Days
02105                 reg_dl=IO_Read(0x71);
02106                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02107                 break;
02108         case 0x05:      // set RTC date
02109                 if(date_host_forced) {
02110                         InitRtc();                                                      // make sure BCD and no am/pm
02111                         WriteCmosByte(0x0b, ReadCmosByte(0x0b) | 0x80);         // prohibit updates
02112                         WriteCmosByte(0x32, reg_ch);    // century
02113                         WriteCmosByte(0x09, reg_cl);    // year
02114                         WriteCmosByte(0x08, reg_dh);    // month
02115                         WriteCmosByte(0x07, reg_dl);    // day
02116                         WriteCmosByte(0x0b, (ReadCmosByte(0x0b) & 0x7f));       // allow updates
02117                 }
02118                 break;
02119         case 0x80:      /* Pcjr Setup Sound Multiplexer */
02120                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT1A:80:Setup tandy sound multiplexer to %d",reg_al);
02121                 break;
02122         case 0x81:      /* Tandy sound system check */
02123         case 0x82:      /* Tandy sound system start recording */
02124         case 0x83:      /* Tandy sound system start playback */
02125         case 0x84:      /* Tandy sound system stop playing */
02126         case 0x85:      /* Tandy sound system reset */
02127                 TandyDAC_Handler(reg_ah);
02128                 break;
02129         case 0xb1:              /* PCI Bios Calls */
02130                 if (pcibus_enable) {
02131                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_WARN)("INT1A:PCI bios call %2X",reg_al);
02132                         switch (reg_al) {
02133                                 case 0x01:      // installation check
02134                                         if (PCI_IsInitialized()) {
02135                                                 reg_ah=0x00;
02136                                                 reg_al=0x01;    // cfg space mechanism 1 supported
02137                                                 reg_bx=0x0210;  // ver 2.10
02138                                                 reg_cx=0x0000;  // only one PCI bus
02139                                                 reg_edx=0x20494350;
02140                                                 reg_edi=PCI_GetPModeInterface();
02141                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02142                                         } else {
02143                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02144                                         }
02145                                         break;
02146                                 case 0x02: {    // find device
02147                                         Bitu devnr=0;
02148                                         Bitu count=0x100;
02149                                         Bit32u devicetag=(reg_cx<<16)|reg_dx;
02150                                         Bits found=-1;
02151                                         for (Bitu i=0; i<=count; i++) {
02152                                                 IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(i<<8));     // query unique device/subdevice entries
02153                                                 if (IO_ReadD(0xcfc)==devicetag) {
02154                                                         if (devnr==reg_si) {
02155                                                                 found=i;
02156                                                                 break;
02157                                                         } else {
02158                                                                 // device found, but not the SIth device
02159                                                                 devnr++;
02160                                                         }
02161                                                 }
02162                                         }
02163                                         if (found>=0) {
02164                                                 reg_ah=0x00;
02165                                                 reg_bh=0x00;    // bus 0
02166                                                 reg_bl=(Bit8u)(found&0xff);
02167                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02168                                         } else {
02169                                                 reg_ah=0x86;    // device not found
02170                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02171                                         }
02172                                         }
02173                                         break;
02174                                 case 0x03: {    // find device by class code
02175                                         Bitu devnr=0;
02176                                         Bitu count=0x100;
02177                                         Bit32u classtag=reg_ecx&0xffffff;
02178                                         Bits found=-1;
02179                                         for (Bitu i=0; i<=count; i++) {
02180                                                 IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(i<<8));     // query unique device/subdevice entries
02181                                                 if (IO_ReadD(0xcfc)!=0xffffffff) {
02182                                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(i<<8)|0x08);
02183                                                         if ((IO_ReadD(0xcfc)>>8)==classtag) {
02184                                                                 if (devnr==reg_si) {
02185                                                                         found=i;
02186                                                                         break;
02187                                                                 } else {
02188                                                                         // device found, but not the SIth device
02189                                                                         devnr++;
02190                                                                 }
02191                                                         }
02192                                                 }
02193                                         }
02194                                         if (found>=0) {
02195                                                 reg_ah=0x00;
02196                                                 reg_bh=0x00;    // bus 0
02197                                                 reg_bl=(Bit8u)(found&0xff);
02198                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02199                                         } else {
02200                                                 reg_ah=0x86;    // device not found
02201                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02202                                         }
02203                                         }
02204                                         break;
02205                                 case 0x08:      // read configuration byte
02206                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02207                                         reg_cl=IO_ReadB(0xcfc+(reg_di&3));
02208                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02209                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02210                                         break;
02211                                 case 0x09:      // read configuration word
02212                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02213                                         reg_cx=IO_ReadW(0xcfc+(reg_di&2));
02214                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02215                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02216                                         break;
02217                                 case 0x0a:      // read configuration dword
02218                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02219                                         reg_ecx=IO_ReadD(0xcfc+(reg_di&3));
02220                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02221                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02222                                         break;
02223                                 case 0x0b:      // write configuration byte
02224                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02225                                         IO_WriteB(0xcfc+(reg_di&3),reg_cl);
02226                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02227                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02228                                         break;
02229                                 case 0x0c:      // write configuration word
02230                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02231                                         IO_WriteW(0xcfc+(reg_di&2),reg_cx);
02232                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02233                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02234                                         break;
02235                                 case 0x0d:      // write configuration dword
02236                                         IO_WriteD(0xcf8,0x80000000|(reg_bx<<8)|(reg_di&0xfc));
02237                                         IO_WriteD(0xcfc+(reg_di&3),reg_ecx);
02238                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02239                                         reg_ah=0x00;
02240                                         break;
02241                                 default:
02242                                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT1A:PCI BIOS: unknown function %x (%x %x %x)",
02243                                                 reg_ax,reg_bx,reg_cx,reg_dx);
02244                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02245                                         break;
02246                         }
02247                 }
02248                 else {
02249                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02250                 }
02251                 break;
02252         default:
02253                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT1A:Undefined call %2X",reg_ah);
02254         }
02255         return CBRET_NONE;
02256 }

02259 bool INT16_peek_key(Bit16u &code);

02268     "  C1  ",
02269     "  CU  ",

02281 // shortcuts offered by SHIFT F1-F10. You can bring this onscreen using CTRL+F7. This row shows '*' in col 2.
02282 // [0] is onscreen display, [1] is what is entered to STDIN.
02283 const char *pc98_shcut_key[10][2] = {
02284     "dir a:",   "dir a:\x0D",
02285     "dir b:",   "dir b:\x0D",
02286     "copy  ",   "copy ",
02287     "del   ",   "del ",

02294     "time\x0D ","time\x0D"

02298 
02299 void update_pc98_function_row(bool enable) {
02300     pc98_function_row = enable;
02301 
02302     mem_writeb(0x712,25 - 1 - (pc98_function_row ? 1 : 0));
02303     real_writeb(BIOSMEM_SEG,BIOSMEM_NB_ROWS,25 - 1 - (pc98_function_row ? 1 : 0));
02304 
02305         unsigned char c = real_readb(BIOSMEM_SEG,BIOSMEM_CURSOR_POS);
02306         unsigned char r = real_readb(BIOSMEM_SEG,BIOSMEM_CURSOR_POS+1);
02307     unsigned int o = 80 * 24;
02308 
02309     if (pc98_function_row) {
02310         if (r > 23) r = 23;
02311 
02312         /* draw the function row.
02313          * based on on real hardware:
02314          *
02315          * The function key is 72 chars wide. 4 blank chars on each side of the screen.
02316          * It is divided into two halves, 36 chars each.
02317          * Within each half, aligned to it's side, is 5 x 7 regions.
02318          * 6 of the 7 are inverted. centered in the white block is the function key. */
02319         for (unsigned int i=0;i < 40;) {
02320             mem_writew(0xA0000+((o+i)*2),0x0000);
02321             mem_writeb(0xA2000+((o+i)*2),0xE1);
02322 
02323             mem_writew(0xA0000+((o+(79-i))*2),0x0000);
02324             mem_writeb(0xA2000+((o+(79-i))*2),0xE1);
02325 
02326             if (i >= 3 && i < 38)
02327                 i += 7;
02328             else
02329                 i++;
02330         }
02331 
02332         for (unsigned int i=0;i < 5;i++) {
02333             unsigned int co = 4 + (i * 7);
02334             const char *str = pc98_func_key[i];
02335 
02336             for (unsigned int j=0;j < 6;j++) {
02337                 mem_writew(0xA0000+((o+co+j)*2),str[j]);
02338                 mem_writeb(0xA2000+((o+co+j)*2),0xE5); // white  reverse  visible
02339            }
02340         }
02341 
02342         for (unsigned int i=5;i < 10;i++) {
02343             unsigned int co = 42 + ((i - 5) * 7);
02344             const char *str = pc98_func_key[i];
02345 
02346             for (unsigned int j=0;j < 6;j++) {
02347                 mem_writew(0xA0000+((o+co+j)*2),str[j]);
02348                 mem_writeb(0xA2000+((o+co+j)*2),0xE5); // white  reverse  visible
02349            }
02350         }
02351     }
02352     else {
02353         /* erase the function row */
02354         for (unsigned int i=0;i < 80;i++) {
02355             mem_writew(0xA0000+((o+i)*2),0x0000);
02356             mem_writeb(0xA2000+((o+i)*2),0xE1);
02357         }
02358     }
02359 
02360     real_writeb(BIOSMEM_SEG,BIOSMEM_CURSOR_POS,c);
02361     real_writeb(BIOSMEM_SEG,BIOSMEM_CURSOR_POS+1,r);
02362 
02363     void vga_pc98_direct_cursor_pos(Bit16u address);
02364     vga_pc98_direct_cursor_pos((r*80)+c);
02365 }

02367 void pc98_set_digpal_entry(unsigned char ent,unsigned char grb);
02368 void PC98_show_cursor(bool show);
02369 
02370 static Bitu INT18_PC98_Handler(void) {
02371     Bit16u temp16;
02372 
02373 #if 0
02374     if (reg_ah >= 0x0A) {
02375             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18h unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02376                 reg_ax,
02377                 reg_bx,
02378                 reg_cx,
02379                 reg_dx,
02380                 reg_si,
02381                 reg_di,
02382                 SegValue(ds),
02383                 SegValue(es));
02384     }
02385 #endif
02386  
02387     /* NTS: Based on information gleaned from Neko Project II source code including comments which
02388      *      I've run through GNU iconv to convert from SHIFT-JIS to UTF-8 here in case Google Translate
02389      *      got anything wrong. */
02390     switch (reg_ah) {
02391         case 0x00: /* Reading of key data (キー・データの読みだし) */
02392             /* FIXME: We use the IBM PC/AT keyboard buffer to fake this call.
02393              *        This will be replaced with PROPER emulation once the PC-98 keyboard handler has been
02394              *        updated to write the buffer the way PC-98 BIOSes do it.
02395              *
02396              *        IBM PC/AT keyboard buffer at 40:1E-40:3D
02397              *
02398              *        PC-98 keyboard buffer at 50:02-50:21 */
02399             /* This call blocks until keyboard input */
02400             if (INT16_get_key(temp16)) {
02401                 reg_ax = temp16;
02402             }
02403             else {
02404                 reg_ip += 1; /* step over IRET, to NOPs which then JMP back to callback */
02405             }
02406             break;
02407         case 0x01: /* Sense of key buffer state (キー・バッファ状態のセンス) */
02408             /* This call returns whether or not there is input waiting.
02409              * The waiting data is read, but NOT discarded from the buffer. */
02410             if (INT16_peek_key(temp16)) {
02411                 reg_ax = temp16;
02412                 reg_bh = 1;
02413             }
02414             else {
02415                 reg_bh = 0;
02416             }
02417             break;
02418         case 0x02: /* Sense of shift key state (シフト・キー状態のセンス) */
02419             reg_al = mem_readb(0x52A + 0x0E); /* FIXME: Seems to match 14th bitmap byte. Does real hardware do this?? */
02420             break;
02421         case 0x03: /* Initialization of keyboard interface (キーボード・インタフェイスの初期化) */
02422             /* TODO */
02423             break;
02424         case 0x04: /* Sense of key input state (キー入力状態のセンス) */
02425             reg_ah = mem_readb(0x52A + (reg_al & 0x0F));
02426             break;
02427         case 0x05: /* Key input sense (キー入力センス) */
02428             /* This appears to return a key from the buffer (and remove from
02429              * buffer) or return BH == 0 to signal no key was pending. */
02430             if (INT16_get_key(temp16)) {
02431                 reg_ax = temp16;
02432                 reg_bh = 1;
02433             }
02434             else {
02435                 reg_bh = 0;
02436             }
02437             break;
02438         // TODO: "Edge" is using INT 18h AH=06h, what is that?
02439         //       Neko Project is also unaware of such a call.
02440         case 0x0C: /* text layer enable */
02441             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].force_fifo_complete();
02442             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].display_enable = true;
02443             break;
02444         case 0x0D: /* text layer disable */
02445             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].force_fifo_complete();
02446             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].display_enable = false;
02447             break;
02448         case 0x0E: /* set text display area (DX=byte offset) */
02449             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].force_fifo_complete();
02450             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].param_ram[0] = (reg_dx >> 1) & 0xFF;
02451             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].param_ram[1] = (reg_dx >> 9) & 0xFF;
02452             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].param_ram[2] = (400 << 4) & 0xFF;
02453             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].param_ram[3] = (400 << 4) >> 8;
02454             break;
02455         case 0x11: /* show cursor */
02456             PC98_show_cursor(true);
02457             break;
02458         case 0x12: /* hide cursor */
02459             PC98_show_cursor(false);
02460             break;
02461         case 0x13: /* set cursor position (DX=byte position) */
02462             void vga_pc98_direct_cursor_pos(Bit16u address);
02463 
02464             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].force_fifo_complete();
02465             vga_pc98_direct_cursor_pos(reg_dx >> 1);
02466             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].cursor_enable = true; // FIXME: Right?
02467             break;
02468         case 0x14: /* read FONT RAM */
02469             {
02470                 unsigned int i,o,r;
02471 
02472                 /* DX = code (must be 0x76xx or 0x7700)
02473                  * BX:CX = 34-byte region to write to */
02474                 if (reg_dh == 0x80) { /* 8x16 ascii */
02475                     i = (reg_bx << 4) + reg_cx + 2;
02476                     mem_writew(i-2,0x0102);
02477                     for (r=0;r < 16;r++) {
02478                         o = (reg_dl*16)+r;
02479 
02480                         assert((o+2) <= sizeof(vga.draw.font));
02481 
02482                         mem_writeb(i+r,vga.draw.font[o]);
02483                     }
02484                 }
02485                 else if ((reg_dh & 0xFC) == 0x28) { /* 8x16 kanji */
02486                     i = (reg_bx << 4) + reg_cx + 2;
02487                     mem_writew(i-2,0x0202);
02488                     for (r=0;r < 16;r++) {
02489                         o = (((((reg_dl & 0x7F)*128)+((reg_dh - 0x20) & 0x7F))*16)+r)*2;
02490 
02491                         assert((o+2) <= sizeof(vga.draw.font));
02492 
02493                         mem_writeb(i+r+0,vga.draw.font[o+0]);
02494                     }
02495                 }
02496                 else if (reg_dh != 0) { /* 16x16 kanji */
02497                     i = (reg_bx << 4) + reg_cx + 2;
02498                     mem_writew(i-2,0x0202);
02499                     for (r=0;r < 16;r++) {
02500                         o = (((((reg_dl & 0x7F)*128)+((reg_dh - 0x20) & 0x7F))*16)+r)*2;
02501 
02502                         assert((o+2) <= sizeof(vga.draw.font));
02503 
02504                         mem_writeb(i+(r*2)+0,vga.draw.font[o+0]);
02505                         mem_writeb(i+(r*2)+1,vga.draw.font[o+1]);
02506                     }
02507                 }
02508                 else {
02509                     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18h AH=14h font RAM read ignored, code 0x%04x not supported",reg_dx);
02510                 }
02511             }
02512             break;
02513         case 0x16: /* fill screen with chr + attr */
02514             {
02515                 /* DL = character
02516                  * DH = attribute */
02517                 unsigned int i;
02518 
02519                 for (i=0;i < 0x2000;i += 2) {
02520                     vga.mem.linear[i+0] = reg_dl;
02521                     vga.mem.linear[i+1] = 0x00;
02522                 }
02523                 for (   ;i < 0x3FE0;i += 2) {
02524                     vga.mem.linear[i+0] = reg_dh;
02525                     vga.mem.linear[i+1] = 0x00;
02526                 }
02527             }
02528             break;
02529         case 0x1A: /* load FONT RAM */
02530             {
02531                 unsigned int i,o,r;
02532 
02533                 /* DX = code (must be 0x76xx or 0x7700)
02534                  * BX:CX = 34-byte region to read from */
02535                 if ((reg_dh & 0x7E) == 0x76) {
02536                     i = (reg_bx << 4) + reg_cx + 2;
02537                     for (r=0;r < 16;r++) {
02538                         o = (((((reg_dl & 0x7F)*128)+((reg_dh - 0x20) & 0x7F))*16)+r)*2;
02539 
02540                         assert((o+2) <= sizeof(vga.draw.font));
02541 
02542                         vga.draw.font[o+0] = mem_readb(i+(r*2)+0);
02543                         vga.draw.font[o+1] = mem_readb(i+(r*2)+1);
02544                     }
02545                 }
02546                 else {
02547                     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18h AH=1Ah font RAM load ignored, code 0x%04x out of range",reg_dx);
02548                 }
02549             }
02550             break;
02551         /* From this point on the INT 18h call list appears to wander off from the keyboard into CRT/GDC/display management. */
02552         case 0x40: /* Start displaying the graphics screen (グラフィック画面の表示開始) */
02553             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].force_fifo_complete();
02554             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].display_enable = true;
02555  
02556             {
02557                 unsigned char b = mem_readb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/);
02558                 mem_writeb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/,b | 0x80);
02559             }
02560             break;
02561         case 0x41: /* Stop displaying the graphics screen (グラフィック画面の表示終了) */
02562             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].force_fifo_complete();
02563             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].display_enable = false;
02564 
02565             {
02566                 unsigned char b = mem_readb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/);
02567                 mem_writeb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/,b & (~0x80));
02568             }
02569             break;
02570         case 0x42: /* Display area setup (表示領域の設定) */
02571             pc98_gdc[GDC_MASTER].force_fifo_complete();
02572             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].force_fifo_complete();
02573             /* reset scroll area of graphics */
02574             if ((reg_ch & 0xC0) == 0x40) { /* 640x200 G-RAM upper half */
02575                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[0] = (200*40) & 0xFF;
02576                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[1] = (200*40) >> 8;
02577             }
02578             else {
02579                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[0] = 0;
02580                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[1] = 0;
02581             }
02582             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[2] = 0xF0;
02583             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].param_ram[3] = 0x3F;
02584             pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].active_display_words_per_line = 40; /* 40 x 16 = 640 pixel wide graphics */
02585 
02586             // CH
02587             //   [7:6] = G-RAM setup
02588             //           00 = no graphics (?)
02589             //           01 = 640x200 upper half
02590             //           10 = 640x200 lower half
02591             //           11 = 640x400
02592 
02593             // FIXME: This is a guess. I have no idea as to actual behavior, yet.
02594             //        This seems to help with clearing the text layer when games start the graphics.
02595             //        This is ALSO how we will detect games that switch on the 200-line double-scan mode vs 400-line mode.
02596             if ((reg_ch & 0xC0) != 0) {
02597                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].doublescan = ((reg_ch & 0xC0) == 0x40) || ((reg_ch & 0xC0) == 0x80);
02598                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].row_height = pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].doublescan ? 2 : 1;
02599             }
02600             else {
02601                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].doublescan = false;
02602                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].row_height = 1;
02603             }
02604 
02605             {
02606                 unsigned char b = mem_readb(0x597);
02607 
02608                 b &= ~3;
02609                 b |= (reg_ch - 1) & 3;
02610 
02611                 mem_writeb(0x597,b);
02612             }
02613 
02614             {
02615                 unsigned char b = mem_readb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/);
02616 
02617                 // Real hardware behavior: graphics selection updated by BIOS to reflect MEMB_PRXCRT state
02618                 pc98_gdc[GDC_SLAVE].display_enable = !!(b & 0x80);
02619             }
02620 
02621             pc98_gdc_vramop &= ~(1 << VOPBIT_ACCESS);
02622             GDC_display_plane = 0;
02623 
02624             prev_pc98_mode42 = reg_ch;
02625 
02626             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18 AH=42h CH=0x%02X",reg_ch);
02627             break;
02628         case 0x43:  // Palette register settings? Only works in digital mode? --leonier
02629                     //
02630                     // This is said to fix Thexder's GAME ARTS logo. --Jonathan C.
02631                     //
02632                     // TODO: Validate this against real PC-98 hardware and BIOS
02633             {
02634                 unsigned int gbcpc = SegValue(ds)*0x10 + reg_bx;
02635                 for(int i=0;i<4;i++)
02636                 {
02637                     unsigned char p=mem_readb(gbcpc+4+i);
02638                     pc98_set_digpal_entry(7-2*i, p&0xF);
02639                     pc98_set_digpal_entry(6-2*i, p>>4);
02640                 }
02641                 LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18 AH=43h CX=0x%04X DS=0x%04X", reg_cx, SegValue(ds));
02642                 break;
02643             }
02644         default:
02645             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 18h unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02646                 reg_ax,
02647                 reg_bx,
02648                 reg_cx,
02649                 reg_dx,
02650                 reg_si,
02651                 reg_di,
02652                 SegValue(ds),
02653                 SegValue(es));
02654             break;
02655     };
02656 
02657     /* FIXME: What do actual BIOSes do when faced with an unknown INT 18h call? */
02658     return CBRET_NONE;
02659 }
02660 
02661 #define PC98_FLOPPY_HIGHDENSITY     0x01
02662 #define PC98_FLOPPY_2HEAD           0x02
02663 #define PC98_FLOPPY_RPM_3MODE       0x04
02664 #define PC98_FLOPPY_RPM_IBMPC       0x08
02665 
02666 unsigned char PC98_BIOS_FLOPPY_BUFFER[32768]; /* 128 << 8 */
02667 
02668 static unsigned int PC98_FDC_SZ_TO_BYTES(unsigned int sz) {
02669     return 128U << sz;
02670 }
02671 
02672 void PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL_GEO_UNPACK(unsigned int &fdc_cyl,unsigned int &fdc_head,unsigned int &fdc_sect,unsigned int &fdc_sz) {
02673     fdc_cyl = reg_cl;
02674     fdc_head = reg_dh;
02675     fdc_sect = reg_dl;
02676     fdc_sz = reg_ch;
02677     if (fdc_sz > 8) fdc_sz = 8;
02678 }
02679 
02680 void PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL(unsigned int flags) {
02681     static unsigned int fdc_cyl=0,fdc_head=0,fdc_sect=0,fdc_sz=0; // FIXME: Rename and move out. Making "static" is a hack here.
02682     Bit32u img_heads=0,img_cyl=0,img_sect=0,img_ssz=0;
02683     unsigned int status;
02684     unsigned int size,accsize,unitsize;
02685     unsigned long memaddr;
02686     imageDisk *floppy;
02687 
02688     /* AL bits[1:0] = which floppy drive */
02689     if ((reg_al & 3) >= 2) {
02690         /* This emulation only supports up to 2 floppy drives */
02691         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02692         reg_ah = 0x00;
02693         /* TODO? Error code? */
02694         return;
02695     }
02696 
02697     floppy = GetINT13FloppyDrive(reg_al & 3);
02698 
02699     /* what to do is in the lower 4 bits of AH */
02700     switch (reg_ah & 0x0F) {
02701         /* TODO: 0x00 = seek to track (in CL) */
02702         /* TODO: 0x01 = test read? */
02703         /* TODO: 0x03 = equipment flags? */
02704         /* TODO: 0x04 = format detect? */
02705         /* TODO: 0x05 = write disk */
02706         /* TODO: 0x07 = recalibrate (seek to track 0) */
02707         /* TODO: 0x0A = Read ID */
02708         /* TODO: 0x0D = Format track */
02709         /* TODO: 0x0E = ?? */
02710         case 0x02: /* read sectors */
02711         case 0x06: /* read sectors (what's the difference from 0x02?) */
02712             /* AH bits[4:4] = If set, seek to track specified */
02713             /* CL           = cylinder (track) */
02714             /* CH           = sector size (0=128 1=256 2=512 3=1024 etc) */
02715             /* DL           = sector number (1-based) */
02716             /* DH           = head */
02717             /* BX           = size (in bytes) of data to read */
02718             /* ES:BP        = buffer to read data into */
02719             if (floppy == NULL) {
02720                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02721                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02722                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02723                 return;
02724             }
02725                 floppy->Get_Geometry(&img_heads, &img_cyl, &img_sect, &img_ssz);
02726 
02727             PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL_GEO_UNPACK(/*&*/fdc_cyl,/*&*/fdc_head,/*&*/fdc_sect,/*&*/fdc_sz);
02728             unitsize = PC98_FDC_SZ_TO_BYTES(fdc_sz);
02729             if (unitsize != img_ssz || img_heads == 0 || img_cyl == 0 || img_sect == 0) {
02730                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02731                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02732                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02733                 return;
02734             }
02735 
02736             size = reg_bx;
02737             memaddr = (SegValue(es) << 4U) + reg_bp;
02738             while (size > 0) {
02739                 accsize = size > unitsize ? unitsize : size;
02740 
02741                 if (floppy->Read_Sector(fdc_head,fdc_cyl,fdc_sect,PC98_BIOS_FLOPPY_BUFFER) != 0) {
02742                     CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02743                     reg_ah = 0x00;
02744                     /* TODO? Error code? */
02745                     return;
02746                 }
02747 
02748                 for (unsigned int i=0;i < accsize;i++)
02749                     mem_writeb(memaddr+i,PC98_BIOS_FLOPPY_BUFFER[i]);
02750 
02751                 memaddr += accsize;
02752                 size -= accsize;
02753 
02754                 if ((++fdc_sect) > img_sect) {
02755                     fdc_sect = 1;
02756                     if ((++fdc_head) >= img_heads) {
02757                         fdc_head = 0;
02758                         fdc_cyl++;
02759                     }
02760                 }
02761             }
02762 
02763             reg_ah = 0x00;
02764             CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02765             break;
02766         case 0x04: /* drive status */
02767             status = 0;
02768 
02769             /* TODO: bit 4 is set if write protected */
02770 
02771             if (reg_al & 0x80) { /* high density */
02772                 status |= 0x01;
02773             }
02774             else { /* double density */
02775                 /* TODO: */
02776                 status |= 0x01;
02777             }
02778 
02779             if ((reg_ax & 0x8F40) == 0x8400) {
02780                 status |= 8;        /* 1MB/640KB format, spindle speed for 3-mode */
02781                 if (reg_ah & 0x40) /* DOSBox-X always supports 1.44MB */
02782                     status |= 4;    /* 1.44MB format, spindle speed for IBM PC format */
02783             }
02784 
02785             if (floppy == NULL)
02786                 status |= 0xC0;
02787 
02788             reg_ah = status;
02789             CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02790             break;
02791         /* TODO: 0x00 = seek to track (in CL) */
02792         /* TODO: 0x01 = test read? */
02793         /* TODO: 0x03 = equipment flags? */
02794         /* TODO: 0x04 = format detect? */
02795         /* TODO: 0x05 = write disk */
02796         /* TODO: 0x07 = recalibrate (seek to track 0) */
02797         /* TODO: 0x0A = Read ID */
02798         /* TODO: 0x0D = Format track */
02799         /* TODO: 0x0E = ?? */
02800         case 0x05: /* write sectors */
02801             /* AH bits[4:4] = If set, seek to track specified */
02802             /* CL           = cylinder (track) */
02803             /* CH           = sector size (0=128 1=256 2=512 3=1024 etc) */
02804             /* DL           = sector number (1-based) */
02805             /* DH           = head */
02806             /* BX           = size (in bytes) of data to read */
02807             /* ES:BP        = buffer to write data from */
02808             if (floppy == NULL) {
02809                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02810                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02811                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02812                 return;
02813             }
02814                 floppy->Get_Geometry(&img_heads, &img_cyl, &img_sect, &img_ssz);
02815 
02816             /* TODO: Error if write protected */
02817 
02818             PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL_GEO_UNPACK(/*&*/fdc_cyl,/*&*/fdc_head,/*&*/fdc_sect,/*&*/fdc_sz);
02819             unitsize = PC98_FDC_SZ_TO_BYTES(fdc_sz);
02820             if (unitsize != img_ssz || img_heads == 0 || img_cyl == 0 || img_sect == 0) {
02821                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02822                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02823                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02824                 return;
02825             }
02826 
02827             size = reg_bx;
02828             memaddr = (SegValue(es) << 4U) + reg_bp;
02829             while (size > 0) {
02830                 accsize = size > unitsize ? unitsize : size;
02831 
02832                 for (unsigned int i=0;i < accsize;i++)
02833                     PC98_BIOS_FLOPPY_BUFFER[i] = mem_readb(memaddr+i);
02834 
02835                 if (floppy->Write_Sector(fdc_head,fdc_cyl,fdc_sect,PC98_BIOS_FLOPPY_BUFFER) != 0) {
02836                     CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02837                     reg_ah = 0x00;
02838                     /* TODO? Error code? */
02839                     return;
02840                 }
02841 
02842                 memaddr += accsize;
02843                 size -= accsize;
02844 
02845                 if ((++fdc_sect) > img_sect) {
02846                     fdc_sect = 1;
02847                     if ((++fdc_head) >= img_heads) {
02848                         fdc_head = 0;
02849                         fdc_cyl++;
02850                     }
02851                 }
02852             }
02853 
02854             reg_ah = 0x00;
02855             CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02856             break;
02857         case 0x07: /* recalibrate (seek to track 0) */
02858             if (floppy == NULL) {
02859                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02860                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02861                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02862                 return;
02863             }
02864 
02865             reg_ah = 0x00;
02866             CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02867             break;
02868         case 0x0A: /* read ID */
02869             if (floppy == NULL) {
02870                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02871                 reg_ah = 0x00;
02872                 /* TODO? Error code? */
02873                 return;
02874             }
02875 
02876                 floppy->Get_Geometry(&img_heads, &img_cyl, &img_sect, &img_ssz);
02877  
02878             if (reg_ah & 0x10) { // seek to track number in CL
02879                 if (reg_cl >= img_cyl) {
02880                     CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02881                     reg_ah = 0x00;
02882                     /* TODO? Error code? */
02883                     return;
02884                 }
02885 
02886                 fdc_cyl = img_cyl;
02887             }
02888 
02889             reg_cl = fdc_cyl;
02890             reg_dh = fdc_head;
02891             reg_dl = fdc_sect;
02892             /* ^ FIXME: A more realistic emulation would return a random number from 1 to N
02893              *          where N=sectors/track because the floppy motor is running and tracks
02894              *          are moving past the head. */
02895             reg_ch = fdc_sz;
02896 
02897             reg_ah = 0x00;
02898             CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02899             break;
02900         default:
02901             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Bh unknown FDC BIOS call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02902                     reg_ax,
02903                     reg_bx,
02904                     reg_cx,
02905                     reg_dx,
02906                     reg_si,
02907                     reg_di,
02908                     SegValue(ds),
02909                     SegValue(es));
02910             CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02911             break;
02912     };
02913 }
02914 
02915 static Bitu INT19_PC98_Handler(void) {
02916     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 19h unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02917         reg_ax,
02918         reg_bx,
02919         reg_cx,
02920         reg_dx,
02921         reg_si,
02922         reg_di,
02923         SegValue(ds),
02924         SegValue(es));
02925 
02926     return CBRET_NONE;
02927 }
02928 
02929 static Bitu INT1A_PC98_Handler(void) {
02930     /* HACK: This makes the "test" program in DOSLIB work.
02931      *       We'll remove this when we implement INT 1Ah */
02932     if (reg_ax == 0x1000) {
02933         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
02934         reg_ax = 0;
02935     }
02936 
02937     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Ah unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02938         reg_ax,
02939         reg_bx,
02940         reg_cx,
02941         reg_dx,
02942         reg_si,
02943         reg_di,
02944         SegValue(ds),
02945         SegValue(es));
02946 
02947     return CBRET_NONE;
02948 }
02949 
02950 static Bitu INT1B_PC98_Handler(void) {
02951     /* As BIOS interfaces for disk I/O go, this is fairly unusual */
02952     switch (reg_al & 0xF0) {
02953         /* floppy disk access */
02954         /* AL bits[1:0] = floppy drive number */
02955         /* Uses INT42 if high density, INT41 if double density */
02956         /* AH bits[3:0] = command */
02957         case 0x90: /* 1.2MB HD */
02958             PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL(PC98_FLOPPY_HIGHDENSITY|PC98_FLOPPY_2HEAD|PC98_FLOPPY_RPM_3MODE);
02959             break;
02960         case 0x30: /* 1.44MB HD (NTS: not supported until the early 1990s) */
02961         case 0xB0:
02962             PC98_BIOS_FDC_CALL(PC98_FLOPPY_HIGHDENSITY|PC98_FLOPPY_2HEAD|PC98_FLOPPY_RPM_IBMPC);
02963             break;
02964         /* TODO: Other disk formats */
02965         /* TODO: Future SASI/SCSI BIOS emulation for hard disk images */
02966         default:
02967             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Bh unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
02968                     reg_ax,
02969                     reg_bx,
02970                     reg_cx,
02971                     reg_dx,
02972                     reg_si,
02973                     reg_di,
02974                     SegValue(ds),
02975                     SegValue(es));
02976             CALLBACK_SCF(true);
02977             break;
02978     };
02979 
02980     return CBRET_NONE;
02981 }
02982 
02983 void PC98_Interval_Timer_Continue(void) {
02984     /* assume: interrupts are disabled */
02985     IO_WriteB(0x71,0x00);
02986     // TODO: What time interval is this supposed to be?
02987     if (PIT_TICK_RATE == PIT_TICK_RATE_PC98_8MHZ)
02988         IO_WriteB(0x71,0x4E);
02989     else
02990         IO_WriteB(0x71,0x60);
02991 
02992     PIC_SetIRQMask(0,false);
02993 }
02994 
02995 unsigned char pc98_dec2bcd(unsigned char c) {
02996     return ((c / 10) << 4) + (c % 10);
02997 }
02998 
02999 static Bitu INT1C_PC98_Handler(void) {
03000     if (reg_ah == 0x00) { /* get time and date */
03001         time_t curtime;
03002         struct tm *loctime;
03003         curtime = time (NULL);
03004         loctime = localtime (&curtime);
03005 
03006         unsigned char tmp[6];
03007 
03008         tmp[0] = pc98_dec2bcd(loctime->tm_year % 100);
03009         tmp[1] = ((loctime->tm_mon + 1) << 4) + loctime->tm_wday;
03010         tmp[2] = pc98_dec2bcd(loctime->tm_mday);
03011         tmp[3] = pc98_dec2bcd(loctime->tm_hour);
03012         tmp[4] = pc98_dec2bcd(loctime->tm_min);
03013         tmp[5] = pc98_dec2bcd(loctime->tm_sec);
03014 
03015         unsigned long mem = (SegValue(es) << 4) + reg_bx;
03016 
03017         for (unsigned int i=0;i < 6;i++)
03018             mem_writeb(mem+i,tmp[i]);
03019     }
03020     else if (reg_ah == 0x02) { /* set interval timer (single event) */
03021         /* es:bx = interrupt handler to execute
03022          * cx = timer interval in ticks (FIXME: what units of time?) */
03023         mem_writew(0x1C,reg_bx);
03024         mem_writew(0x1E,SegValue(es));
03025         mem_writew(0x58A,reg_cx);
03026 
03027         IO_WriteB(0x77,0x36);   /* mode 3, binary, low-byte high-byte 16-bit counter */
03028 
03029         PC98_Interval_Timer_Continue();
03030     }
03031     else if (reg_ah == 0x03) { /* continue interval timer */
03032         PC98_Interval_Timer_Continue();
03033     }
03034     else {
03035         LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Ch unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
03036                 reg_ax,
03037                 reg_bx,
03038                 reg_cx,
03039                 reg_dx,
03040                 reg_si,
03041                 reg_di,
03042                 SegValue(ds),
03043                 SegValue(es));
03044     }
03045 
03046     return CBRET_NONE;
03047 }
03048 
03049 static Bitu INT1D_PC98_Handler(void) {
03050     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Dh unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
03051         reg_ax,
03052         reg_bx,
03053         reg_cx,
03054         reg_dx,
03055         reg_si,
03056         reg_di,
03057         SegValue(ds),
03058         SegValue(es));
03059 
03060     return CBRET_NONE;
03061 }
03062 
03063 static Bitu INT1E_PC98_Handler(void) {
03064     LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Eh unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
03065         reg_ax,
03066         reg_bx,
03067         reg_cx,
03068         reg_dx,
03069         reg_si,
03070         reg_di,
03071         SegValue(ds),
03072         SegValue(es));
03073 
03074     return CBRET_NONE;
03075 }
03076 
03077 void PC98_EXTMEMCPY(void) {
03078     bool enabled = MEM_A20_Enabled();
03079     MEM_A20_Enable(true);
03080 
03081     Bitu   bytes        = ((reg_cx - 1) & 0xFFFF) + 1; // bytes, except that 0 == 64KB
03082     PhysPt data         = SegPhys(es)+reg_bx;
03083     PhysPt source       = (mem_readd(data+0x12) & 0x00FFFFFF) + (mem_readb(data+0x17)<<24);
03084     PhysPt dest         = (mem_readd(data+0x1A) & 0x00FFFFFF) + (mem_readb(data+0x1F)<<24);
03085 
03086     LOG_MSG("PC-98 memcpy: src=0x%x dst=0x%x data=0x%x count=0x%x",
03087         (unsigned int)source,(unsigned int)dest,(unsigned int)data,(unsigned int)bytes);
03088 
03089     MEM_BlockCopy(dest,source,bytes);
03090     MEM_A20_Enable(enabled);
03091     Segs.limit[cs] = 0xFFFF;
03092     Segs.limit[ds] = 0xFFFF;
03093     Segs.limit[es] = 0xFFFF;
03094     Segs.limit[ss] = 0xFFFF;
03095 
03096     CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03097 }
03098 
03099 static Bitu INT1F_PC98_Handler(void) {
03100     switch (reg_ah) {
03101         case 0x90:
03102             /* Copy extended memory */
03103             PC98_EXTMEMCPY();
03104             break;
03105         default:
03106             LOG_MSG("PC-98 INT 1Fh unknown call AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X DS=%04X ES=%04X",
03107                     reg_ax,
03108                     reg_bx,
03109                     reg_cx,
03110                     reg_dx,
03111                     reg_si,
03112                     reg_di,
03113                     SegValue(ds),
03114                     SegValue(es));
03115             CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03116             break;
03117     };
03118 
03119     return CBRET_NONE;
03120 }

03168 /* 
03169  * Define the following define to 1 if you want dosbox to check 
03170  * the system time every 5 seconds and adjust 1/2 a second to sync them.
03171  */
03172 #ifndef DOSBOX_CLOCKSYNC
03173 #define DOSBOX_CLOCKSYNC 0
03174 #endif
03175 
03176 static void BIOS_HostTimeSync() {
03177         /* Setup time and date */
03178         struct timeb timebuffer;
03179         ftime(&timebuffer);
03180         
03181         struct tm *loctime;
03182         loctime = localtime (&timebuffer.time);
03183 
03184         /*
03185         loctime->tm_hour = 23;
03186         loctime->tm_min = 59;
03187         loctime->tm_sec = 45;
03188         loctime->tm_mday = 28;
03189         loctime->tm_mon = 2-1;
03190         loctime->tm_year = 2007 - 1900;
03191         */
03192 
03193         dos.date.day=(Bit8u)loctime->tm_mday;
03194         dos.date.month=(Bit8u)loctime->tm_mon+1;
03195         dos.date.year=(Bit16u)loctime->tm_year+1900;
03196 
03197         Bit32u ticks=(Bit32u)(((double)(
03198                 loctime->tm_hour*3600*1000+
03199                 loctime->tm_min*60*1000+
03200                 loctime->tm_sec*1000+
03201                 timebuffer.millitm))*(((double)PIT_TICK_RATE/65536.0)/1000.0));
03202         mem_writed(BIOS_TIMER,ticks);
03203 }
