03205 // TODO: make option
03206 bool enable_bios_timer_synchronize_keyboard_leds = true;
03207 
03208 void KEYBOARD_SetLEDs(Bit8u bits);
03209 
03210 void BIOS_KEYBOARD_SetLEDs(Bitu state) {
03211         Bitu x = mem_readb(BIOS_KEYBOARD_LEDS);
03212 
03213         x &= ~7;
03214         x |= (state & 7);
03215         mem_writeb(BIOS_KEYBOARD_LEDS,x);
03216         KEYBOARD_SetLEDs(state);
03217 }
03218 
03219 /* PC-98 IRQ 0 system timer */
03220 static Bitu INT8_PC98_Handler(void) {
03221     Bit16u counter = mem_readw(0x58A) - 1;
03222     mem_writew(0x58A,counter);
03223 
03224     /* NTS 2018/02/23: I just confirmed from the ROM BIOS of an actual
03225      *                 PC-98 system that this implementation and Neko Project II
03226      *                 are 100% accurate to what the BIOS actually does.
03227      *                 INT 07h really is the "timer tick" interrupt called
03228      *                 from INT 08h / IRQ 0, and the BIOS really does call
03229      *                 INT 1Ch AH=3 from INT 08h if the tick count has not
03230      *                 yet reached zero.
03231      *
03232      *                 I'm guessing NEC's BIOS developers invented this prior
03233      *                 to the Intel 80286 and it's INT 07h
03234      *                 "Coprocessor not present" exception. */
03235 
03236     if (counter == 0) {
03237         /* mask IRQ 0 */
03238         IO_WriteB(0x02,IO_ReadB(0x02) | 0x01);
03239         /* ack IRQ 0 */
03240         IO_WriteB(0x00,0x20);
03241         /* INT 07h */
03242             CPU_Interrupt(7,CPU_INT_SOFTWARE,reg_eip);
03243     }
03244     else {
03245         /* ack IRQ 0 */
03246         IO_WriteB(0x00,0x20);
03247         /* make sure it continues ticking */
03248         PC98_Interval_Timer_Continue();
03249     }
03250 
03251         return CBRET_NONE;
03252 }
03253 
03254 static Bitu INT8_Handler(void) {
03255         /* Increase the bios tick counter */
03256         Bit32u value = mem_readd(BIOS_TIMER) + 1;
03257         if(value >= 0x1800B0) {
03258                 // time wrap at midnight
03259                 mem_writeb(BIOS_24_HOURS_FLAG,mem_readb(BIOS_24_HOURS_FLAG)+1);
03260                 value=0;
03261         }
03262 
03263         /* Legacy BIOS behavior: This isn't documented at all but most BIOSes
03264            check the BIOS data area for LED keyboard status. If it sees that
03265            value change, then it sends it to the keyboard. This is why on
03266            older DOS machines you could change LEDs by writing to 40:17.
03267            We have to emulate this also because Windows 3.1/9x seems to rely on
03268            it when handling the keyboard from it's own driver. Their driver does
03269            hook the keyboard and handles keyboard I/O by itself, but it still
03270            allows the BIOS to do the keyboard magic from IRQ 0 (INT 8h). Yech. */
03271         if (enable_bios_timer_synchronize_keyboard_leds) {
03272                 Bitu should_be = (mem_readb(BIOS_KEYBOARD_STATE) >> 4) & 7;
03273                 Bitu led_state = (mem_readb(BIOS_KEYBOARD_LEDS) & 7);
03274 
03275                 if (should_be != led_state)
03276                         BIOS_KEYBOARD_SetLEDs(should_be);
03277         }
03278 
03279 #if DOSBOX_CLOCKSYNC
03280         static bool check = false;
03281         if((value %50)==0) {
03282                 if(((value %100)==0) && check) {
03283                         check = false;
03284                         time_t curtime;struct tm *loctime;
03285                         curtime = time (NULL);loctime = localtime (&curtime);
03286                         Bit32u ticksnu = (Bit32u)((loctime->tm_hour*3600+loctime->tm_min*60+loctime->tm_sec)*(float)PIT_TICK_RATE/65536.0);
03287                         Bit32s bios = value;Bit32s tn = ticksnu;
03288                         Bit32s diff = tn - bios;
03289                         if(diff>0) {
03290                                 if(diff < 18) { diff  = 0; } else diff = 9;
03291                         } else {
03292                                 if(diff > -18) { diff = 0; } else diff = -9;
03293                         }
03294              
03295                         value += diff;
03296                 } else if((value%100)==50) check = true;
03297         }
03298 #endif
03299         mem_writed(BIOS_TIMER,value);
03300 
03301         /* decrease floppy motor timer */
03302         Bit8u val = mem_readb(BIOS_DISK_MOTOR_TIMEOUT);
03303         if (val) mem_writeb(BIOS_DISK_MOTOR_TIMEOUT,val-1);
03304         /* and running drive */
03305         mem_writeb(BIOS_DRIVE_RUNNING,mem_readb(BIOS_DRIVE_RUNNING) & 0xF0);
03306         return CBRET_NONE;
03307 }
03308 #undef DOSBOX_CLOCKSYNC
03309

03311         return CBRET_NONE;
03312 }

03314 static Bitu INT12_Handler(void) {
03315         reg_ax=mem_readw(BIOS_MEMORY_SIZE);
03316         return CBRET_NONE;
03317 }
03318 
03319 static Bitu INT17_Handler(void) {
03320         if (reg_ah > 0x2 || reg_dx > 0x2) {     // 0-2 printer port functions
03321                                                                                 // and no more than 3 parallel ports
03322                 LOG_MSG("BIOS INT17: Unhandled call AH=%2X DX=%4x",reg_ah,reg_dx);
03323                 return CBRET_NONE;
03324         }
03325 
03326         switch(reg_ah) {
03327         case 0x00:              // PRINTER: Write Character
03328                 if(parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]!=0) {
03329                         if(parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]->Putchar(reg_al))
03330                                 reg_ah=parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]->getPrinterStatus();
03331                         else reg_ah=1;
03332                 }
03333                 break;
03334         case 0x01:              // PRINTER: Initialize port
03335                 if(parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]!= 0) {
03336                         parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]->initialize();
03337                         reg_ah=parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]->getPrinterStatus();
03338                 }
03339                 break;
03340         case 0x02:              // PRINTER: Get Status
03341                 if(parallelPortObjects[reg_dx] != 0)
03342                         reg_ah=parallelPortObjects[reg_dx]->getPrinterStatus();
03343                 //LOG_MSG("printer status: %x",reg_ah);
03344                 break;
03345         };
03346         return CBRET_NONE;
03347 }
03348 
03349 static bool INT14_Wait(Bit16u port, Bit8u mask, Bit8u timeout, Bit8u* retval) {
03350         double starttime = PIC_FullIndex();
03351         double timeout_f = timeout * 1000.0;
03352         while (((*retval = IO_ReadB(port)) & mask) != mask) {
03353                 if (starttime < (PIC_FullIndex() - timeout_f)) {
03354                         return false;
03355                 }
03356                 CALLBACK_Idle();
03357         }
03358         return true;
03359 }
03360 
03361 static Bitu INT4B_Handler(void) {
03362         /* TODO: This is where the Virtual DMA specification is accessed on modern systems.
03363          *       When we implement that, move this to EMM386 emulation code. */
03364 
03365         if (reg_ax >= 0x8102 && reg_ax <= 0x810D) {
03366                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Guest OS attempted Virtual DMA specification call (INT 4Bh AX=%04x BX=%04x CX=%04x DX=%04x",
03367                         reg_ax,reg_bx,reg_cx,reg_dx);
03368         }
03369         else if (reg_ah == 0x80) {
03370                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Guest OS attempted IBM SCSI interface call");
03371         }
03372         else if (reg_ah <= 0x02) {
03373                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Guest OS attempted TI Professional PC parallel port function AH=%02x",reg_ah);
03374         }
03375         else {
03376                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Guest OS attempted unknown INT 4Bh call AX=%04x",reg_ax);
03377         }
03378         
03379         /* Oh, I'm just a BIOS that doesn't know what the hell you're doing. CF=1 */
03380         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03381         return CBRET_NONE;
03382 }
03383 
03384 static Bitu INT14_Handler(void) {
03385         if (reg_ah > 0x3 || reg_dx > 0x3) {     // 0-3 serial port functions
03386                                                                                 // and no more than 4 serial ports
03387                 LOG_MSG("BIOS INT14: Unhandled call AH=%2X DX=%4x",reg_ah,reg_dx);
03388                 return CBRET_NONE;
03389         }
03390         
03391         Bit16u port = real_readw(0x40,reg_dx*2); // DX is always port number
03392         Bit8u timeout = mem_readb(BIOS_COM1_TIMEOUT + reg_dx);
03393         if (port==0)    {
03394                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_NORMAL)("BIOS INT14: port %d does not exist.",reg_dx);
03395                 return CBRET_NONE;
03396         }
03397         switch (reg_ah) {
03398         case 0x00:      {
03399                 // Initialize port
03400                 // Parameters:                          Return:
03401                 // AL: port parameters          AL: modem status
03402                 //                                                      AH: line status
03403 
03404                 // set baud rate
03405                 Bitu baudrate = 9600;
03406                 Bit16u baudresult;
03407                 Bitu rawbaud=reg_al>>5;
03408                 
03409                 if (rawbaud==0){ baudrate=110;}
03410                 else if (rawbaud==1){ baudrate=150;}
03411                 else if (rawbaud==2){ baudrate=300;}
03412                 else if (rawbaud==3){ baudrate=600;}
03413                 else if (rawbaud==4){ baudrate=1200;}
03414                 else if (rawbaud==5){ baudrate=2400;}
03415                 else if (rawbaud==6){ baudrate=4800;}
03416                 else if (rawbaud==7){ baudrate=9600;}
03417 
03418                 baudresult = (Bit16u)(115200 / baudrate);
03419 
03420                 IO_WriteB(port+3, 0x80);        // enable divider access
03421                 IO_WriteB(port, (Bit8u)baudresult&0xff);
03422                 IO_WriteB(port+1, (Bit8u)(baudresult>>8));
03423 
03424                 // set line parameters, disable divider access
03425                 IO_WriteB(port+3, reg_al&0x1F); // LCR
03426                 
03427                 // disable interrupts
03428                 IO_WriteB(port+1, 0); // IER
03429 
03430                 // get result
03431                 reg_ah=(Bit8u)(IO_ReadB(port+5)&0xff);
03432                 reg_al=(Bit8u)(IO_ReadB(port+6)&0xff);
03433                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03434                 break;
03435         }
03436         case 0x01: // Transmit character
03437                 // Parameters:                          Return:
03438                 // AL: character                        AL: unchanged
03439                 // AH: 0x01                                     AH: line status from just before the char was sent
03440                 //                                                              (0x80 | unpredicted) in case of timeout
03441                 //                                              [undoc] (0x80 | line status) in case of tx timeout
03442                 //                                              [undoc] (0x80 | modem status) in case of dsr/cts timeout
03443 
03444                 // set DTR & RTS on
03445                 IO_WriteB(port+4,0x3);
03446                 // wait for DSR & CTS
03447                 if (INT14_Wait(port+6, 0x30, timeout, &reg_ah)) {
03448                         // wait for TX buffer empty
03449                         if (INT14_Wait(port+5, 0x20, timeout, &reg_ah)) {
03450                                 // fianlly send the character
03451                                 IO_WriteB(port,reg_al);
03452                         } else
03453                                 reg_ah |= 0x80;
03454                 } else // timed out
03455                         reg_ah |= 0x80;
03456 
03457                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03458                 break;
03459         case 0x02: // Read character
03460                 // Parameters:                          Return:
03461                 // AH: 0x02                                     AL: received character
03462                 //                                              [undoc] will be trashed in case of timeout
03463                 //                                                      AH: (line status & 0x1E) in case of success
03464                 //                                                              (0x80 | unpredicted) in case of timeout
03465                 //                                              [undoc] (0x80 | line status) in case of rx timeout
03466                 //                                              [undoc] (0x80 | modem status) in case of dsr timeout
03467 
03468                 // set DTR on
03469                 IO_WriteB(port+4,0x1);
03470 
03471                 // wait for DSR
03472                 if (INT14_Wait(port+6, 0x20, timeout, &reg_ah)) {
03473                         // wait for character to arrive
03474                         if (INT14_Wait(port+5, 0x01, timeout, &reg_ah)) {
03475                                 reg_ah &= 0x1E;
03476                                 reg_al = IO_ReadB(port);
03477                         } else
03478                                 reg_ah |= 0x80;
03479                 } else
03480                         reg_ah |= 0x80;
03481 
03482                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03483                 break;
03484         case 0x03: // get status
03485                 reg_ah=(Bit8u)(IO_ReadB(port+5)&0xff);
03486                 reg_al=(Bit8u)(IO_ReadB(port+6)&0xff);
03487                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03488                 break;
03489 
03490         }
03491         return CBRET_NONE;
03492 }

03494 Bits HLT_Decode(void);
03495 void KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(Bitu val);
03496 unsigned char KEYBOARD_AUX_GetType();
03497 unsigned char KEYBOARD_AUX_DevStatus();
03498 unsigned char KEYBOARD_AUX_Resolution();
03499 unsigned char KEYBOARD_AUX_SampleRate();
03500 void KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer(void);
03501 
03502 static Bitu INT15_Handler(void) {
03503         if( ( machine==MCH_AMSTRAD ) && ( reg_ah<0x07 ) ) {
03504                 switch(reg_ah) {
03505                         case 0x00:
03506                                 // Read/Reset Mouse X/Y Counts.
03507                                 // CX = Signed X Count.
03508                                 // DX = Signed Y Count.
03509                                 // CC.
03510                         case 0x01:
03511                                 // Write NVR Location.
03512                                 // AL = NVR Address to be written (0-63).
03513                                 // BL = NVR Data to be written.
03514 
03515                                 // AH = Return Code.
03516                                 // 00 = NVR Written Successfully.
03517                                 // 01 = NVR Address out of range.
03518                                 // 02 = NVR Data write error.
03519                                 // CC.
03520                         case 0x02:
03521                                 // Read NVR Location.
03522                                 // AL = NVR Address to be read (0-63).
03523 
03524                                 // AH = Return Code.
03525                                 // 00 = NVR read successfully.
03526                                 // 01 = NVR Address out of range.
03527                                 // 02 = NVR checksum error.
03528                                 // AL = Byte read from NVR.
03529                                 // CC.
03530                         default:
03531                                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_NORMAL)("INT15 Unsupported PC1512 Call %02X",reg_ah);
03532                                 return CBRET_NONE;
03533                         case 0x03:
03534                                 // Write VDU Colour Plane Write Register.
03535                                 vga.amstrad.write_plane = reg_al & 0x0F;
03536                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03537                                 break;
03538                         case 0x04:
03539                                 // Write VDU Colour Plane Read Register.
03540                                 vga.amstrad.read_plane = reg_al & 0x03;
03541                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03542                                 break;
03543                         case 0x05:
03544                                 // Write VDU Graphics Border Register.
03545                                 vga.amstrad.border_color = reg_al & 0x0F;
03546                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03547                                 break;
03548                         case 0x06:
03549                                 // Return ROS Version Number.
03550                                 reg_bx = 0x0001;
03551                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03552                                 break;
03553                 }
03554         }
03555         switch (reg_ah) {
03556         case 0x06:
03557                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_NORMAL)("INT15 Unkown Function 6 (Amstrad?)");
03558                 break;
03559         case 0xC0:      /* Get Configuration*/
03560                 CPU_SetSegGeneral(es,biosConfigSeg);
03561                 reg_bx = 0;
03562                 reg_ah = 0;
03563                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03564                 break;
03565         case 0x4f:      /* BIOS - Keyboard intercept */
03566                 /* Carry should be set but let's just set it just in case */
03567                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03568                 break;
03569         case 0x83:      /* BIOS - SET EVENT WAIT INTERVAL */
03570                 {
03571                         if(reg_al == 0x01) { /* Cancel it */
03572                                 mem_writeb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE,0);
03573                                 IO_Write(0x70,0xb);
03574                                 IO_Write(0x71,IO_Read(0x71)&~0x40);
03575                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03576                                 break;
03577                         }
03578                         if (mem_readb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE)) {
03579                                 reg_ah=0x80;
03580                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03581                                 break;
03582                         }
03583                         Bit32u count=(reg_cx<<16)|reg_dx;
03584                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_POINTER,RealMake(SegValue(es),reg_bx));
03585                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT,count);
03586                         mem_writeb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE,1);
03587                         /* Reprogram RTC to start */
03588                         IO_Write(0x70,0xb);
03589                         IO_Write(0x71,IO_Read(0x71)|0x40);
03590                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03591                 }
03592                 break;
03593         case 0x84:      /* BIOS - JOYSTICK SUPPORT (XT after 11/8/82,AT,XT286,PS) */
03594                 if (reg_dx == 0x0000) {
03595                         // Get Joystick button status
03596                         if (JOYSTICK_IsEnabled(0) || JOYSTICK_IsEnabled(1)) {
03597                                 reg_al = IO_ReadB(0x201)&0xf0;
03598                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03599                         } else {
03600                                 // dos values
03601                                 reg_ax = 0x00f0; reg_dx = 0x0201;
03602                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03603                         }
03604                 } else if (reg_dx == 0x0001) {
03605                         if (JOYSTICK_IsEnabled(0)) {
03606                                 reg_ax = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_X(0)*127+128);
03607                                 reg_bx = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_Y(0)*127+128);
03608                                 if(JOYSTICK_IsEnabled(1)) {
03609                                         reg_cx = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_X(1)*127+128);
03610                                         reg_dx = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_Y(1)*127+128);
03611                                 }
03612                                 else {
03613                                         reg_cx = reg_dx = 0;
03614                                 }
03615                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03616                         } else if (JOYSTICK_IsEnabled(1)) {
03617                                 reg_ax = reg_bx = 0;
03618                                 reg_cx = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_X(1)*127+128);
03619                                 reg_dx = (Bit16u)(JOYSTICK_GetMove_Y(1)*127+128);
03620                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03621                         } else {                        
03622                                 reg_ax = reg_bx = reg_cx = reg_dx = 0;
03623                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03624                         }
03625                 } else {
03626                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT15:84:Unknown Bios Joystick functionality.");
03627                 }
03628                 break;
03629         case 0x86:      /* BIOS - WAIT (AT,PS) */
03630                 {
03631                         if (mem_readb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE)) {
03632                                 reg_ah=0x83;
03633                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03634                                 break;
03635                         }
03636                         Bit8u t;
03637                         Bit32u count=(reg_cx<<16)|reg_dx;
03638                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_POINTER,RealMake(0,BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_TEMP));
03639                         mem_writed(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT,count);
03640                         mem_writeb(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_ACTIVE,1);
03641 
03642                         /* if the user has not set the option, warn if IRQs are masked */
03643                         if (!int15_wait_force_unmask_irq) {
03644                                 /* make sure our wait function works by unmasking IRQ 2, and IRQ 8.
03645                                  * (bugfix for 1993 demo Yodel "Mayday" demo. this demo keeps masking IRQ 2 for some stupid reason.) */
03646                                 if ((t=IO_Read(0x21)) & (1 << 2)) {
03647                                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT15:86:Wait: IRQ 2 masked during wait. "
03648                                                 "Consider adding 'int15 wait force unmask irq=true' to your dosbox.conf");
03649                                 }
03650                                 if ((t=IO_Read(0xA1)) & (1 << 0)) {
03651                                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT15:86:Wait: IRQ 8 masked during wait. "
03652                                                 "Consider adding 'int15 wait force unmask irq=true' to your dosbox.conf");
03653                                 }
03654                         }
03655 
03656                         /* Reprogram RTC to start */
03657                         IO_Write(0x70,0xb);
03658                         IO_Write(0x71,IO_Read(0x71)|0x40);
03659                         while (mem_readd(BIOS_WAIT_FLAG_COUNT)) {
03660                                 if (int15_wait_force_unmask_irq) {
03661                                         /* make sure our wait function works by unmasking IRQ 2, and IRQ 8.
03662                                          * (bugfix for 1993 demo Yodel "Mayday" demo. this demo keeps masking IRQ 2 for some stupid reason.) */
03663                                         if ((t=IO_Read(0x21)) & (1 << 2)) {
03664                                                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_WARN)("INT15:86:Wait: IRQ 2 masked during wait. "
03665                                                         "This condition might result in an infinite wait on "
03666                                                         "some BIOSes. Unmasking IRQ to keep things moving along.");
03667                                                 IO_Write(0x21,t & ~(1 << 2));
03668 
03669                                         }
03670                                         if ((t=IO_Read(0xA1)) & (1 << 0)) {
03671                                                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_WARN)("INT15:86:Wait: IRQ 8 masked during wait. "
03672                                                         "This condition might result in an infinite wait on some "
03673                                                         "BIOSes. Unmasking IRQ to keep things moving along.");
03674                                                 IO_Write(0xA1,t & ~(1 << 0));
03675                                         }
03676                                 }
03677 
03678                                 CALLBACK_Idle();
03679                         }
03680                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03681                         break;
03682                 }
03683         case 0x87:      /* Copy extended memory */
03684                 {
03685                         bool enabled = MEM_A20_Enabled();
03686                         MEM_A20_Enable(true);
03687                         Bitu   bytes    = reg_cx * 2;
03688                         PhysPt data             = SegPhys(es)+reg_si;
03689                         PhysPt source   = (mem_readd(data+0x12) & 0x00FFFFFF) + (mem_readb(data+0x17)<<24);
03690                         PhysPt dest             = (mem_readd(data+0x1A) & 0x00FFFFFF) + (mem_readb(data+0x1F)<<24);
03691                         MEM_BlockCopy(dest,source,bytes);
03692                         reg_ax = 0x00;
03693                         MEM_A20_Enable(enabled);
03694                         Segs.limit[cs] = 0xFFFF;
03695                         Segs.limit[ds] = 0xFFFF;
03696                         Segs.limit[es] = 0xFFFF;
03697                         Segs.limit[ss] = 0xFFFF;
03698                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03699                         break;
03700                 }       
03701         case 0x88:      /* SYSTEM - GET EXTENDED MEMORY SIZE (286+) */
03702                 /* This uses the 16-bit value read back from CMOS which is capped at 64MB */
03703                 reg_ax=other_memsystems?0:size_extended;
03704                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_NORMAL)("INT15:Function 0x88 Remaining %04X kb",reg_ax);
03705                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03706                 break;
03707         case 0x89:      /* SYSTEM - SWITCH TO PROTECTED MODE */
03708                 {
03709                         IO_Write(0x20,0x10);IO_Write(0x21,reg_bh);IO_Write(0x21,0);IO_Write(0x21,0xFF);
03710                         IO_Write(0xA0,0x10);IO_Write(0xA1,reg_bl);IO_Write(0xA1,0);IO_Write(0xA1,0xFF);
03711                         MEM_A20_Enable(true);
03712                         PhysPt table=SegPhys(es)+reg_si;
03713                         CPU_LGDT(mem_readw(table+0x8),mem_readd(table+0x8+0x2) & 0xFFFFFF);
03714                         CPU_LIDT(mem_readw(table+0x10),mem_readd(table+0x10+0x2) & 0xFFFFFF);
03715                         CPU_SET_CRX(0,CPU_GET_CRX(0)|1);
03716                         CPU_SetSegGeneral(ds,0x18);
03717                         CPU_SetSegGeneral(es,0x20);
03718                         CPU_SetSegGeneral(ss,0x28);
03719                         Bitu ret = mem_readw(SegPhys(ss)+reg_sp);
03720                         reg_sp+=6;                      //Clear stack of interrupt frame
03721                         CPU_SetFlags(0,FMASK_ALL);
03722                         reg_ax=0;
03723                         CPU_JMP(false,0x30,ret,0);
03724                 }
03725                 break;
03726         case 0x8A:      /* EXTENDED MEMORY SIZE */
03727                 {
03728                         Bitu sz = MEM_TotalPages()*4;
03729                         if (sz >= 1024) sz -= 1024;
03730                         else sz = 0;
03731                         reg_ax = sz & 0xFFFF;
03732                         reg_dx = sz >> 16;
03733                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03734                 }
03735                 break;
03736         case 0x90:      /* OS HOOK - DEVICE BUSY */
03737                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03738                 reg_ah=0;
03739                 break;
03740         case 0x91:      /* OS HOOK - DEVICE POST */
03741                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03742                 reg_ah=0;
03743                 break;
03744         case 0xc2:      /* BIOS PS2 Pointing Device Support */
03745                         /* TODO: Our reliance on AUX emulation means that at some point, AUX emulation
03746                          *       must always be enabled if BIOS PS/2 emulation is enabled. Future planned change:
03747                          *
03748                          *       If biosps2=true and aux=true, carry on what we're already doing now: emulate INT 15h by
03749                          *         directly writing to the AUX port of the keyboard controller.
03750                          *
03751                          *       If biosps2=false, the aux= setting enables/disables AUX emulation as it already does now.
03752                          *         biosps2=false implies that we're emulating a keyboard controller with AUX but no BIOS
03753                          *         support for it (however rare that might be). This gives the user of DOSBox-X the means
03754                          *         to test that scenario especially in case he/she is developing a homebrew OS and needs
03755                          *         to ensure their code can handle cases like that gracefully.
03756                          *
03757                          *       If biosps2=true and aux=false, AUX emulation is enabled anyway, but the keyboard emulation
03758                          *         must act as if the AUX port is not there so the guest OS cannot control it. Again, not
03759                          *         likely on real hardware, but a useful test case for homebrew OS developers.
03760                          *
03761                          *       If you the user set aux=false, then you obviously want to test a system configuration
03762                          *       where the keyboard controller has no AUX port. If you set biosps2=true, then you want to
03763                          *       test an OS that uses BIOS functions to setup the "pointing device" but you do not want the
03764                          *       guest OS to talk directly to the AUX port on the keyboard controller.
03765                          *
03766                          *       Logically that's not likely to happen on real hardware, but we like giving the end-user
03767                          *       options to play with, so instead, if aux=false and biosps2=true, DOSBox-X should print
03768                          *       a warning stating that INT 15h mouse emulation with a PS/2 port is nonstandard and may
03769                          *       cause problems with OSes that need to talk directly to hardware.
03770                          *
03771                          *       It is noteworthy that PS/2 mouse support in MS-DOS mouse drivers as well as Windows 3.x,
03772                          *       Windows 95, and Windows 98, is carried out NOT by talking directly to the AUX port but
03773                          *       instead by relying on the BIOS INT 15h functions here to do the dirty work. For those
03774                          *       scenarios, biosps2=true and aux=false is perfectly safe and does not cause issues.
03775                          *
03776                          *       OSes that communicate directly with the AUX port however (Linux, Windows NT) will not work
03777                          *       unless aux=true. */
03778                 if (en_bios_ps2mouse) {
03779 //                      LOG_MSG("INT 15h AX=%04x BX=%04x\n",reg_ax,reg_bx);
03780                         switch (reg_al) {
03781                                 case 0x00:              // enable/disable
03782                                         if (reg_bh==0) {        // disable
03783                                                 KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xF5);
03784                                                 Mouse_SetPS2State(false);
03785                                                 reg_ah=0;
03786                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03787                                                 KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03788                                         } else if (reg_bh==0x01) {      //enable
03789                                                 if (!Mouse_SetPS2State(true)) {
03790                                                         reg_ah=5;
03791                                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03792                                                         break;
03793                                                 }
03794                                                 KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xF4);
03795                                                 KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03796                                                 reg_ah=0;
03797                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03798                                         } else {
03799                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03800                                                 reg_ah=1;
03801                                         }
03802                                         break;
03803                                 case 0x01:              // reset
03804                                         KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xFF);
03805                                         Mouse_SetPS2State(false);
03806                                         KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03807                                         reg_bx=0x00aa;  // mouse
03808                                         // fall through
03809                                 case 0x05:              // initialize
03810                                         if (reg_bh >= 3 && reg_bh <= 4) {
03811                                                 /* TODO: BIOSes remember this value as the number of bytes to store before
03812                                                  *       calling the device callback. Setting this value to "1" is perfectly
03813                                                  *       valid if you want a byte-stream like mode (at the cost of one
03814                                                  *       interrupt per byte!). Most OSes will call this with BH=3 for standard
03815                                                  *       PS/2 mouse protocol. You can also call this with BH=4 for Intellimouse
03816                                                  *       protocol support, though testing (so far with VirtualBox) shows the
03817                                                  *       device callback still only gets the first three bytes on the stack.
03818                                                  *       Contrary to what you might think, the BIOS does not interpret the
03819                                                  *       bytes at all.
03820                                                  *
03821                                                  *       The source code of CuteMouse 1.9 seems to suggest some BIOSes take
03822                                                  *       pains to repack the 4th byte in the upper 8 bits of one of the WORDs
03823                                                  *       on the stack in Intellimouse mode at the cost of shifting the W and X
03824                                                  *       fields around. I can't seem to find any source on who does that or
03825                                                  *       if it's even true, so I disregard the example at this time.
03826                                                  *
03827                                                  *       Anyway, you need to store off this value somewhere and make use of
03828                                                  *       it in src/ints/mouse.cpp device callback emulation to reframe the
03829                                                  *       PS/2 mouse bytes coming from AUX (if aux=true) or emulate the
03830                                                  *       re-framing if aux=false to emulate this protocol fully. */
03831                                                 LOG_MSG("INT 15h mouse initialized to %u-byte protocol\n",reg_bh);
03832                                                 KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xF6); /* set defaults */
03833                                                 Mouse_SetPS2State(false);
03834                                                 KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03835                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03836                                                 reg_ah=0;
03837                                         }
03838                                         else {
03839                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03840                                                 reg_ah=0x02; /* invalid input */
03841                                         }
03842                                         break;
03843                                 case 0x02: {            // set sampling rate
03844                                         static const unsigned char tbl[7] = {10,20,40,60,80,100,200};
03845                                         KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xF3);
03846                                         if (reg_bl > 6) reg_bl = 6;
03847                                         KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(tbl[reg_bh]);
03848                                         KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03849                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03850                                         reg_ah=0;
03851                                         } break;
03852                                 case 0x03:              // set resolution
03853                                         KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xE8);
03854                                         KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(reg_bh&3);
03855                                         KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03856                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03857                                         reg_ah=0;
03858                                         break;
03859                                 case 0x04:              // get type
03860                                         reg_bh=KEYBOARD_AUX_GetType();  // ID
03861                                         LOG_MSG("INT 15h reporting mouse device ID 0x%02x\n",reg_bh);
03862                                         KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03863                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03864                                         reg_ah=0;
03865                                         break;
03866                                 case 0x06:              // extended commands
03867                                         if (reg_bh == 0x00) {
03868                                                 /* Read device status and info.
03869                                                  * Windows 9x does not appear to use this, but Windows NT 3.1 does (prior to entering
03870                                                  * full 32-bit protected mode) */
03871                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03872                                                 reg_bx=KEYBOARD_AUX_DevStatus();
03873                                                 reg_cx=KEYBOARD_AUX_Resolution();
03874                                                 reg_dx=KEYBOARD_AUX_SampleRate();
03875                                                 KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03876                                                 reg_ah=0;
03877                                         }
03878                                         else if ((reg_bh==0x01) || (reg_bh==0x02)) { /* set scaling */
03879                                                 KEYBOARD_AUX_Write(0xE6+reg_bh-1); /* 0xE6 1:1   or 0xE7 2:1 */
03880                                                 KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
03881                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false); 
03882                                                 reg_ah=0;
03883                                         } else {
03884                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03885                                                 reg_ah=1;
03886                                         }
03887                                         break;
03888                                 case 0x07:              // set callback
03889                                         Mouse_ChangePS2Callback(SegValue(es),reg_bx);
03890                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03891                                         reg_ah=0;
03892                                         break;
03893                                 default:
03894                                         LOG_MSG("INT 15h unknown mouse call AX=%04x\n",reg_ax);
03895                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03896                                         reg_ah=1;
03897                                         break;
03898                         }
03899                 }
03900                 else {
03901                         reg_ah=0x86;
03902                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03903                         if ((IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) || (machine==MCH_CGA)) {
03904                                 /* relict from comparisons, as int15 exits with a retf2 instead of an iret */
03905                                 CALLBACK_SZF(false);
03906                         }
03907                 }
03908                 break;
03909         case 0xc3:      /* set carry flag so BorlandRTM doesn't assume a VECTRA/PS2 */
03910                 reg_ah=0x86;
03911                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03912                 break;
03913         case 0xc4:      /* BIOS POS Programm option Select */
03914                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_NORMAL)("INT15:Function %X called, bios mouse not supported",reg_ah);
03915                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
03916                 break;
03917         case 0x53: // APM BIOS
03918                 if (APMBIOS) {
03919                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_DEBUG)("APM BIOS call AX=%04x BX=0x%04x CX=0x%04x\n",reg_ax,reg_bx,reg_cx);
03920                         switch(reg_al) {
03921                                 case 0x00: // installation check
03922                                         reg_ah = 1;                             // major
03923                                         reg_al = APM_BIOS_minor_version;        // minor
03924                                         reg_bx = 0x504d;                        // 'PM'
03925                                         reg_cx = (APMBIOS_allow_prot16?0x01:0x00) + (APMBIOS_allow_prot32?0x02:0x00);
03926                                         // 32-bit interface seems to be needed for standby in win95
03927                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03928                                         break;
03929                                 case 0x01: // connect real mode interface
03930                                         if(!APMBIOS_allow_realmode) {
03931                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attemped real-mode connection, which is disabled in your dosbox.conf\n");
03932                                                 reg_ah = 0x86;  // APM not present
03933                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03934                                                 break;
03935                                         }
03936                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0) {
03937                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
03938                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03939                                                 break;
03940                                         }
03941                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) { // not yet connected
03942                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: Connected to real-mode interface\n");
03943                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03944                                                 APMBIOS_connect_mode = APMBIOS_CONNECT_REAL;
03945                                                 apm_realmode_connected=true;
03946                                         } else {
03947                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attempted to connect to real-mode interface when already connected\n");
03948                                                 reg_ah = APMBIOS_connected_already_err(); // interface connection already in effect
03949                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03950                                         }
03951                                         APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version = 0;
03952                                         break;
03953                                 case 0x02: // connect 16-bit protected mode interface
03954                                         if(!APMBIOS_allow_prot16) {
03955                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attemped 16-bit protected mode connection, which is disabled in your dosbox.conf\n");
03956                                                 reg_ah = 0x06;  // not supported
03957                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03958                                                 break;
03959                                         }
03960                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0) {
03961                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
03962                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03963                                                 break;
03964                                         }
03965                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) { // not yet connected
03966                                                 /* NTS: We use the same callback address for both 16-bit and 32-bit
03967                                                  *      because only the DOS callback and RETF instructions are involved,
03968                                                  *      which can be executed as either 16-bit or 32-bit code without problems. */
03969                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: Connected to 16-bit protected mode interface\n");
03970                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
03971                                                 reg_ax = INT15_apm_pmentry >> 16;       // AX = 16-bit code segment (real mode base)
03972                                                 reg_bx = INT15_apm_pmentry & 0xFFFF;    // BX = offset of entry point
03973                                                 reg_cx = INT15_apm_pmentry >> 16;       // CX = 16-bit data segment (NTS: doesn't really matter)
03974                                                 reg_si = 0xFFFF;                        // SI = code segment length
03975                                                 reg_di = 0xFFFF;                        // DI = data segment length
03976                                                 APMBIOS_connect_mode = APMBIOS_CONNECT_PROT16;
03977                                                 apm_realmode_connected=true;
03978                                         } else {
03979                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attempted to connect to 16-bit protected mode interface when already connected\n");
03980                                                 reg_ah = APMBIOS_connected_already_err(); // interface connection already in effect
03981                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03982                                         }
03983                                         APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version = 0;
03984                                         break;
03985                                 case 0x03: // connect 32-bit protected mode interface
03986                                         // Note that Windows 98 will NOT talk to the APM BIOS unless the 32-bit protected mode connection is available.
03987                                         // And if you lie about it in function 0x00 and then fail, Windows 98 will fail with a "Windows protection error".
03988                                         if(!APMBIOS_allow_prot32) {
03989                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attemped 32-bit protected mode connection, which is disabled in your dosbox.conf\n");
03990                                                 reg_ah = 0x08;  // not supported
03991                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03992                                                 break;
03993                                         }
03994                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0) {
03995                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
03996                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
03997                                                 break;
03998                                         }
03999                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) { // not yet connected
04000                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: Connected to 32-bit protected mode interface\n");
04001                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04002                                                 /* NTS: We use the same callback address for both 16-bit and 32-bit
04003                                                  *      because only the DOS callback and RETF instructions are involved,
04004                                                  *      which can be executed as either 16-bit or 32-bit code without problems. */
04005                                                 reg_ax = INT15_apm_pmentry >> 16;       // AX = 32-bit code segment (real mode base)
04006                                                 reg_ebx = INT15_apm_pmentry & 0xFFFF;   // EBX = offset of entry point
04007                                                 reg_cx = INT15_apm_pmentry >> 16;       // CX = 16-bit code segment (real mode base)
04008                                                 reg_dx = INT15_apm_pmentry >> 16;       // DX = data segment (real mode base) (?? what size?)
04009                                                 reg_esi = 0xFFFFFFFF;                   // ESI = upper word: 16-bit code segment len  lower word: 32-bit code segment length
04010                                                 reg_di = 0xFFFF;                        // DI = data segment length
04011                                                 APMBIOS_connect_mode = APMBIOS_CONNECT_PROT32;
04012                                                 apm_realmode_connected=true;
04013                                         } else {
04014                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS attempted to connect to 32-bit protected mode interface when already connected\n");
04015                                                 reg_ah = APMBIOS_connected_already_err(); // interface connection already in effect
04016                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04017                                         }
04018                                         APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version = 0;
04019                                         break;
04020                                 case 0x04: // DISCONNECT INTERFACE
04021                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0) {
04022                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04023                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04024                                                 break;
04025                                         }
04026                                         if(apm_realmode_connected) {
04027                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS: OS disconnected\n");
04028                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04029                                                 apm_realmode_connected=false;
04030                                         } else {
04031                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04032                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04033                                         }
04034                                         APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version = 0;
04035                                         break;
04036                                 case 0x05: // CPU IDLE
04037                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04038                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04039                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04040                                                 break;
04041                                         }
04042 
04043                                         // Trigger CPU HLT instruction.
04044                                         // NTS: For whatever weird reason, NOT emulating HLT makes Windows 95
04045                                         //      crashy when the APM driver is active! There's something within
04046                                         //      the Win95 kernel that apparently screws up really badly if
04047                                         //      the APM IDLE call returns immediately. The best case scenario
04048                                         //      seems to be that Win95's APM driver has some sort of timing
04049                                         //      logic to it that if it detects an immediate return, immediately
04050                                         //      shuts down and powers off the machine. Windows 98 also seems
04051                                         //      to require a HLT, and will act erratically without it.
04052                                         //
04053                                         //      Also need to note that the choice of "HLT" is not arbitrary
04054                                         //      at all. The APM BIOS standard mentions CPU IDLE either stopping
04055                                         //      the CPU clock temporarily or issuing HLT as a valid method.
04056                                         //
04057                                         // TODO: Make this a dosbox.conf configuration option: what do we do
04058                                         //       on APM idle calls? Allow selection between "nothing" "hlt"
04059                                         //       and "software delay".
04060                                         if (!(reg_flags&0x200)) {
04061                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS warning: CPU IDLE called with IF=0, not HLTing\n");
04062                                         }
04063                                         else if (cpudecoder == &HLT_Decode) { /* do not re-execute HLT, it makes DOSBox hang */
04064                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS warning: CPU IDLE HLT within HLT (DOSBox core failure)\n");
04065                                         }
04066                                         else {
04067                                                 CPU_HLT(reg_eip);
04068                                         }
04069                                         break;
04070                                 case 0x06: // CPU BUSY
04071                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04072                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04073                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04074                                                 break;
04075                                         }
04076 
04077                                         /* OK. whatever. system no longer idle */
04078                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04079                                         break;
04080                                 case 0x07:
04081                                         if(reg_bx != 0x1) {
04082                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // wrong device ID
04083                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04084                                                 break;
04085                                         }
04086                                         if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04087                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04088                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04089                                                 break;
04090                                         }
04091                                         switch(reg_cx) {
04092                                                 case 0x3: // power off
04093                                                         throw(0);
04094                                                         break;
04095                                                 default:
04096                                                         reg_ah = 0x0A; // invalid parameter value in CX
04097                                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04098                                                         break;
04099                                         }
04100                                         break;
04101                                 case 0x08: // ENABLE/DISABLE POWER MANAGEMENT
04102                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0 && reg_bx != 0x1) {
04103                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04104                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04105                                                 break;
04106                                         } else if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04107                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04108                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04109                                                 break;
04110                                         }
04111                                         if(reg_cx==0x0) LOG_MSG("disable APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04112                                         else if(reg_cx==0x1) LOG_MSG("enable APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04113                                         else {
04114                                                 reg_ah = 0x0A; // invalid parameter value in CX
04115                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04116                                         }
04117                                         break;
04118                                 case 0x0a: // GET POWER STATUS
04119                                         if (!apm_realmode_connected) {
04120                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04121                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04122                                                 break;
04123                                         }
04124                                         if (reg_bx != 0x0001 && reg_bx != 0x8001) {
04125                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04126                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04127                                                 break;
04128                                         }
04129                                         /* FIXME: Allow configuration and shell commands to dictate whether or
04130                                          *        not we emulate a laptop with a battery */
04131                                         reg_bh = 0x01;          // AC line status (1=on-line)
04132                                         reg_bl = 0xFF;          // Battery status (unknown)
04133                                         reg_ch = 0x80;          // Battery flag (no system battery)
04134                                         reg_cl = 0xFF;          // Remaining battery charge (unknown)
04135                                         reg_dx = 0xFFFF;        // Remaining battery life (unknown)
04136                                         reg_si = 0;             // Number of battery units (if called with reg_bx == 0x8001)
04137                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04138                                         break;
04139                                 case 0x0b: // GET PM EVENT
04140                                         if (!apm_realmode_connected) {
04141                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04142                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04143                                                 break;
04144                                         }
04145                                         reg_ah = 0x80; // no power management events pending
04146                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04147                                         break;
04148                                 case 0x0d:
04149                                         // NTS: NOT implementing this call can cause Windows 98's APM driver to crash on startup
04150                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0 && reg_bx != 0x1) {
04151                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04152                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04153                                                 break;
04154                                         } else if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04155                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04156                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04157                                                 break;
04158                                         }
04159                                         if(reg_cx==0x0) {
04160                                                 LOG_MSG("disable APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04161                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04162                                         }
04163                                         else if(reg_cx==0x1) {
04164                                                 LOG_MSG("enable APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04165                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04166                                         }
04167                                         else {
04168                                                 reg_ah = 0x0A; // invalid parameter value in CX
04169                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04170                                         }
04171                                         break;
04172                                 case 0x0e:
04173                                         if (APM_BIOS_minor_version != 0) { // APM 1.1 or higher only
04174                                                 if(reg_bx != 0x0) {
04175                                                         reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04176                                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04177                                                         break;
04178                                                 } else if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04179                                                         reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04180                                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04181                                                         break;
04182                                                 }
04183                                                 reg_ah = reg_ch; /* we are called with desired version in CH,CL, return actual version in AH,AL */
04184                                                 reg_al = reg_cl;
04185                                                 if(reg_ah != 1) reg_ah = 1;                                             // major
04186                                                 if(reg_al > APM_BIOS_minor_version) reg_al = APM_BIOS_minor_version;    // minor
04187                                                 APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version = reg_al;                              // what we decided becomes the interface we emulate
04188                                                 LOG_MSG("APM BIOS negotiated to v1.%u",APM_BIOS_connected_minor_version);
04189                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04190                                         }
04191                                         else { // APM 1.0 does not recognize this call
04192                                                 reg_ah = 0x0C; // function not supported
04193                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04194                                         }
04195                                         break;
04196                                 case 0x0f:
04197                                         if(reg_bx != 0x0 && reg_bx != 0x1) {
04198                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04199                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);                     
04200                                                 break;
04201                                         } else if(!apm_realmode_connected) {
04202                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;
04203                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04204                                                 break;
04205                                         }
04206                                         if(reg_cx==0x0) {
04207                                                 LOG_MSG("disengage APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04208                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04209                                         }
04210                                         else if(reg_cx==0x1) {
04211                                                 LOG_MSG("engage APM for device %4x",reg_bx);
04212                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04213                                         }
04214                                         else {
04215                                                 reg_ah = 0x0A; // invalid parameter value in CX
04216                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04217                                         }
04218                                         break;
04219                                 case 0x10:
04220                                         if (!apm_realmode_connected) {
04221                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04222                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04223                                                 break;
04224                                         }
04225                                         if (reg_bx != 0) {
04226                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04227                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04228                                                 break;
04229                                         }
04230                                         reg_ah = 0;
04231                                         reg_bl = 0; // number of battery units
04232                                         reg_cx = 0x03; // can enter suspend/standby and will post standby/resume events
04233                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04234                                         break;
04235                                 case 0x13://enable/disable/query timer based requests
04236                                         // NTS: NOT implementing this call can cause Windows 98's APM driver to crash on startup
04237                                         if (!apm_realmode_connected) {
04238                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04239                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04240                                                 break;
04241                                         }
04242                                         if (reg_bx != 0) {
04243                                                 reg_ah = 0x09;  // unrecognized device ID
04244                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04245                                                 break;
04246                                         }
04247 
04248                                         if (reg_cx == 0) { // disable
04249                                                 APM_inactivity_timer = false;
04250                                                 reg_cx = 0;
04251                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04252                                         }
04253                                         else if (reg_cx == 1) { // enable
04254                                                 APM_inactivity_timer = true;
04255                                                 reg_cx = 1;
04256                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04257                                         }
04258                                         else if (reg_cx == 2) { // get enabled status
04259                                                 reg_cx = APM_inactivity_timer ? 1 : 0;
04260                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04261                                         }
04262                                         else {
04263                                                 reg_ah = 0x0A; // invalid parameter value in CX
04264                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04265                                         }
04266                                         break;
04267                                 default:
04268                                         LOG_MSG("Unknown APM BIOS call AX=%04x\n",reg_ax);
04269                                         if (!apm_realmode_connected) {
04270                                                 reg_ah = 0x03;  // interface not connected
04271                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04272                                                 break;
04273                                         }
04274                                         reg_ah = 0x0C; // function not supported
04275                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04276                                         break;
04277                         }
04278                 }
04279                 else {
04280                         reg_ah=0x86;
04281                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04282                         LOG_MSG("APM BIOS call attempted. set apmbios=1 if you want power management\n");
04283                         if ((IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) || (machine==MCH_CGA) || (machine==MCH_AMSTRAD)) {
04284                                 /* relict from comparisons, as int15 exits with a retf2 instead of an iret */
04285                                 CALLBACK_SZF(false);
04286                         }
04287                 }
04288                 break;
04289         case 0xe8:
04290                 switch (reg_al) {
04291                         case 0x01: { /* E801: memory size */
04292                                         Bitu sz = MEM_TotalPages()*4;
04293                                         if (sz >= 1024) sz -= 1024;
04294                                         else sz = 0;
04295                                         reg_ax = reg_cx = (sz > 0x3C00) ? 0x3C00 : sz; /* extended memory between 1MB and 16MB in KBs */
04296                                         sz -= reg_ax;
04297                                         sz /= 64;       /* extended memory size from 16MB in 64KB blocks */
04298                                         if (sz > 65535) sz = 65535;
04299                                         reg_bx = reg_dx = sz;
04300                                         CALLBACK_SCF(false);
04301                                 }
04302                                 break;
04303                         case 0x20: { /* E820: MEMORY LISTING */
04304                                         if (reg_edx == 0x534D4150 && reg_ecx >= 20 && (MEM_TotalPages()*4) >= 24000) {
04305                                                 /* return a minimalist list:
04306                                                  *
04307                                                  *    0) 0x000000-0x09EFFF       Free memory
04308                                                  *    1) 0x0C0000-0x0FFFFF       Reserved
04309                                                  *    2) 0x100000-...            Free memory (no ACPI tables) */
04310                                                 if (reg_ebx < 3) {
04311                                                         uint32_t base,len,type;
04312                                                         Bitu seg = SegValue(es);
04313 
04314                                                         assert((MEM_TotalPages()*4096) >= 0x100000);
04315 
04316                                                         switch (reg_ebx) {
04317                                                                 case 0: base=0x000000; len=0x09F000; type=1; break;
04318                                                                 case 1: base=0x0C0000; len=0x040000; type=2; break;
04319                                                                 case 2: base=0x100000; len=(MEM_TotalPages()*4096)-0x100000; type=1; break;
04320                                                                 default: E_Exit("Despite checks EBX is wrong value"); /* BUG! */
04321                                                         };
04322 
04323                                                         /* write to ES:DI */
04324                                                         real_writed(seg,reg_di+0x00,base);
04325                                                         real_writed(seg,reg_di+0x04,0);
04326                                                         real_writed(seg,reg_di+0x08,len);
04327                                                         real_writed(seg,reg_di+0x0C,0);
04328                                                         real_writed(seg,reg_di+0x10,type);
04329                                                         reg_ecx = 20;
04330 
04331                                                         /* return EBX pointing to next entry. wrap around, as most BIOSes do.
04332                                                          * the program is supposed to stop on CF=1 or when we return EBX == 0 */
04333                                                         if (++reg_ebx >= 3) reg_ebx = 0;
04334                                                 }
04335                                                 else {
04336                                                         CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04337                                                 }
04338 
04339                                                 reg_eax = 0x534D4150;
04340                                         }
04341                                         else {
04342                                                 reg_eax = 0x8600;
04343                                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04344                                         }
04345                                 }
04346                                 break;
04347                         default:
04348                                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT15:Unknown call ah=E8, al=%2X",reg_al);
04349                                 reg_ah=0x86;
04350                                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04351                                 if ((IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) || (machine==MCH_CGA) || (machine==MCH_AMSTRAD)) {
04352                                         /* relict from comparisons, as int15 exits with a retf2 instead of an iret */
04353                                         CALLBACK_SZF(false);
04354                                 }
04355                 }
04356                 break;
04357         default:
04358                 LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_ERROR)("INT15:Unknown call ax=%4X",reg_ax);
04359                 reg_ah=0x86;
04360                 CALLBACK_SCF(true);
04361                 if ((IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) || (machine==MCH_CGA) || (machine==MCH_AMSTRAD)) {
04362                         /* relict from comparisons, as int15 exits with a retf2 instead of an iret */
04363                         CALLBACK_SZF(false);
04364                 }
04365         }
04366         return CBRET_NONE;
04367 }
