04410 void BIOS_ZeroExtendedSize(bool in) {
04411         if(in) other_memsystems++; 
04412         else other_memsystems--;
04413         if(other_memsystems < 0) other_memsystems=0;
04414 
04415     if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
04416         Bitu mempages = MEM_TotalPages(); /* in 4KB pages */
04417 
04418         /* What applies to IBM PC/AT (zeroing out the extended memory size)
04419          * also applies to PC-98, when HIMEM.SYS is loaded */
04420         if (in) mempages = 0;
04421 
04422         /* extended memory size (286 systems, below 16MB) */
04423         if (mempages > (1024UL/4UL)) {
04424             unsigned int ext = ((mempages - (1024UL/4UL)) * 4096UL) / (128UL * 1024UL); /* convert to 128KB units */
04425 
04426             /* extended memory, up to 16MB capacity (for 286 systems?)
04427              *
04428              * MS-DOS drivers will "allocate" for themselves by taking from the top of
04429              * extended memory then subtracting from this value.
04430              *
04431              * capacity does not include conventional memory below 1MB, nor any memory
04432              * above 16MB.
04433              *
04434              * PC-98 systems may reserve the top 1MB, limiting the top to 15MB instead.
04435              *
04436              * 0x70 = 128KB * 0x70 = 14MB
04437              * 0x78 = 128KB * 0x70 = 15MB */
04438             if (ext > 0x78) ext = 0x78;
04439 
04440             mem_writeb(0x401,ext);
04441         }
04442         else {
04443             mem_writeb(0x401,0x00);
04444         }
04445 
04446         /* extended memory size (386 systems, at or above 16MB) */
04447         if (mempages > ((1024UL*16UL)/4UL)) {
04448             unsigned int ext = ((mempages - ((1024UL*16UL)/4UL)) * 4096UL) / (1024UL * 1024UL); /* convert to MB */
04449 
04450             /* extended memory, at or above 16MB capacity (for 386+ systems?)
04451              *
04452              * MS-DOS drivers will "allocate" for themselves by taking from the top of
04453              * extended memory then subtracting from this value.
04454              *
04455              * capacity does not include conventional memory below 1MB, nor any memory
04456              * below 16MB. */
04457             if (ext > 0xFFFE) ext = 0xFFFE;
04458 
04459             mem_writew(0x594,ext);
04460         }
04461         else {
04462             mem_writew(0x594,0x00);
04463         }
04464     }
04465 }
04466 
04467 unsigned char do_isapnp_chksum(unsigned char *d,int i) {
04468         unsigned char sum = 0;
04469 
04470         while (i-- > 0)
04471                 sum += *d++;
04472 
04473         return (0x100 - sum) & 0xFF;
04474 }
04475 
04476 void MEM_ResetPageHandler_Unmapped(Bitu phys_page, Bitu pages);
04477 
04478 unsigned int dos_conventional_limit = 0;
04479 
04480 bool AdapterROM_Read(Bitu address,unsigned long *size) {
04481         unsigned char chksum=0;
04482         unsigned char c[3];
04483         unsigned int i;
04484 
04485         if ((address & 0x1FF) != 0) {
04486                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("AdapterROM_Read: Caller attempted ROM scan not aligned to 512-byte boundary");
04487                 return false;
04488         }
04489 
04490         for (i=0;i < 3;i++)
04491                 c[i] = mem_readb(address+i);
04492 
04493         if (c[0] == 0x55 && c[1] == 0xAA) {
04494                 *size = (unsigned long)c[2] * 512UL;
04495                 for (i=0;i < (unsigned int)(*size);i++) chksum += mem_readb(address+i);
04496                 if (chksum != 0) {
04497                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_WARN)("AdapterROM_Read: Found ROM at 0x%lx but checksum failed\n",(unsigned long)address);
04498                         return false;
04499                 }
04500 
04501                 return true;
04502         }
04503 
04504         return false;
04505 }

04507 #include "src/gui/dosbox.vga16.bmp.h"
04508 #include "src/gui/dosbox.cga640.bmp.h"
04509 
04510 void DrawDOSBoxLogoCGA6(unsigned int x,unsigned int y) {
04511         unsigned char *s = dosbox_cga640_bmp;
04512         unsigned char *sf = s + sizeof(dosbox_cga640_bmp);
04513         uint32_t width,height;
04514         unsigned int dx,dy;
04515         uint32_t vram;
04516         uint32_t off;
04517         uint32_t sz;
04518 
04519         if (memcmp(s,"BM",2)) return;
04520         sz = host_readd(s+2); // size of total bitmap
04521         off = host_readd(s+10); // offset of bitmap
04522         if ((s+sz) > sf) return;
04523         if ((s+14+40) > sf) return;
04524 
04525         sz = host_readd(s+34); // biSize
04526         if ((s+off+sz) > sf) return;
04527         if (host_readw(s+26) != 1) return; // biBitPlanes
04528         if (host_readw(s+28) != 1)  return; // biBitCount
04529 
04530         width = host_readd(s+18);
04531         height = host_readd(s+22);
04532         if (width > (640-x) || height > (200-y)) return;
04533 
04534         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Drawing CGA logo (%u x %u)",(int)width,(int)height);
04535         for (dy=0;dy < height;dy++) {
04536                 vram  = ((y+dy) >> 1) * 80;
04537                 vram += ((y+dy) & 1) * 0x2000;
04538                 vram += (x / 8);
04539                 s = dosbox_cga640_bmp + off + ((height-(dy+1))*((width+7)/8));
04540                 for (dx=0;dx < width;dx += 8) {
04541                         mem_writeb(0xB8000+vram,*s);
04542                         vram++;
04543                         s++;
04544                 }
04545         }
04546 }
04547 
04548 /* HACK: Re-use the VGA logo */
04549 void DrawDOSBoxLogoPC98(unsigned int x,unsigned int y) {
04550         unsigned char *s = dosbox_vga16_bmp;
04551         unsigned char *sf = s + sizeof(dosbox_vga16_bmp);
04552         unsigned int bit,dx,dy;
04553         uint32_t width,height;
04554     unsigned char p[4];
04555     unsigned char c;
04556         uint32_t vram;
04557         uint32_t off;
04558         uint32_t sz;
04559 
04560         if (memcmp(s,"BM",2)) return;
04561         sz = host_readd(s+2); // size of total bitmap
04562         off = host_readd(s+10); // offset of bitmap
04563         if ((s+sz) > sf) return;
04564         if ((s+14+40) > sf) return;
04565 
04566         sz = host_readd(s+34); // biSize
04567         if ((s+off+sz) > sf) return;
04568         if (host_readw(s+26) != 1) return; // biBitPlanes
04569         if (host_readw(s+28) != 4)  return; // biBitCount
04570 
04571         width = host_readd(s+18);
04572         height = host_readd(s+22);
04573         if (width > (640-x) || height > (350-y)) return;
04574 
04575         // EGA/VGA Write Mode 2
04576         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Drawing VGA logo as PC-98 (%u x %u)",(int)width,(int)height);
04577     for (dy=0;dy < height;dy++) {
04578         vram = ((y+dy) * 80) + (x / 8);
04579         s = dosbox_vga16_bmp + off + ((height-(dy+1))*((width+1)/2));
04580         for (dx=0;dx < width;dx += 8) {
04581             p[0] = p[1] = p[2] = p[3] = 0;
04582             for (bit=0;bit < 8;) {
04583                 c = (*s >> 4);
04584                 p[0] |= ((c >> 0) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04585                 p[1] |= ((c >> 1) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04586                 p[2] |= ((c >> 2) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04587                 p[3] |= ((c >> 3) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04588                 bit++;
04589 
04590                 c = (*s++) & 0xF;
04591                 p[0] |= ((c >> 0) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04592                 p[1] |= ((c >> 1) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04593                 p[2] |= ((c >> 2) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04594                 p[3] |= ((c >> 3) & 1) << (7 - bit);
04595                 bit++;
04596             }
04597 
04598             mem_writeb(0xA8000+vram,p[0]);
04599             mem_writeb(0xB0000+vram,p[1]);
04600             mem_writeb(0xB8000+vram,p[2]);
04601             mem_writeb(0xE0000+vram,p[3]);
04602             vram++;
04603         }
04604     }
04605 }
04606 
04607 void DrawDOSBoxLogoVGA(unsigned int x,unsigned int y) {
04608         unsigned char *s = dosbox_vga16_bmp;
04609         unsigned char *sf = s + sizeof(dosbox_vga16_bmp);
04610         unsigned int bit,dx,dy;
04611         uint32_t width,height;
04612         uint32_t vram;
04613         uint32_t off;
04614         uint32_t sz;
04615 
04616         if (memcmp(s,"BM",2)) return;
04617         sz = host_readd(s+2); // size of total bitmap
04618         off = host_readd(s+10); // offset of bitmap
04619         if ((s+sz) > sf) return;
04620         if ((s+14+40) > sf) return;
04621 
04622         sz = host_readd(s+34); // biSize
04623         if ((s+off+sz) > sf) return;
04624         if (host_readw(s+26) != 1) return; // biBitPlanes
04625         if (host_readw(s+28) != 4)  return; // biBitCount
04626 
04627         width = host_readd(s+18);
04628         height = host_readd(s+22);
04629         if (width > (640-x) || height > (350-y)) return;
04630 
04631         // EGA/VGA Write Mode 2
04632         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Drawing VGA logo (%u x %u)",(int)width,(int)height);
04633         IO_Write(0x3CE,0x05); // graphics mode
04634         IO_Write(0x3CF,0x02); // read=0 write=2 odd/even=0 shift=0 shift256=0
04635         IO_Write(0x3CE,0x03); // data rotate
04636         IO_Write(0x3CE,0x00); // no rotate, no XOP
04637         for (bit=0;bit < 8;bit++) {
04638                 const unsigned char shf = ((bit & 1) ^ 1) * 4;
04639 
04640                 IO_Write(0x3CE,0x08); // bit mask
04641                 IO_Write(0x3CF,0x80 >> bit);
04642 
04643                 for (dy=0;dy < height;dy++) {
04644                         vram = ((y+dy) * 80) + (x / 8);
04645                         s = dosbox_vga16_bmp + off + (bit/2) + ((height-(dy+1))*((width+1)/2));
04646                         for (dx=bit;dx < width;dx += 8) {
04647                                 mem_readb(0xA0000+vram); // load VGA latches
04648                                 mem_writeb(0xA0000+vram,(*s >> shf) & 0xF);
04649                                 vram++;
04650                                 s += 4;
04651                         }
04652                 }
04653         }
04654         // restore write mode 0
04655         IO_Write(0x3CE,0x05); // graphics mode
04656         IO_Write(0x3CF,0x00); // read=0 write=0 odd/even=0 shift=0 shift256=0
04657         IO_Write(0x3CE,0x08); // bit mask
04658         IO_Write(0x3CF,0xFF);
04659 }
04660 
04661 static int bios_pc98_posx = 0;
04662 
04663 static void BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(const int x,int &y,const char *msg) {
04664         const char *s = msg;
04665 
04666     if (machine != MCH_PC98) {
04667         while (*s != 0) {
04668             if (*s == '\n') {
04669                 y++;
04670                 reg_eax = 0x0200;       // set cursor pos
04671                 reg_ebx = 0;            // page zero
04672                 reg_dh = y;             // row 4
04673                 reg_dl = x;             // column 20
04674                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
04675                 s++;
04676             }
04677             else {
04678                 reg_eax = 0x0E00 | ((unsigned char)(*s++));
04679                 reg_ebx = 0x07;
04680                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
04681             }
04682         }
04683     }
04684     else {
04685         unsigned int bo;
04686 
04687         while (*s != 0) {
04688             if (*s == '\n') {
04689                 y++;
04690                 s++;
04691                 bios_pc98_posx = x;
04692 
04693                 bo = ((y * 80) + bios_pc98_posx) * 2;
04694             }
04695             else if (*s == '\r') {
04696                 s++; /* ignore */
04697             }
04698             else {
04699                 bo = ((y * 80) + (bios_pc98_posx++)) * 2; /* NTS: note the post increment */
04700 
04701                 mem_writew(0xA0000+bo,*s++);
04702                 mem_writeb(0xA2000+bo,0xE1);
04703             }
04704 
04705             reg_eax = 0x1300;   // set cursor pos (PC-98)
04706             reg_edx = bo;       // byte position
04707                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
04708         }
04709     }
04710 }

04746 void write_FFFF_PC98_signature() {
04747     /* this may overwrite the existing signature.
04748      * PC-98 systems DO NOT have an ASCII date at F000:FFF5
04749      * and the WORD value at F000:FFFE is said to be a checksum of the BIOS */
04750 
04751     // The farjump at the processor reset entry point (jumps to POST routine)
04752     phys_writeb(0xffff0,0xEA);                                  // FARJMP
04753     phys_writew(0xffff1,RealOff(BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION));  // offset
04754     phys_writew(0xffff3,RealSeg(BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION));  // segment
04755 
04756     // write nothing (not used)
04757     for(Bitu i = 0; i < 9; i++) phys_writeb(0xffff5+i,0);
04758 
04759     // fake BIOS checksum
04760     phys_writew(0xffffe,0xABCD);
04761 }
04762 
04763 extern bool                         gdc_5mhz_mode;
04764 extern bool                         enable_pc98_egc;
04765 extern bool                         enable_pc98_grcg;
04766 extern bool                         enable_pc98_16color;
04767 
04768 void gdc_egc_enable_update_vars(void) {
04769     unsigned char b;
04770 
04771     b = mem_readb(0x54D);
04772     b &= ~0x40;
04773     if (enable_pc98_egc) b |= 0x40;
04774     mem_writeb(0x54D,b);
04775 
04776     b = mem_readb(0x597);
04777     b &= ~0x04;
04778     if (enable_pc98_egc) b |= 0x04;
04779     mem_writeb(0x597,b);
04780 
04781     if (!enable_pc98_egc)
04782         pc98_gdc_vramop &= ~(1 << VOPBIT_EGC);
04783 }
04784 
04785 void gdc_grcg_enable_update_vars(void) {
04786     unsigned char b;
04787 
04788     b = mem_readb(0x54C);
04789     b &= ~0x02;
04790     if (enable_pc98_grcg) b |= 0x02;
04791     mem_writeb(0x54C,b);
04792         
04793         //TODO: How to reset GRCG?
04794 }
04795 
04796 
04797 void gdc_16color_enable_update_vars(void) {
04798     unsigned char b;
04799 
04800     b = mem_readb(0x54C);
04801     b &= ~0x04;
04802     if (enable_pc98_16color) b |= 0x04;
04803     mem_writeb(0x54C,b);
04804         
04805         if(!enable_pc98_16color) {//force switch to 8-colors mode
04806                 void pc98_port6A_command_write(unsigned char b);
04807                 pc98_port6A_command_write(0x00);
04808         }
04809 }
04810 
04811 class BIOS:public Module_base{
04812 private:
04813         static Bitu cb_bios_post__func(void) {
04814                 void TIMER_BIOS_INIT_Configure();
04815 #if C_DEBUG
04816         void DEBUG_CheckCSIP();
04817 #endif
04818 
04819 #if C_HEAVY_DEBUG
04820         /* the game/app obviously crashed, which is way more important
04821          * to log than what we do here in the BIOS at POST */
04822         void DEBUG_StopLog(void);
04823         DEBUG_StopLog();
04824 #endif
04825 
04826                 if (bios_first_init) {
04827                         /* clear the first 1KB-32KB */
04828                         for (Bit16u i=0x400;i<0x8000;i++) real_writeb(0x0,i,0);
04829                 }
04830 
04831         if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
04832             for (unsigned int i=0;i < 20;i++) callback[i].Uninstall();
04833 
04834             /* clear out 0x50 segment (TODO: 0x40 too?) */
04835             for (unsigned int i=0;i < 0x100;i++) phys_writeb(0x500+i,0);
04836 
04837             write_FFFF_PC98_signature();
04838             BIOS_ZeroExtendedSize(false);
04839 
04840             unsigned char memsize_real_code = 0;
04841             Bitu mempages = MEM_TotalPages(); /* in 4KB pages */
04842 
04843             /* NTS: Fill in the 3-bit code in FLAGS1 that represents
04844              *      how much lower conventional memory is in the system.
04845              *
04846              *      Note that MEM.EXE requires this value, or else it
04847              *      will complain about broken UMB linkage and fail
04848              *      to show anything else. */
04849             /* TODO: In the event we eventually support "high resolution mode"
04850              *       we can indicate 768KB here, code == 5, meaning that
04851              *       the RAM extends up to 0xBFFFF instead of 0x9FFFF */
04852             if (mempages >= (640UL/4UL))        /* 640KB */
04853                 memsize_real_code = 4;
04854             else if (mempages >= (512UL/4UL))   /* 512KB */
04855                 memsize_real_code = 3;
04856             else if (mempages >= (384UL/4UL))   /* 384KB */
04857                 memsize_real_code = 2;
04858             else if (mempages >= (256UL/4UL))   /* 256KB */
04859                 memsize_real_code = 1;
04860             else                                /* 128KB */
04861                 memsize_real_code = 0;
04862 
04863             /* BIOS flags */
04864             /* bit[7:7] = Startup            1=hot start    0=cold start
04865              * bit[6:6] = BASIC type         ??
04866              * bit[5:5] = Keyboard beep      1=don't beep   0=beep          ... when buffer full
04867              * bit[4:4] = Expansion conv RAM 1=present      0=absent
04868              * bit[3:3] = ??
04869              * bit[2:2] = ??
04870              * bit[1:1] = HD mode            1=1MB mode     0=640KB mode    ... of the floppy drive
04871              * bit[0:0] = Model              1=other        0=PC-9801 original */
04872             /* NTS: MS-DOS 5.0 appears to reduce it's BIOS calls and render the whole
04873              *      console as green IF bit 0 is clear.
04874              *
04875              *      If bit 0 is set, INT 1Ah will be hooked by MS-DOS and, for some odd reason,
04876              *      MS-DOS's hook proc will call to our INT 1Ah + 0x19 bytes. */
04877             mem_writeb(0x500,0x01 | 0x02/*high density drive*/);
04878 
04879             /* BIOS flags */
04880             /* timer setup will set/clear bit 7 */
04881             /* bit[7:7] = system clock freq  1=8MHz         0=5/10Mhz
04882              *          = timer clock freq   1=1.9968MHz    0=2.4576MHz
04883              * bit[6:6] = CPU                1=V30          0=Intel (8086 through Pentium)
04884              * bit[5:5] = Model info         1=Other model  0=PC-9801 Muji, PC-98XA
04885              * bit[4:4] = Model info         ...
04886              * bit[3:3] = Model info         1=High res     0=normal
04887              * bit[2:0] = Realmode memsize
04888              *                             000=128KB      001=256KB
04889              *                             010=384KB      011=512KB
04890              *                             100=640KB      101=768KB
04891              *
04892              * Ref: http://hackipedia.org/browse/Computer/Platform/PC,%20NEC%20PC-98/Collections/Undocumented%209801,%209821%20Volume%202%20(webtech.co.jp)/memsys.txt */
04893             mem_writeb(0x501,0x20 | memsize_real_code);
04894 
04895             /* set up some default state */
04896             mem_writeb(0x54C/*MEMB_PRXCRT*/,0x4F); /* default graphics layer off, 24KHz hsync */
04897 
04898             /* keyboard buffer */
04899             mem_writew(0x524/*tail*/,0x502);
04900             mem_writew(0x526/*tail*/,0x502);
04901 
04902             /* various BIOS flags */
04903             mem_writeb(0x53B,0x0F); // CRT_RASTER, 640x400 24.83KHz-hsync 56.42Hz-vsync
04904             mem_writeb(0x54C,(enable_pc98_grcg ? 0x02 : 0x00) | (enable_pc98_16color ? 0x04 : 0x00)); // PRXCRT, 16-color G-VRAM, GRCG
04905             mem_writeb(0x54D,(enable_pc98_egc ? 0x40 : 0x00) | (gdc_5mhz_mode ? 0x20 : 0x00) | (gdc_5mhz_mode ? 0x04 : 0x00)); // EGC
04906             mem_writeb(0x597,(enable_pc98_egc ? 0x04 : 0x00/*FIXME*/)); // EGC
04907         }
04908 
04909         if (bios_user_reset_vector_blob != 0 && !bios_user_reset_vector_blob_run) {
04910             LOG_MSG("BIOS POST: Running user reset vector blob at 0x%lx",(unsigned long)bios_user_reset_vector_blob);
04911             bios_user_reset_vector_blob_run = true;
04912 
04913             assert((bios_user_reset_vector_blob&0xF) == 0); /* must be page aligned */
04914 
04915             SegSet16(cs,bios_user_reset_vector_blob>>4);
04916             reg_eip = 0;
04917 
04918 #if C_DEBUG
04919             /* help the debugger reflect the new instruction pointer */
04920             DEBUG_CheckCSIP();
04921 #endif
04922 
04923             return CBRET_NONE;
04924         }
04925 
04926                 if (cpu.pmode) E_Exit("BIOS error: POST function called while in protected/vm86 mode");
04927 
04928         CPU_CLI();
04929 
04930                 /* we need A20 enabled for BIOS boot-up */
04931                 void A20Gate_OverrideOn(Section *sec);
04932                 void MEM_A20_Enable(bool enabled);
04933                 A20Gate_OverrideOn(NULL);
04934                 MEM_A20_Enable(true);
04935 
04936         BIOS_OnResetComplete(NULL);
04937 
04938                 adapter_scan_start = 0xC0000;
04939                 bios_has_exec_vga_bios = false;
04940                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("BIOS: executing POST routine");
04941 
04942                 // TODO: Anything we can test in the CPU here?
04943 
04944                 // initialize registers
04945                 SegSet16(ds,0x0000);
04946                 SegSet16(es,0x0000);
04947                 SegSet16(fs,0x0000);
04948                 SegSet16(gs,0x0000);
04949                 SegSet16(ss,0x0000);
04950 
04951                 {
04952                         Bitu sz = MEM_TotalPages();
04953 
04954                         /* The standard BIOS is said to put it's stack (at least at OS boot time) 512 bytes past the end of the boot sector
04955                          * meaning that the boot sector loads to 0000:7C00 and the stack is set grow downward from 0000:8000 */
04956 
04957                         if (sz > 8) sz = 8; /* 4KB * 8 = 32KB = 0x8000 */
04958                         sz *= 4096;
04959                         reg_esp = sz - 4;
04960                         reg_ebp = 0;
04961                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("BIOS: POST stack set to 0000:%04x",reg_esp);
04962                 }
04963 
04964         if (dosbox_int_iocallout != IO_Callout_t_none) {
04965             IO_FreeCallout(dosbox_int_iocallout);
04966             dosbox_int_iocallout = IO_Callout_t_none;
04967         }
04968 
04969         if (isapnp_biosstruct_base != 0) {
04970             ROMBIOS_FreeMemory(isapnp_biosstruct_base);
04971             isapnp_biosstruct_base = 0;
04972         }
04973 
04974                 if (BOCHS_PORT_E9) {
04975                         delete BOCHS_PORT_E9;
04976                         BOCHS_PORT_E9=NULL;
04977                 }
04978                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT) {
04979                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT;
04980                         ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT=NULL;
04981                 }
04982                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT) {
04983                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT;
04984                         ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT=NULL;
04985                 }
04986                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT) {
04987                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT;
04988                         ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT=NULL;
04989                 }
04990 
04991                 extern Bitu call_default,call_default2;
04992 
04993         if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
04994             /* INT 40h-FFh generic stub routine */
04995             callback[18].Uninstall();
04996             callback[18].Install(&INTGEN_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int stub ???");
04997             for (unsigned int i=0x40;i < 0x100;i++) RealSetVec(i,callback[18].Get_RealPointer());
04998 
04999             /* need handler at INT 07h */
05000             real_writed(0,0x07*4,BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION);
05001         }
05002         else {
05003             /* Clear the vector table */
05004             for (Bit16u i=0x70*4;i<0x400;i++) real_writeb(0x00,i,0);
05005 
05006             /* Only setup default handler for first part of interrupt table */
05007             for (Bit16u ct=0;ct<0x60;ct++) {
05008                 real_writed(0,ct*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));
05009             }
05010             for (Bit16u ct=0x68;ct<0x70;ct++) {
05011                 real_writed(0,ct*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));
05012             }
05013 
05014             // default handler for IRQ 2-7
05015             for (Bit16u ct=0x0A;ct <= 0x0F;ct++)
05016                 RealSetVec(ct,BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION);
05017         }
05018 
05019         if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05020             CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq07default,NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC1,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION),"bios irq 0-7 default handler");
05021             CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq815default,NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ815_DEF_LOCATION),"bios irq 8-15 default handler");
05022 
05023             BIOS_UnsetupKeyboard();
05024             BIOS_UnsetupDisks();
05025 
05026             /* no such INT 4Bh */
05027             int4b_callback.Uninstall();
05028 
05029             /* remove some IBM-style BIOS interrupts that don't exist on PC-98 */
05030             /* IRQ to INT arrangement
05031              *
05032              * IBM          PC-98           IRQ
05033              * --------------------------------
05034              * 0x08         0x08            0
05035              * 0x09         0x09            1
05036              * 0x0A CASCADE 0x0A            2
05037              * 0x0B         0x0B            3
05038              * 0x0C         0x0C            4
05039              * 0x0D         0x0D            5
05040              * 0x0E         0x0E            6
05041              * 0x0F         0x0F CASCADE    7
05042              * 0x70         0x10            8
05043              * 0x71         0x11            9
05044              * 0x72         0x12            10
05045              * 0x73         0x13            11
05046              * 0x74         0x14            12
05047              * 0x75         0x15            13
05048              * 0x76         0x16            14
05049              * 0x77         0x17            15
05050              *
05051              * As part of the change the IRQ cascade emulation needs to change for PC-98 as well.
05052              * IBM uses IRQ 2 for cascade.
05053              * PC-98 uses IRQ 7 for cascade. */
05054 
05055             void INT10_EnterPC98(Section *sec);
05056             INT10_EnterPC98(NULL); /* INT 10h */
05057 
05058             callback[1].Uninstall(); /* INT 11h */
05059             callback[2].Uninstall(); /* INT 12h */
05060             callback[3].Uninstall(); /* INT 14h */
05061             callback[4].Uninstall(); /* INT 15h */
05062             callback[5].Uninstall(); /* INT 17h */
05063             callback[6].Uninstall(); /* INT 1Ah */
05064             callback[7].Uninstall(); /* INT 1Ch */
05065             callback[10].Uninstall(); /* INT 19h */
05066             callback[11].Uninstall(); /* INT 76h: IDE IRQ 14 */
05067             callback[12].Uninstall(); /* INT 77h: IDE IRQ 15 */
05068             callback[15].Uninstall(); /* INT 18h: Enter BASIC */
05069 
05070             /* IRQ 6 is nothing special */
05071             callback[13].Uninstall(); /* INT 0Eh: IDE IRQ 6 */
05072             callback[13].Install(NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC1,"irq 6");
05073 
05074             /* IRQ 8 is nothing special */
05075             callback[8].Uninstall();
05076             callback[8].Install(NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,"irq 8");
05077 
05078             /* IRQ 9 is nothing special */
05079             callback[9].Uninstall();
05080             callback[9].Install(NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,"irq 9");
05081 
05082             /* INT 18h keyboard and video display functions */
05083             callback[1].Install(&INT18_PC98_Handler,CB_INT16,"Int 18 keyboard and display");
05084             callback[1].Set_RealVec(0x18,/*reinstall*/true);
05085 
05086             /* INT 19h *STUB* */
05087             callback[2].Install(&INT19_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 19 ???");
05088             callback[2].Set_RealVec(0x19,/*reinstall*/true);
05089 
05090             /* INT 1Ah *STUB* */
05091             callback[3].Install(&INT1A_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1A ???");
05092             callback[3].Set_RealVec(0x1A,/*reinstall*/true);
05093 
05094             /* MS-DOS 5.0 FIXUP:
05095              * - For whatever reason, if we set bits in the BIOS data area that
05096              *   indicate we're NOT the original model of the PC-98, MS-DOS will
05097              *   hook our INT 1Ah and then call down to 0x19 bytes into our
05098              *   INT 1Ah procedure. If anyone can explain this, I'd like to hear it. --J.C.
05099              *
05100              * NTS: On real hardware, the BIOS appears to have an INT 1Ah, a bunch of NOPs,
05101              *      then at 0x19 bytes into the procedure, the actual handler. This is what
05102              *      MS-DOS is pointing at.
05103              *
05104              *      But wait, there's more.
05105              *
05106              *      MS-DOS calldown pushes DS and DX onto the stack (after the IRET frame)
05107              *      before JMPing into the BIOS.
05108              *
05109              *      Apparently the function at INT 1Ah + 0x19 is expected to do this:
05110              *
05111              *      <function code>
05112              *      POP     DX
05113              *      POP     DS
05114              *      IRET
05115              *
05116              *      I can only imaging what a headache this might have caused NEC when
05117              *      maintaining the platform and compatibility! */
05118             {
05119                 Bitu addr = callback[3].Get_RealPointer();
05120                 addr = ((addr >> 16) << 4) + (addr & 0xFFFF);
05121 
05122                 /* to make this work, we need to pop the two regs, then JMP to our
05123                  * callback and proceed as normal. */
05124                 phys_writeb(addr + 0x19,0x5A);       // POP DX
05125                 phys_writeb(addr + 0x1A,0x1F);       // POP DS
05126                 phys_writeb(addr + 0x1B,0xEB);       // jmp short ...
05127                 phys_writeb(addr + 0x1C,0x100 - 0x1D);
05128             }
05129 
05130             /* INT 1Bh *STUB* */
05131             callback[4].Install(&INT1B_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1B ???");
05132             callback[4].Set_RealVec(0x1B,/*reinstall*/true);
05133 
05134             /* INT 1Ch *STUB* */
05135             callback[5].Install(&INT1C_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1C ???");
05136             callback[5].Set_RealVec(0x1C,/*reinstall*/true);
05137 
05138             /* INT 1Dh *STUB* */
05139             callback[6].Install(&INT1D_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1D ???");
05140             callback[6].Set_RealVec(0x1D,/*reinstall*/true);
05141 
05142             /* INT 1Eh *STUB* */
05143             callback[7].Install(&INT1E_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1E ???");
05144             callback[7].Set_RealVec(0x1E,/*reinstall*/true);
05145 
05146             /* INT 1Fh *STUB* */
05147             callback[10].Install(&INT1F_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1F ???");
05148             callback[10].Set_RealVec(0x1F,/*reinstall*/true);
05149 
05150             /* INT DCh *STUB* */
05151             callback[16].Install(&INTDC_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int DC ???");
05152             callback[16].Set_RealVec(0xDC,/*reinstall*/true);
05153 
05154             /* INT F2h *STUB* */
05155             callback[17].Install(&INTF2_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int F2 ???");
05156             callback[17].Set_RealVec(0xF2,/*reinstall*/true);
05157 
05158             // default handler for IRQ 2-7
05159             for (Bit16u ct=0x0A;ct <= 0x0F;ct++)
05160                 RealSetVec(ct,BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION);
05161 
05162             // default handler for IRQ 8-15
05163             for (Bit16u ct=0;ct < 8;ct++)
05164                 RealSetVec(ct+(IS_PC98_ARCH ? 0x10 : 0x70),BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ815_DEF_LOCATION);
05165         }
05166 
05167                 // setup a few interrupt handlers that point to bios IRETs by default
05168         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH)
05169             real_writed(0,0x0e*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default2));  //design your own railroad
05170 
05171         if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05172             real_writew(0,0x58A,0xFFFFU); // countdown timer value
05173                 PIC_SetIRQMask(0,true); /* PC-98 keeps the timer off unless INT 1Ch is called to set a timer interval */
05174         }
05175 
05176                 real_writed(0,0x66*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));       //war2d
05177                 real_writed(0,0x67*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));
05178                 real_writed(0,0x68*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));
05179                 real_writed(0,0x5c*4,CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_default));       //Network stuff
05180                 //real_writed(0,0xf*4,0); some games don't like it
05181 
05182                 bios_first_init = false;
05183 
05184                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_BIOS_INIT);
05185 
05186                 TIMER_BIOS_INIT_Configure();
05187 
05188                 void INT10_Startup(Section *sec);
05189                 INT10_Startup(NULL);
05190 
05191         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05192             extern Bit8u BIOS_tandy_D4_flag;
05193             real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,BIOS_tandy_D4_flag);
05194         }
05195 
05196                 /* INT 13 Bios Disk Support */
05197                 BIOS_SetupDisks();
05198 
05199                 /* INT 16 Keyboard handled in another file */
05200                 BIOS_SetupKeyboard();
05201 
05202         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05203             int4b_callback.Set_RealVec(0x4B,/*reinstall*/true);
05204             callback[1].Set_RealVec(0x11,/*reinstall*/true);
05205             callback[2].Set_RealVec(0x12,/*reinstall*/true);
05206             callback[3].Set_RealVec(0x14,/*reinstall*/true);
05207             callback[4].Set_RealVec(0x15,/*reinstall*/true);
05208             callback[5].Set_RealVec(0x17,/*reinstall*/true);
05209             callback[6].Set_RealVec(0x1A,/*reinstall*/true);
05210             callback[7].Set_RealVec(0x1C,/*reinstall*/true);
05211             callback[8].Set_RealVec(0x70,/*reinstall*/true);
05212             callback[9].Set_RealVec(0x71,/*reinstall*/true);
05213             callback[10].Set_RealVec(0x19,/*reinstall*/true);
05214             callback[11].Set_RealVec(0x76,/*reinstall*/true);
05215             callback[12].Set_RealVec(0x77,/*reinstall*/true);
05216             callback[13].Set_RealVec(0x0E,/*reinstall*/true);
05217             callback[15].Set_RealVec(0x18,/*reinstall*/true);
05218         }
05219 
05220         // FIXME: We're using IBM PC memory size storage even in PC-98 mode.
05221         //        This cannot be removed, because the DOS kernel uses this variable even in PC-98 mode.
05222         mem_writew(BIOS_MEMORY_SIZE,t_conv);
05223 
05224                 RealSetVec(0x08,BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ0_LOCATION);
05225                 // pseudocode for CB_IRQ0:
05226                 //      sti
05227                 //      callback INT8_Handler
05228                 //      push ds,ax,dx
05229                 //      int 0x1c
05230                 //      cli
05231                 //      mov al, 0x20
05232                 //      out 0x20, al
05233                 //      pop dx,ax,ds
05234                 //      iret
05235 
05236         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05237             mem_writed(BIOS_TIMER,0);                   //Calculate the correct time
05238             phys_writew(Real2Phys(RealGetVec(0x12))+0x12,0x20); //Hack for Jurresic
05239         }
05240 
05241         phys_writeb(Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION),0xcf);     /* bios default interrupt vector location -> IRET */
05242 
05243         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05244             // tandy DAC setup
05245             bool use_tandyDAC=(real_readb(0x40,0xd4)==0xff);
05246 
05247             tandy_sb.port=0;
05248             tandy_dac.port=0;
05249             if (use_tandyDAC) {
05250                 /* tandy DAC sound requested, see if soundblaster device is available */
05251                 Bitu tandy_dac_type = 0;
05252                 if (Tandy_InitializeSB()) {
05253                     tandy_dac_type = 1;
05254                 } else if (Tandy_InitializeTS()) {
05255                     tandy_dac_type = 2;
05256                 }
05257                 if (tandy_dac_type) {
05258                     real_writew(0x40,0xd0,0x0000);
05259                     real_writew(0x40,0xd2,0x0000);
05260                     real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,0xff);        /* tandy DAC init value */
05261                     real_writed(0x40,0xd6,0x00000000);
05262                     /* install the DAC callback handler */
05263                     tandy_DAC_callback[0]=new CALLBACK_HandlerObject();
05264                     tandy_DAC_callback[1]=new CALLBACK_HandlerObject();
05265                     tandy_DAC_callback[0]->Install(&IRQ_TandyDAC,CB_IRET,"Tandy DAC IRQ");
05266                     tandy_DAC_callback[1]->Install(NULL,CB_TDE_IRET,"Tandy DAC end transfer");
05267                     // pseudocode for CB_TDE_IRET:
05268                     //  push ax
05269                     //  mov ax, 0x91fb
05270                     //  int 15
05271                     //  cli
05272                     //  mov al, 0x20
05273                     //  out 0x20, al
05274                     //  pop ax
05275                     //  iret
05276 
05277                     Bit8u tandy_irq = 7;
05278                     if (tandy_dac_type==1) tandy_irq = tandy_sb.irq;
05279                     else if (tandy_dac_type==2) tandy_irq = tandy_dac.irq;
05280                     Bit8u tandy_irq_vector = tandy_irq;
05281                     if (tandy_irq_vector<8) tandy_irq_vector += 8;
05282                     else tandy_irq_vector += (0x70-8);
05283 
05284                     RealPt current_irq=RealGetVec(tandy_irq_vector);
05285                     real_writed(0x40,0xd6,current_irq);
05286                     for (Bit16u i=0; i<0x10; i++) phys_writeb(PhysMake(0xf000,0xa084+i),0x80);
05287                 } else real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,0x00);
05288             }
05289         }
05290 
05291         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05292             /* Setup some stuff in 0x40 bios segment */
05293 
05294             // Disney workaround
05295             //          Bit16u disney_port = mem_readw(BIOS_ADDRESS_LPT1);
05296             // port timeouts
05297             // always 1 second even if the port does not exist
05298             //          BIOS_SetLPTPort(0, disney_port);
05299             for(Bitu i = 1; i < 3; i++) BIOS_SetLPTPort(i, 0);
05300             mem_writeb(BIOS_COM1_TIMEOUT,1);
05301             mem_writeb(BIOS_COM2_TIMEOUT,1);
05302             mem_writeb(BIOS_COM3_TIMEOUT,1);
05303             mem_writeb(BIOS_COM4_TIMEOUT,1);
05304 
05305             void BIOS_Post_register_parports();
05306             BIOS_Post_register_parports();
05307 
05308             void BIOS_Post_register_comports();
05309             BIOS_Post_register_comports();
05310         }
05311 
05312         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05313             /* Setup equipment list */
05314             // look http://www.bioscentral.com/misc/bda.htm
05315 
05316             //Bit16u config=0x4400;     //1 Floppy, 2 serial and 1 parallel 
05317             Bit16u config = 0x0;
05318 
05319             Bitu bios_post_parport_count();
05320             config |= bios_post_parport_count() << 14;
05321 
05322             Bitu bios_post_comport_count();
05323             config |= bios_post_comport_count() << 9;
05324 
05325 #if (C_FPU)
05326             extern bool enable_fpu;
05327 
05328             //FPU
05329             if (enable_fpu)
05330                 config|=0x2;
05331 #endif
05332             switch (machine) {
05333                 case MCH_HERC:
05334                     //Startup monochrome
05335                     config|=0x30;
05336                     break;
05337                 case EGAVGA_ARCH_CASE:
05338                 case MCH_CGA:
05339                 case TANDY_ARCH_CASE:
05340                 case MCH_AMSTRAD:
05341                     //Startup 80x25 color
05342                     config|=0x20;
05343                     break;
05344                 default:
05345                     //EGA VGA
05346                     config|=0;
05347                     break;
05348             }
05349 
05350             // PS2 mouse
05351             bool KEYBOARD_Report_BIOS_PS2Mouse();
05352             if (KEYBOARD_Report_BIOS_PS2Mouse())
05353                 config |= 0x04;
05354 
05355             // Gameport
05356             config |= 0x1000;
05357             mem_writew(BIOS_CONFIGURATION,config);
05358             CMOS_SetRegister(0x14,(Bit8u)(config&0xff)); //Should be updated on changes
05359         }
05360 
05361         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05362             /* Setup extended memory size */
05363             IO_Write(0x70,0x30);
05364             size_extended=IO_Read(0x71);
05365             IO_Write(0x70,0x31);
05366             size_extended|=(IO_Read(0x71) << 8);
05367             BIOS_HostTimeSync();
05368         }
05369         else {
05370             /* Provide a valid memory size anyway */
05371             size_extended=MEM_TotalPages()*4;
05372             if (size_extended >= 1024) size_extended -= 1024;
05373             else size_extended = 0;
05374         }
05375 
05376         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05377             /* PS/2 mouse */
05378             void BIOS_PS2Mouse_Startup(Section *sec);
05379             BIOS_PS2Mouse_Startup(NULL);
05380         }
05381 
05382         if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05383             /* this belongs HERE not on-demand from INT 15h! */
05384             biosConfigSeg = ROMBIOS_GetMemory(16/*one paragraph*/,"BIOS configuration (INT 15h AH=0xC0)",/*paragraph align*/16)>>4;
05385             if (biosConfigSeg != 0) {
05386                 PhysPt data = PhysMake(biosConfigSeg,0);
05387                 phys_writew(data,8);                                            // 8 Bytes following
05388                 if (IS_TANDY_ARCH) {
05389                     if (machine==MCH_TANDY) {
05390                         // Model ID (Tandy)
05391                         phys_writeb(data+2,0xFF);
05392                     } else {
05393                         // Model ID (PCJR)
05394                         phys_writeb(data+2,0xFD);
05395                     }
05396                     phys_writeb(data+3,0x0A);                                   // Submodel ID
05397                     phys_writeb(data+4,0x10);                                   // Bios Revision
05398                     /* Tandy doesn't have a 2nd PIC, left as is for now */
05399                     phys_writeb(data+5,(1<<6)|(1<<5)|(1<<4));   // Feature Byte 1
05400                 } else {
05401                     if (PS1AudioCard) { /* FIXME: Won't work because BIOS_Init() comes before PS1SOUND_Init() */
05402                         phys_writeb(data+2,0xFC);                                       // Model ID (PC)
05403                         phys_writeb(data+3,0x0B);                                       // Submodel ID (PS/1).
05404                     } else {
05405                         phys_writeb(data+2,0xFC);                                       // Model ID (PC)
05406                         phys_writeb(data+3,0x00);                                       // Submodel ID
05407                     }
05408                     phys_writeb(data+4,0x01);                                   // Bios Revision
05409                     phys_writeb(data+5,(1<<6)|(1<<5)|(1<<4));   // Feature Byte 1
05410                 }
05411                 phys_writeb(data+6,(1<<6));                             // Feature Byte 2
05412                 phys_writeb(data+7,0);                                  // Feature Byte 3
05413                 phys_writeb(data+8,0);                                  // Feature Byte 4
05414                 phys_writeb(data+9,0);                                  // Feature Byte 5
05415             }
05416         }
05417 
05418                 // ISA Plug & Play I/O ports
05419                 if (!IS_PC98_ARCH) {
05420                         ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT = new IO_WriteHandleObject;
05421                         ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT->Install(0x279,isapnp_write_port,IO_MB);
05422                         ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT = new IO_WriteHandleObject;
05423                         ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT->Install(0xA79,isapnp_write_port,IO_MB);
05424                         ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT = new IO_ReadHandleObject;
05425                         ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT->Install(ISA_PNP_WPORT,isapnp_read_port,IO_MB);
05426                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Registered ISA PnP read port at 0x%03x",ISA_PNP_WPORT);
05427                 }
05428 
05429                 if (!IS_PC98_ARCH && enable_integration_device) {
05430             /* integration device callout */
05431             if (dosbox_int_iocallout == IO_Callout_t_none)
05432                 dosbox_int_iocallout = IO_AllocateCallout(IO_TYPE_MB);
05433             if (dosbox_int_iocallout == IO_Callout_t_none)
05434                 E_Exit("Failed to get dosbox integration IO callout handle");
05435 
05436             {
05437                 IO_CalloutObject *obj = IO_GetCallout(dosbox_int_iocallout);
05438                 if (obj == NULL) E_Exit("Failed to get dosbox integration IO callout");
05439                 obj->Install(0x28,IOMASK_Combine(IOMASK_FULL,IOMASK_Range(4)),dosbox_integration_cb_port_r,dosbox_integration_cb_port_w);
05440                 IO_PutCallout(obj);
05441             }
05442 
05443             /* DOSBox integration device */
05444             if (isapnpigdevice == NULL && enable_integration_device_pnp) {
05445                 isapnpigdevice = new ISAPnPIntegrationDevice;
05446                 ISA_PNP_devreg(isapnpigdevice);
05447             }
05448                 }
05449 
05450                 // ISA Plug & Play BIOS entrypoint
05451         // NTS: Apparently, Windows 95, 98, and ME will re-enumerate and re-install PnP devices if our entry point changes it's address.
05452                 if (!IS_PC98_ARCH && ISAPNPBIOS) {
05453                         int i;
05454                         Bitu base;
05455                         unsigned char c,tmp[256];
05456 
05457                         if (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping)
05458                                 isapnp_biosstruct_base = base = 0xFE100; /* take the unused space just after the fake BIOS signature */
05459                         else
05460                                 isapnp_biosstruct_base = base = ROMBIOS_GetMemory(0x21,"ISA Plug & Play BIOS struct",/*paragraph alignment*/0x10);
05461 
05462                         if (base == 0) E_Exit("Unable to allocate ISA PnP struct");
05463                         LOG_MSG("ISA Plug & Play BIOS enabled");
05464 
05465                         call_pnp_r = CALLBACK_Allocate();
05466                         call_pnp_rp = PNPentry_real = CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_pnp_r);
05467                         CALLBACK_Setup(call_pnp_r,ISAPNP_Handler_RM,CB_RETF,"ISA Plug & Play entry point (real)");
05468                         //LOG_MSG("real entry pt=%08lx\n",PNPentry_real);
05469 
05470                         call_pnp_p = CALLBACK_Allocate();
05471                         call_pnp_pp = PNPentry_prot = CALLBACK_RealPointer(call_pnp_p);
05472                         CALLBACK_Setup(call_pnp_p,ISAPNP_Handler_PM,CB_RETF,"ISA Plug & Play entry point (protected)");
05473                         //LOG_MSG("prot entry pt=%08lx\n",PNPentry_prot);
05474 
05475                         phys_writeb(base+0,'$');
05476                         phys_writeb(base+1,'P');
05477                         phys_writeb(base+2,'n');
05478                         phys_writeb(base+3,'P');
05479                         phys_writeb(base+4,0x10);               /* Version:             1.0 */
05480                         phys_writeb(base+5,0x21);               /* Length:              0x21 bytes */
05481                         phys_writew(base+6,0x0000);             /* Control field:       Event notification not supported */
05482                         /* skip checksum atm */
05483                         phys_writed(base+9,0);                  /* Event notify flag addr: (none) */
05484                         phys_writed(base+0xD,call_pnp_rp);      /* Real-mode entry point */
05485                         phys_writew(base+0x11,call_pnp_pp&0xFFFF); /* Protected mode offset */
05486                         phys_writed(base+0x13,(call_pnp_pp >> 12) & 0xFFFF0); /* Protected mode code segment base */
05487                         phys_writed(base+0x17,ISAPNP_ID('D','O','S',0,7,4,0));          /* OEM device identifier (DOSBox 0.740, get it?) */
05488                         phys_writew(base+0x1B,0xF000);          /* real-mode data segment */
05489                         phys_writed(base+0x1D,0xF0000);         /* protected mode data segment address */
05490                         /* run checksum */
05491                         c=0;
05492                         for (i=0;i < 0x21;i++) {
05493                                 if (i != 8) c += phys_readb(base+i);
05494                         }
05495                         phys_writeb(base+8,0x100-c);            /* checksum value: set so that summing bytes across the struct == 0 */
05496 
05497                         /* input device (keyboard) */
05498                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_Keyboard,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_Keyboard),true))
05499                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05500 
05501                         /* input device (mouse) */
05502                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_Mouse,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_Mouse),true))
05503                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05504 
05505                         /* DMA controller */
05506                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_DMA_Controller,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_DMA_Controller),true))
05507                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05508 
05509                         /* Interrupt controller */
05510                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_PIC,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_PIC),true))
05511                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05512 
05513                         /* Timer */
05514                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_Timer,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_Timer),true))
05515                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05516 
05517                         /* Realtime clock */
05518                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_RTC,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_RTC),true))
05519                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05520 
05521                         /* PC speaker */
05522                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_PC_Speaker,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_PC_Speaker),true))
05523                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05524 
05525                         /* System board */
05526                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_System_Board,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_System_Board),true))
05527                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05528 
05529                         /* Motherboard PNP resources and general */
05530                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_General_ISAPNP,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_General_ISAPNP),true))
05531                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05532 
05533                         /* ISA bus, meaning, a computer with ISA slots.
05534                          * The purpose of this device is to convince Windows 95 to automatically install it's
05535                          * "ISA Plug and Play bus" so that PnP devices are recognized automatically */
05536                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_ISA_BUS,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_ISA_BUS),true))
05537                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05538 
05539                         if (pcibus_enable) {
05540                                 /* PCI bus, meaning, a computer with PCI slots.
05541                                  * The purpose of this device is to tell Windows 95 that a PCI bus is present. Without
05542                                  * this entry, PCI devices will not be recognized until you manually install the PCI driver. */
05543                                 if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_PCI_BUS,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_PCI_BUS),true))
05544                                         LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05545                         }
05546 
05547                         /* APM BIOS device. To help Windows 95 see our APM BIOS. */
05548                         if (APMBIOS && APMBIOS_pnp) {
05549                                 LOG_MSG("Registering APM BIOS as ISA Plug & Play BIOS device node");
05550                                 if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_APM_BIOS,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_APM_BIOS),true))
05551                                         LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05552                         }
05553 
05554 #if (C_FPU)
05555                         /* Numeric Coprocessor */
05556                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(ISAPNP_sysdev_Numeric_Coprocessor,sizeof(ISAPNP_sysdev_Numeric_Coprocessor),true))
05557                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05558 #endif
05559 
05560                         /* RAM resources. we have to construct it */
05561                         /* NTS: We don't do this here, but I have an old Toshiba laptop who's PnP BIOS uses
05562                          *      this device ID to report both RAM and ROM regions. */
05563                         {
05564                                 Bitu max = MEM_TotalPages() * 4096;
05565                                 const unsigned char h1[9] = {
05566                                         ISAPNP_SYSDEV_HEADER(
05567                                                 ISAPNP_ID('P','N','P',0x0,0xC,0x0,0x1), /* PNP0C01 System device, motherboard resources */
05568                                                 ISAPNP_TYPE(0x05,0x00,0x00),            /* type: Memory, RAM, general */
05569                                                 0x0001 | 0x0002)
05570                                 };
05571 
05572                                 i = 0;
05573                                 memcpy(tmp+i,h1,9); i += 9;                     /* can't disable, can't configure */
05574                                 /*----------allocated--------*/
05575                                 tmp[i+0] = 0x80 | 6;                            /* 32-bit memory range */
05576                                 tmp[i+1] = 9;                                   /* length=9 */
05577                                 tmp[i+2] = 0;
05578                                 tmp[i+3] = 0x01;                                /* writeable, no cache, 8-bit, not shadowable, not ROM */
05579                                 host_writed(tmp+i+4,0x00000);                   /* base */
05580                                 host_writed(tmp+i+8,max > 0xA0000 ? 0xA0000 : 0x00000); /* length */
05581                                 i += 9+3;
05582 
05583                                 if (max > 0x100000) {
05584                                         tmp[i+0] = 0x80 | 6;                            /* 32-bit memory range */
05585                                         tmp[i+1] = 9;                                   /* length=9 */
05586                                         tmp[i+2] = 0;
05587                                         tmp[i+3] = 0x01;
05588                                         host_writed(tmp+i+4,0x100000);                  /* base */
05589                                         host_writed(tmp+i+8,max-0x100000);              /* length */
05590                                         i += 9+3;
05591                                 }
05592 
05593                                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05594                                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05595                                 i += 2;
05596                                 /*-------------possible-----------*/
05597                                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05598                                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05599                                 i += 2;
05600                                 /*-------------compatible---------*/
05601                                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05602                                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05603                                 i += 2;
05604 
05605                                 if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(tmp,i))
05606                                         LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05607                         }
05608 
05609                         /* register parallel ports */
05610                         for (Bitu portn=0;portn < 3;portn++) {
05611                                 Bitu port = mem_readw(BIOS_ADDRESS_LPT1+(portn*2));
05612                                 if (port != 0) {
05613                                         const unsigned char h1[9] = {
05614                                                 ISAPNP_SYSDEV_HEADER(
05615                                                         ISAPNP_ID('P','N','P',0x0,0x4,0x0,0x0), /* PNP0400 Standard LPT printer port */
05616                                                         ISAPNP_TYPE(0x07,0x01,0x00),            /* type: General parallel port */
05617                                                         0x0001 | 0x0002)
05618                                         };
05619 
05620                                         i = 0;
05621                                         memcpy(tmp+i,h1,9); i += 9;                     /* can't disable, can't configure */
05622                                         /*----------allocated--------*/
05623                                         tmp[i+0] = (8 << 3) | 7;                        /* IO resource */
05624                                         tmp[i+1] = 0x01;                                /* 16-bit decode */
05625                                         host_writew(tmp+i+2,port);                      /* min */
05626                                         host_writew(tmp+i+4,port);                      /* max */
05627                                         tmp[i+6] = 0x10;                                /* align */
05628                                         tmp[i+7] = 0x03;                                /* length */
05629                                         i += 7+1;
05630 
05631                                         /* TODO: If/when LPT emulation handles the IRQ, add IRQ resource here */
05632 
05633                                         tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05634                                         tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05635                                         i += 2;
05636                                         /*-------------possible-----------*/
05637                                         tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05638                                         tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05639                                         i += 2;
05640                                         /*-------------compatible---------*/
05641                                         tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
05642                                         tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
05643                                         i += 2;
05644 
05645                                         if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(tmp,i))
05646                                                 LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
05647                                 }
05648                         }
05649 
05650                         void BIOS_Post_register_comports_PNP();
05651                         BIOS_Post_register_comports_PNP();
05652 
05653             void BIOS_Post_register_IDE();
05654             BIOS_Post_register_IDE();
05655 
05656             void BIOS_Post_register_FDC();
05657             BIOS_Post_register_FDC();
05658                 }
05659 
05660         CPU_STI();
05661 
05662                 return CBRET_NONE;
05663         }
05664         CALLBACK_HandlerObject cb_bios_scan_video_bios;
05665         static Bitu cb_bios_scan_video_bios__func(void) {
05666                 unsigned long size;
05667 
05668         /* NTS: As far as I can tell, video is integrated into the PC-98 BIOS and there is no separate BIOS */
05669                 if (IS_PC98_ARCH) return CBRET_NONE;
05670 
05671                 if (cpu.pmode) E_Exit("BIOS error: VIDEO BIOS SCAN function called while in protected/vm86 mode");
05672 
05673                 if (!bios_has_exec_vga_bios) {
05674                         bios_has_exec_vga_bios = true;
05675                         if (IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) {
05676                                 /* make sure VGA BIOS is there at 0xC000:0x0000 */
05677                                 if (AdapterROM_Read(0xC0000,&size)) {
05678                                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("BIOS VIDEO ROM SCAN found VGA BIOS (size=%lu)",size);
05679                                         adapter_scan_start = 0xC0000 + size;
05680 
05681                     // step back into the callback instruction that triggered this call
05682                     reg_eip -= 4;
05683 
05684                     // FAR CALL into the VGA BIOS
05685                     CPU_CALL(false,0xC000,0x0003,reg_eip);
05686                     return CBRET_NONE;
05687                 }
05688                 else {
05689                     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_WARN)("BIOS VIDEO ROM SCAN did not find VGA BIOS");
05690                                 }
05691                         }
05692                         else {
05693                                 // CGA, MDA, Tandy, PCjr. No video BIOS to scan for
05694                         }
05695                 }
05696 
05697                 return CBRET_NONE;
05698         }
05699         CALLBACK_HandlerObject cb_bios_adapter_rom_scan;
05700         static Bitu cb_bios_adapter_rom_scan__func(void) {
05701                 unsigned long size;
05702                 Bit32u c1;
05703 
05704         /* FIXME: I have no documentation on how PC-98 scans for adapter ROM or even if it supports it */
05705                 if (IS_PC98_ARCH) return CBRET_NONE;
05706 
05707                 if (cpu.pmode) E_Exit("BIOS error: ADAPTER ROM function called while in protected/vm86 mode");
05708 
05709                 while (adapter_scan_start < 0xF0000) {
05710                         if (AdapterROM_Read(adapter_scan_start,&size)) {
05711                                 Bit16u segm = (Bit16u)(adapter_scan_start >> 4);
05712 
05713                                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("BIOS ADAPTER ROM scan found ROM at 0x%lx (size=%lu)",(unsigned long)adapter_scan_start,size);
05714 
05715                                 c1 = mem_readd(adapter_scan_start+3);
05716                                 adapter_scan_start += size;
05717                                 if (c1 != 0UL) {
05718                                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Running ADAPTER ROM entry point");
05719 
05720                                         // step back into the callback instruction that triggered this call
05721                                         reg_eip -= 4;
05722 
05723                                         // FAR CALL into the VGA BIOS
05724                                         CPU_CALL(false,segm,0x0003,reg_eip);
05725                                         return CBRET_NONE;
05726                                 }
05727                                 else {
05728                                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("FIXME: ADAPTER ROM entry point does not exist");
05729                                 }
05730                         }
05731                         else {
05732                                 if (IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) // supposedly newer systems only scan on 2KB boundaries by standard? right?
05733                                         adapter_scan_start = (adapter_scan_start | 2047UL) + 1UL;
05734                                 else // while older PC/XT systems scanned on 512-byte boundaries? right?
05735                                         adapter_scan_start = (adapter_scan_start | 511UL) + 1UL;
05736                         }
05737                 }
05738 
05739                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("BIOS ADAPTER ROM scan complete");
05740                 return CBRET_NONE;
05741         }
05742         CALLBACK_HandlerObject cb_bios_startup_screen;
05743         static Bitu cb_bios_startup_screen__func(void) {
05744                 const char *msg = PACKAGE_STRING " (C) 2002-" COPYRIGHT_END_YEAR " The DOSBox Team\nA fork of DOSBox 0.74 by TheGreatCodeholio\nFor more info visit http://dosbox-x.com\nBased on DOSBox (http://dosbox.com)\n\n";
05745                 int logo_x,logo_y,x,y,rowheight=8;
05746 
05747                 y = 2;
05748                 x = 2;
05749                 logo_y = 2;
05750                 logo_x = 80 - 2 - (224/8);
05751 
05752                 if (cpu.pmode) E_Exit("BIOS error: STARTUP function called while in protected/vm86 mode");
05753 
05754                 // TODO: For those who would rather not use the VGA graphical modes, add a configuration option to "disable graphical splash".
05755                 //       We would then revert to a plain text copyright and status message here (and maybe an ASCII art version of the DOSBox logo).
05756                 if (IS_VGA_ARCH) {
05757                         rowheight = 16;
05758                         reg_eax = 18;           // 640x480 16-color
05759                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05760                         DrawDOSBoxLogoVGA(logo_x*8,logo_y*rowheight);
05761                 }
05762                 else if (machine == MCH_EGA) {
05763                         rowheight = 14;
05764                         reg_eax = 16;           // 640x350 16-color
05765                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05766 
05767                         // color correction: change Dark Puke Yellow to brown
05768                         IO_Read(0x3DA); IO_Read(0x3BA);
05769                         IO_Write(0x3C0,0x06);
05770                         IO_Write(0x3C0,0x14); // red=1 green=1 blue=0
05771                         IO_Read(0x3DA); IO_Read(0x3BA);
05772                         IO_Write(0x3C0,0x20);
05773 
05774                         DrawDOSBoxLogoVGA(logo_x*8,logo_y*rowheight);
05775                 }
05776                 else if (machine == MCH_CGA || machine == MCH_PCJR || machine == MCH_AMSTRAD || machine == MCH_TANDY) {
05777                         rowheight = 8;
05778                         reg_eax = 6;            // 640x200 2-color
05779                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05780 
05781                         DrawDOSBoxLogoCGA6(logo_x*8,logo_y*rowheight);
05782                 }
05783         else if (machine == MCH_PC98) {
05784             // clear the graphics layer
05785             for (unsigned int i=0;i < (80*400);i++) {
05786                 mem_writeb(0xA8000+i,0);        // B
05787                 mem_writeb(0xB0000+i,0);        // G
05788                 mem_writeb(0xB8000+i,0);        // R
05789                 mem_writeb(0xE0000+i,0);        // E
05790             }
05791 
05792             reg_eax = 0x0C00;   // enable text layer (PC-98)
05793                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05794 
05795             reg_eax = 0x1100;   // show cursor (PC-98)
05796                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05797 
05798             reg_eax = 0x1300;   // set cursor pos (PC-98)
05799             reg_edx = 0x0000;   // byte position
05800                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05801 
05802             bios_pc98_posx = x;
05803 
05804             reg_eax = 0x4200;   // setup 640x400 graphics
05805             reg_ecx = 0xC000;
05806                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05807 
05808             // enable the 4th bitplane, for 16-color analog graphics mode.
05809             // TODO: When we allow the user to emulate only the 8-color BGR digital mode,
05810             //       logo drawing should use an alternate drawing method.
05811                 IO_Write(0x6A,0x01);    // enable 16-color analog mode (this makes the 4th bitplane appear)
05812                 IO_Write(0x6A,0x04);    // but we don't need the EGC graphics
05813             // If we caught a game mid-page flip, set the display and VRAM pages back to zero
05814             IO_Write(0xA4,0x00);    // display page 0
05815             IO_Write(0xA6,0x00);    // write to page 0
05816 
05817             // program a VGA-like color palette so we can re-use the VGA logo
05818             for (unsigned int i=0;i < 16;i++) {
05819                 unsigned int bias = (i & 8) ? 0x5 : 0x0;
05820 
05821                 IO_Write(0xA8,i);   // DAC index
05822                 if (i != 6) {
05823                     IO_Write(0xAA,((i & 2) ? 0xA : 0x0) + bias);    // green
05824                     IO_Write(0xAC,((i & 4) ? 0xA : 0x0) + bias);    // red
05825                     IO_Write(0xAE,((i & 1) ? 0xA : 0x0) + bias);    // blue
05826                 }
05827                 else { // brown #6 instead of puke yellow
05828                     IO_Write(0xAA,((i & 2) ? 0x5 : 0x0) + bias);    // green
05829                     IO_Write(0xAC,((i & 4) ? 0xA : 0x0) + bias);    // red
05830                     IO_Write(0xAE,((i & 1) ? 0xA : 0x0) + bias);    // blue
05831                 }
05832             }
05833 
05834                         DrawDOSBoxLogoPC98(logo_x*8,logo_y*rowheight);
05835 
05836             reg_eax = 0x4000;   // show the graphics layer (PC-98) so we can render the DOSBox logo
05837                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05838         }
05839                 else {
05840                         reg_eax = 3;            // 80x25 text
05841                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05842 
05843                         // TODO: For CGA, PCjr, and Tandy, we could render a 4-color CGA version of the same logo.
05844                         //       And for MDA/Hercules, we could render a monochromatic ASCII art version.
05845                 }
05846 
05847         if (machine != MCH_PC98) {
05848             reg_eax = 0x0200;   // set cursor pos
05849                         reg_ebx = 0;            // page zero
05850                         reg_dh = y;             // row 4
05851                         reg_dl = x;             // column 20
05852                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05853                 }
05854 
05855                 BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,msg);
05856 
05857                 {
05858                         uint64_t sz = (uint64_t)MEM_TotalPages() * (uint64_t)4096;
05859                         char tmp[512];
05860 
05861                         if (sz >= ((uint64_t)128 << (uint64_t)20))
05862                                 sprintf(tmp,"%uMB memory installed\r\n",(unsigned int)(sz >> (uint64_t)20));
05863                         else
05864                                 sprintf(tmp,"%uKB memory installed\r\n",(unsigned int)(sz >> (uint64_t)10));
05865 
05866                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,tmp);
05867                 }
05868 
05869                 {
05870                         char tmp[512];
05871                         const char *card = "?";
05872 
05873                         switch (machine) {
05874                                 case MCH_CGA:
05875                                         card = "IBM Color Graphics Adapter";
05876                                         break;
05877                                 case MCH_HERC:
05878                                         card = "IBM Monochrome Display Adapter (Hercules)";
05879                                         break;
05880                                 case MCH_EGA:
05881                                         card = "IBM Enhanced Graphics Adapter";
05882                                         break;
05883                                 case MCH_PCJR:
05884                                         card = "PCjr graohics adapter";
05885                                         break;
05886                                 case MCH_TANDY:
05887                                         card = "Tandy graohics adapter";
05888                                         break;
05889                                 case MCH_VGA:
05890                                         switch (svgaCard) {
05891                                                 case SVGA_TsengET4K:
05892                                                         card = "Tseng ET4000 SVGA";
05893                                                         break;
05894                                                 case SVGA_TsengET3K:
05895                                                         card = "Tseng ET3000 SVGA";
05896                                                         break;
05897                                                 case SVGA_ParadisePVGA1A:
05898                                                         card = "Paradise SVGA";
05899                                                         break;
05900                                                 case SVGA_S3Trio:
05901                                                         card = "S3 Trio SVGA";
05902                                                         break;
05903                                                 default:
05904                                                         card = "Standard VGA";
05905                                                         break;
05906                                         }
05907 
05908                                         break;
05909                                 case MCH_PC98:
05910                                         card = "PC98 graphics";
05911                                         break;
05912                                 case MCH_AMSTRAD:
05913                                         card = "Amstrad graphics";
05914                                         break;
05915                         };
05916 
05917                         sprintf(tmp,"Video card is %s\n",card);
05918                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,tmp);
05919                 }
05920 
05921                 {
05922                         char tmp[512];
05923                         const char *cpu = "?";
05924 
05925                         switch (CPU_ArchitectureType) {
05926                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_8086:
05927                                         cpu = "8086";
05928                                         break;
05929                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_80186:
05930                                         cpu = "80186";
05931                                         break;
05932                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_286:
05933                                         cpu = "286";
05934                                         break;
05935                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_386:
05936                                         cpu = "386";
05937                                         break;
05938                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_486OLD:
05939                                         cpu = "486 (older generation)";
05940                                         break;
05941                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_486NEW:
05942                                         cpu = "486 (later generation)";
05943                                         break;
05944                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_PENTIUM:
05945                                         cpu = "Pentium";
05946                                         break;
05947                                 case CPU_ARCHTYPE_P55CSLOW:
05948                                         cpu = "Pentium MMX";
05949                                         break;
05950                         };
05951 
05952                         extern bool enable_fpu;
05953 
05954                         sprintf(tmp,"%s CPU present",cpu);
05955                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,tmp);
05956                         if (enable_fpu) BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y," with FPU");
05957                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,"\n");
05958                 }
05959 
05960                 if (APMBIOS) {
05961                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,"Advanced Power Management interface active\n");
05962                 }
05963 
05964                 if (ISAPNPBIOS) {
05965                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,"ISA Plug & Play BIOS active\n");
05966                 }
05967 
05968                 BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,"\nHit SPACEBAR to pause at this screen\n");
05969                 y--; /* next message should overprint */
05970         if (machine != MCH_PC98) {
05971                         reg_eax = 0x0200;       // set cursor pos
05972                         reg_ebx = 0;            // page zero
05973                         reg_dh = y;             // row 4
05974                         reg_dl = x;             // column 20
05975                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
05976                 }
05977         else {
05978             reg_eax = 0x1300;   // set cursor pos (PC-98)
05979             reg_edx = ((y * 80) + x) * 2; // byte position
05980                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05981         }
05982 
05983                 // TODO: Then at this screen, we can print messages demonstrating the detection of
05984                 //       IDE devices, floppy, ISA PnP initialization, anything of importance.
05985                 //       I also envision adding the ability to hit DEL or F2 at this point to enter
05986                 //       a "BIOS setup" screen where all DOSBox configuration options can be
05987                 //       modified, with the same look and feel of an old BIOS.
05988 
05989                 bool wait_for_user = false;
05990                 Bit32u lasttick=GetTicks();
05991                 while ((GetTicks()-lasttick)<1000) {
05992             if (machine == MCH_PC98) {
05993                 reg_eax = 0x0100;   // sense key
05994                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
05995                 SETFLAGBIT(ZF,reg_bh == 0);
05996             }
05997             else {
05998                 reg_eax = 0x0100;
05999                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x16);
06000             }
06001 
06002                         if (!GETFLAG(ZF)) {
06003                 if (machine == MCH_PC98) {
06004                     reg_eax = 0x0000;   // read key
06005                     CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
06006                 }
06007                 else {
06008                     reg_eax = 0x0000;
06009                     CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x16);
06010                 }
06011
