06012                                 if (reg_al == 32) { // user hit space
06013                                         BIOS_Int10RightJustifiedPrint(x,y,"Hit ENTER or ESC to continue                    \n"); // overprint
06014                                         wait_for_user = true;
06015                                         break;
06016                                 }
06017                         }
06018                 }
06019 
06020         while (wait_for_user) {
06021             if (machine == MCH_PC98) {
06022                 reg_eax = 0x0000;   // read key
06023                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
06024             }
06025             else {
06026                 reg_eax = 0x0000;
06027                 CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x16);
06028             }
06029 
06030             if (reg_al == 27/*ESC*/ || reg_al == 13/*ENTER*/)
06031                 break;
06032         }
06033 
06034         if (machine == MCH_PC98) {
06035             reg_eax = 0x4100;   // hide the graphics layer (PC-98)
06036                         CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x18);
06037 
06038             // clear the graphics layer
06039             for (unsigned int i=0;i < (80*400);i++) {
06040                 mem_writeb(0xA8000+i,0);        // B
06041                 mem_writeb(0xB0000+i,0);        // G
06042                 mem_writeb(0xB8000+i,0);        // R
06043                 mem_writeb(0xE0000+i,0);        // E
06044             }
06045 
06046             IO_Write(0x6A,0x00);    // switch back to 8-color mode
06047         }
06048         else {
06049             // restore 80x25 text mode
06050             reg_eax = 3;
06051             CALLBACK_RunRealInt(0x10);
06052         }
06053 
06054                 return CBRET_NONE;
06055         }
06056         CALLBACK_HandlerObject cb_bios_boot;
06057         static Bitu cb_bios_boot__func(void) {
06058                 /* Reset/power-on overrides the user's A20 gate preferences.
06059                  * It's time to revert back to what the user wants. */
06060                 void A20Gate_TakeUserSetting(Section *sec);
06061                 void MEM_A20_Enable(bool enabled);
06062                 A20Gate_TakeUserSetting(NULL);
06063                 MEM_A20_Enable(false);
06064 
06065                 if (cpu.pmode) E_Exit("BIOS error: BOOT function called while in protected/vm86 mode");
06066                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_BIOS_BOOT);
06067 
06068                 // TODO: If instructed to, follow the INT 19h boot pattern, perhaps follow the BIOS Boot Specification, etc.
06069 
06070                 // TODO: If instructed to boot a guest OS...
06071 
06072                 // Begin booting the DOSBox shell. NOTE: VM_Boot_DOSBox_Kernel will change CS:IP instruction pointer!
06073                 if (!VM_Boot_DOSBox_Kernel()) E_Exit("BIOS error: BOOT function failed to boot DOSBox kernel");
06074                 return CBRET_NONE;
06075         }
06076 public:
06077         void write_FFFF_signature() {
06078                 /* write the signature at 0xF000:0xFFF0 */
06079 
06080                 // The farjump at the processor reset entry point (jumps to POST routine)
06081                 phys_writeb(0xffff0,0xEA);                                      // FARJMP
06082                 phys_writew(0xffff1,RealOff(BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION));      // offset
06083                 phys_writew(0xffff3,RealSeg(BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION));      // segment
06084 
06085                 // write system BIOS date
06086                 for(Bitu i = 0; i < strlen(bios_date_string); i++) phys_writeb(0xffff5+i,bios_date_string[i]);
06087 
06088                 /* model byte */
06089                 if (machine==MCH_TANDY || machine==MCH_AMSTRAD) phys_writeb(0xffffe,0xff);      /* Tandy model */
06090                 else if (machine==MCH_PCJR) phys_writeb(0xffffe,0xfd);  /* PCJr model */
06091                 else phys_writeb(0xffffe,0xfc); /* PC */
06092 
06093                 // signature
06094                 phys_writeb(0xfffff,0x55);
06095         }
06096         BIOS(Section* configuration):Module_base(configuration){
06097                 /* tandy DAC can be requested in tandy_sound.cpp by initializing this field */
06098                 Bitu wo;
06099 
06100         isapnp_biosstruct_base = 0;
06101 
06102                 { // TODO: Eventually, move this to BIOS POST or init phase
06103                         Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06104 
06105                         bochs_port_e9 = section->Get_bool("bochs debug port e9");
06106 
06107                         // TODO: motherboard init, especially when we get around to full Intel Triton/i440FX chipset emulation
06108                         isa_memory_hole_512kb = section->Get_bool("isa memory hole at 512kb");
06109 
06110                         // FIXME: Erm, well this couldv'e been named better. It refers to the amount of conventional memory
06111                         //        made available to the operating system below 1MB, which is usually DOS.
06112                         dos_conventional_limit = section->Get_int("dos mem limit");
06113                 }
06114 
06115                 if (bochs_port_e9) {
06116                         if (BOCHS_PORT_E9 == NULL) {
06117                                 BOCHS_PORT_E9 = new IO_WriteHandleObject;
06118                                 BOCHS_PORT_E9->Install(0xE9,bochs_port_e9_write,IO_MB);
06119                         }
06120                         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Bochs port E9h emulation is active");
06121                 }
06122                 else {
06123                         if (BOCHS_PORT_E9 != NULL) {
06124                                 delete BOCHS_PORT_E9;
06125                                 BOCHS_PORT_E9 = NULL;
06126                         }
06127                 }
06128 
06129                 /* pick locations */
06130                 if (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping) { /* mapping BIOS the way mainline DOSBox does */
06131                         BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xe05b);
06132                         BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xff53);
06133                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ0_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xfea5);
06134                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ1_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xe987);
06135                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xff55);
06136                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ815_DEF_LOCATION = RealMake(0xf000,0xe880);
06137                 }
06138                 else {
06139                         BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(64/*several callbacks*/,"BIOS default reset location",/*align*/4));
06140                         BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(1/*IRET*/,"BIOS default handler location",/*align*/4));
06141                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ0_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(0x13/*see callback.cpp for IRQ0*/,"BIOS default IRQ0 location",/*align*/4));
06142                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ1_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(0x15/*see callback.cpp for IRQ1*/,"BIOS default IRQ1 location",/*align*/4));
06143                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(7/*see callback.cpp for EOI_PIC1*/,"BIOS default IRQ2-7 location",/*align*/4));
06144                         BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ815_DEF_LOCATION = PhysToReal416(ROMBIOS_GetMemory(9/*see callback.cpp for EOI_PIC1*/,"BIOS default IRQ8-15 location",/*align*/4));
06145                 }
06146 
06147                 write_FFFF_signature();
06148 
06149                 /* Setup all the interrupt handlers the bios controls */
06150 
06151         /* INT 8 Clock IRQ Handler */
06152         call_irq0=CALLBACK_Allocate();
06153         if (IS_PC98_ARCH)
06154             CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq0,INT8_PC98_Handler,CB_IRET,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ0_LOCATION),"IRQ 0 Clock");
06155         else
06156             CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq0,INT8_Handler,CB_IRQ0,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ0_LOCATION),"IRQ 0 Clock");
06157 
06158                 /* INT 11 Get equipment list */
06159                 callback[1].Install(&INT11_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 11 Equipment");
06160 
06161                 /* INT 12 Memory Size default at 640 kb */
06162                 callback[2].Install(&INT12_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 12 Memory");
06163 
06164                 ulimit = 640;
06165                 t_conv = MEM_TotalPages() << 2; /* convert 4096/byte pages -> 1024/byte KB units */
06166                 if (allow_more_than_640kb) {
06167                         if (machine == MCH_CGA)
06168                                 ulimit = 736;           /* 640KB + 64KB + 32KB  0x00000-0xB7FFF */
06169                         else if (machine == MCH_HERC)
06170                                 ulimit = 704;           /* 640KB + 64KB = 0x00000-0xAFFFF */
06171 
06172                         if (t_conv > ulimit) t_conv = ulimit;
06173                         if (t_conv > 640) { /* because the memory emulation has already set things up */
06174                                 bool MEM_map_RAM_physmem(Bitu start,Bitu end);
06175                                 MEM_map_RAM_physmem(0xA0000,(t_conv<<10)-1);
06176                                 memset(GetMemBase()+(640<<10),0,(t_conv-640)<<10);
06177                         }
06178                 }
06179                 else {
06180                         if (t_conv > 640) t_conv = 640;
06181                 }
06182 
06183                 if (IS_TANDY_ARCH) {
06184                         /* reduce reported memory size for the Tandy (32k graphics memory
06185                            at the end of the conventional 640k) */
06186                         if (machine==MCH_TANDY && t_conv > 624) t_conv = 624;
06187                 }
06188 
06189                 /* allow user to further limit the available memory below 1MB */
06190                 if (dos_conventional_limit != 0 && t_conv > dos_conventional_limit)
06191                         t_conv = dos_conventional_limit;
06192 
06193                 // TODO: Allow dosbox.conf to specify an option to add an EBDA (Extended BIOS Data Area)
06194                 //       at the top of the DOS conventional limit, which we then reduce further to hold
06195                 //       it. Most BIOSes past 1992 or so allocate an EBDA.
06196 
06197                 /* if requested to emulate an ISA memory hole at 512KB, further limit the memory */
06198                 if (isa_memory_hole_512kb && t_conv > 512) t_conv = 512;
06199 
06200                 /* and then unmap RAM between t_conv and ulimit */
06201                 if (t_conv < ulimit) {
06202                         Bitu start = (t_conv+3)/4;      /* start = 1KB to page round up */
06203                         Bitu end = ulimit/4;            /* end = 1KB to page round down */
06204                         if (start < end) MEM_ResetPageHandler_Unmapped(start,end-start);
06205                 }
06206 
06207                 /* INT 4B. Now we can safely signal error instead of printing "Invalid interrupt 4B"
06208                  * whenever we install Windows 95. Note that Windows 95 would call INT 4Bh because
06209                  * that is where the Virtual DMA API lies in relation to EMM386.EXE */
06210                 int4b_callback.Install(&INT4B_Handler,CB_IRET,"INT 4B");
06211 
06212                 /* INT 14 Serial Ports */
06213                 callback[3].Install(&INT14_Handler,CB_IRET_STI,"Int 14 COM-port");
06214 
06215                 /* INT 15 Misc Calls */
06216                 callback[4].Install(&INT15_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 15 Bios");
06217 
06218                 /* INT 17 Printer Routines */
06219                 callback[5].Install(&INT17_Handler,CB_IRET_STI,"Int 17 Printer");
06220 
06221                 /* INT 1A TIME and some other functions */
06222                 callback[6].Install(&INT1A_Handler,CB_IRET_STI,"Int 1a Time");
06223 
06224                 /* INT 1C System Timer tick called from INT 8 */
06225                 callback[7].Install(&INT1C_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 1c Timer");
06226                 
06227                 /* IRQ 8 RTC Handler */
06228                 callback[8].Install(&INT70_Handler,CB_IRET,"Int 70 RTC");
06229 
06230                 /* Irq 9 rerouted to irq 2 */
06231                 callback[9].Install(NULL,CB_IRQ9,"irq 9 bios");
06232 
06233                 // INT 19h: Boot function
06234                 callback[10].Install(&INT19_Handler,CB_IRET,"int 19");
06235 
06236                 // INT 76h: IDE IRQ 14
06237                 // This is just a dummy IRQ handler to prevent crashes when
06238                 // IDE emulation fires the IRQ and OS's like Win95 expect
06239                 // the BIOS to handle the interrupt.
06240                 // FIXME: Shouldn't the IRQ send an ACK to the PIC as well?!?
06241                 callback[11].Install(&IRQ14_Dummy,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,"irq 14 ide");
06242 
06243                 // INT 77h: IDE IRQ 15
06244                 // This is just a dummy IRQ handler to prevent crashes when
06245                 // IDE emulation fires the IRQ and OS's like Win95 expect
06246                 // the BIOS to handle the interrupt.
06247                 // FIXME: Shouldn't the IRQ send an ACK to the PIC as well?!?
06248                 callback[12].Install(&IRQ15_Dummy,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,"irq 15 ide");
06249 
06250                 // INT 0Eh: IDE IRQ 6
06251                 callback[13].Install(&IRQ15_Dummy,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC1,"irq 6 floppy");
06252 
06253                 // INT 18h: Enter BASIC
06254                 // Non-IBM BIOS would display "NO ROM BASIC" here
06255                 callback[15].Install(&INT18_Handler,CB_IRET,"int 18");
06256 
06257                 init_vm86_fake_io();
06258 
06259                 /* Irq 2-7 */
06260                 call_irq07default=CALLBACK_Allocate();
06261                 CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq07default,NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC1,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ07_DEF_LOCATION),"bios irq 0-7 default handler");
06262 
06263                 /* Irq 8-15 */
06264                 call_irq815default=CALLBACK_Allocate();
06265                 CALLBACK_Setup(call_irq815default,NULL,CB_IRET_EOI_PIC2,Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_IRQ815_DEF_LOCATION),"bios irq 8-15 default handler");
06266 
06267                 /* BIOS boot stages */
06268                 cb_bios_post.Install(&cb_bios_post__func,CB_RETF,"BIOS POST");
06269                 cb_bios_scan_video_bios.Install(&cb_bios_scan_video_bios__func,CB_RETF,"BIOS Scan Video BIOS");
06270                 cb_bios_adapter_rom_scan.Install(&cb_bios_adapter_rom_scan__func,CB_RETF,"BIOS Adapter ROM scan");
06271                 cb_bios_startup_screen.Install(&cb_bios_startup_screen__func,CB_RETF,"BIOS Startup screen");
06272                 cb_bios_boot.Install(&cb_bios_boot__func,CB_RETF,"BIOS BOOT");
06273 
06274                 // Compatible POST routine location: jump to the callback
06275                 {
06276                         Bitu wo_fence;
06277 
06278                         wo = Real2Phys(BIOS_DEFAULT_RESET_LOCATION);
06279                         wo_fence = wo + 64;
06280 
06281                         // POST
06282                         phys_writeb(wo+0x00,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                               //GRP 4
06283                         phys_writeb(wo+0x01,(Bit8u)0x38);                                               //Extra Callback instruction
06284                         phys_writew(wo+0x02,(Bit16u)cb_bios_post.Get_callback());                       //The immediate word
06285                         wo += 4;
06286 
06287                         // video bios scan
06288                         phys_writeb(wo+0x00,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                               //GRP 4
06289                         phys_writeb(wo+0x01,(Bit8u)0x38);                                               //Extra Callback instruction
06290                         phys_writew(wo+0x02,(Bit16u)cb_bios_scan_video_bios.Get_callback());            //The immediate word
06291                         wo += 4;
06292 
06293                         // adapter ROM scan
06294                         phys_writeb(wo+0x00,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                               //GRP 4
06295                         phys_writeb(wo+0x01,(Bit8u)0x38);                                               //Extra Callback instruction
06296                         phys_writew(wo+0x02,(Bit16u)cb_bios_adapter_rom_scan.Get_callback());           //The immediate word
06297                         wo += 4;
06298 
06299                         // startup screen
06300                         phys_writeb(wo+0x00,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                               //GRP 4
06301                         phys_writeb(wo+0x01,(Bit8u)0x38);                                               //Extra Callback instruction
06302                         phys_writew(wo+0x02,(Bit16u)cb_bios_startup_screen.Get_callback());             //The immediate word
06303                         wo += 4;
06304 
06305             // user boot hook
06306             if (bios_user_boot_hook != 0) {
06307                 phys_writeb(wo+0x00,0x9C);                          //PUSHF
06308                 phys_writeb(wo+0x01,0x9A);                          //CALL FAR
06309                 phys_writew(wo+0x02,0x0000);                        //seg:0
06310                 phys_writew(wo+0x04,bios_user_boot_hook>>4);
06311                 wo += 6;
06312             }
06313 
06314                         // boot
06315             BIOS_boot_code_offset = wo;
06316                         phys_writeb(wo+0x00,(Bit8u)0xFE);                                               //GRP 4
06317                         phys_writeb(wo+0x01,(Bit8u)0x38);                                               //Extra Callback instruction
06318                         phys_writew(wo+0x02,(Bit16u)cb_bios_boot.Get_callback());                       //The immediate word
06319                         wo += 4;
06320 
06321                         /* fence */
06322                         phys_writeb(wo++,0xEB);                                                         // JMP $-2
06323                         phys_writeb(wo++,0xFE);
06324 
06325                         if (wo > wo_fence) E_Exit("BIOS boot callback overrun");
06326                 }
06327         }
06328         ~BIOS(){
06329                 /* snap the CPU back to real mode. this code thinks in terms of 16-bit real mode
06330                  * and if allowed to do it's thing in a 32-bit guest OS like WinNT, will trigger
06331                  * a page fault. */
06332                 CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode();
06333 
06334                 if (BOCHS_PORT_E9) {
06335                         delete BOCHS_PORT_E9;
06336                         BOCHS_PORT_E9=NULL;
06337                 }
06338                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT) {
06339                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT;
06340                         ISAPNP_PNP_ADDRESS_PORT=NULL;
06341                 }
06342                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT) {
06343                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT;
06344                         ISAPNP_PNP_DATA_PORT=NULL;
06345                 }
06346                 if (ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT) {
06347                         delete ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT;
06348                         ISAPNP_PNP_READ_PORT=NULL;
06349                 }
06350         if (isapnpigdevice) {
06351             /* ISA PnP will auto-free it */
06352             isapnpigdevice=NULL;
06353         }
06354 
06355         if (dosbox_int_iocallout != IO_Callout_t_none) {
06356             IO_FreeCallout(dosbox_int_iocallout);
06357             dosbox_int_iocallout = IO_Callout_t_none;
06358         }
06359 
06360                 /* abort DAC playing */
06361                 if (tandy_sb.port) {
06362                         IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0xd3);
06363                         IO_Write(tandy_sb.port+0xc,0xd0);
06364                 }
06365                 real_writeb(0x40,0xd4,0x00);
06366                 if (tandy_DAC_callback[0]) {
06367                         Bit32u orig_vector=real_readd(0x40,0xd6);
06368                         if (orig_vector==tandy_DAC_callback[0]->Get_RealPointer()) {
06369                                 /* set IRQ vector to old value */
06370                                 Bit8u tandy_irq = 7;
06371                                 if (tandy_sb.port) tandy_irq = tandy_sb.irq;
06372                                 else if (tandy_dac.port) tandy_irq = tandy_dac.irq;
06373                                 Bit8u tandy_irq_vector = tandy_irq;
06374                                 if (tandy_irq_vector<8) tandy_irq_vector += 8;
06375                                 else tandy_irq_vector += (0x70-8);
06376 
06377                                 RealSetVec(tandy_irq_vector,real_readd(0x40,0xd6));
06378                                 real_writed(0x40,0xd6,0x00000000);
06379                         }
06380                         delete tandy_DAC_callback[0];
06381                         delete tandy_DAC_callback[1];
06382                         tandy_DAC_callback[0]=NULL;
06383                         tandy_DAC_callback[1]=NULL;
06384                 }
06385 
06386                 /* encourage the callback objects to uninstall HERE while we're in real mode, NOT during the
06387                  * destructor stage where we're back in protected mode */
06388                 for (unsigned int i=0;i < 20;i++) callback[i].Uninstall();
06389 
06390         /* assume these were allocated */
06391         CALLBACK_DeAllocate(call_irq0);
06392         CALLBACK_DeAllocate(call_irq07default);
06393         CALLBACK_DeAllocate(call_irq815default);
06394 
06395                 /* done */
06396                 CPU_Snap_Back_Restore();
06397         }
06398 };
06399 
06400 void BIOS_Enter_Boot_Phase(void) {
06401     /* direct CS:IP right to the instruction that leads to the boot process */
06402     /* note that since it's a callback instruction it doesn't really matter
06403      * what CS:IP is as long as it points to the instruction */
06404     reg_eip = BIOS_boot_code_offset & 0xFUL;
06405         CPU_SetSegGeneral(cs, BIOS_boot_code_offset >> 4UL);
06406 }

06408 void BIOS_SetCOMPort(Bitu port, Bit16u baseaddr) {
06409         switch(port) {
06410         case 0:
06411                 mem_writew(BIOS_BASE_ADDRESS_COM1,baseaddr);
06412                 mem_writeb(BIOS_COM1_TIMEOUT, 10); // FIXME: Right??
06413                 break;
06414         case 1:
06415                 mem_writew(BIOS_BASE_ADDRESS_COM2,baseaddr);
06416                 mem_writeb(BIOS_COM2_TIMEOUT, 10); // FIXME: Right??
06417                 break;
06418         case 2:
06419                 mem_writew(BIOS_BASE_ADDRESS_COM3,baseaddr);
06420                 mem_writeb(BIOS_COM3_TIMEOUT, 10); // FIXME: Right??
06421                 break;
06422         case 3:
06423                 mem_writew(BIOS_BASE_ADDRESS_COM4,baseaddr);
06424                 mem_writeb(BIOS_COM4_TIMEOUT, 10); // FIXME: Right??
06425                 break;
06426         }
06427 }
06428 
06429 void BIOS_SetLPTPort(Bitu port, Bit16u baseaddr) {
06430         switch(port) {
06431         case 0:
06432                 mem_writew(BIOS_ADDRESS_LPT1,baseaddr);
06433                 mem_writeb(BIOS_LPT1_TIMEOUT, 10);
06434                 break;
06435         case 1:
06436                 mem_writew(BIOS_ADDRESS_LPT2,baseaddr);
06437                 mem_writeb(BIOS_LPT2_TIMEOUT, 10);
06438                 break;
06439         case 2:
06440                 mem_writew(BIOS_ADDRESS_LPT3,baseaddr);
06441                 mem_writeb(BIOS_LPT3_TIMEOUT, 10);
06442                 break;
06443         }
06444 }
06445 
06446 void BIOS_PnP_ComPortRegister(Bitu port,Bitu irq) {
06447         /* add to PnP BIOS */
06448         if (ISAPNPBIOS) {
06449                 unsigned char tmp[256];
06450                 int i;
06451 
06452                 /* register serial ports */
06453                 const unsigned char h1[9] = {
06454                         ISAPNP_SYSDEV_HEADER(
06455                                 ISAPNP_ID('P','N','P',0x0,0x5,0x0,0x1), /* PNP0501 16550A-compatible COM port */
06456                                 ISAPNP_TYPE(0x07,0x00,0x02),            /* type: RS-232 communcations device, 16550-compatible */
06457                                 0x0001 | 0x0002)
06458                 };
06459 
06460                 i = 0;
06461                 memcpy(tmp+i,h1,9); i += 9;                     /* can't disable, can't configure */
06462                 /*----------allocated--------*/
06463                 tmp[i+0] = (8 << 3) | 7;                        /* IO resource */
06464                 tmp[i+1] = 0x01;                                /* 16-bit decode */
06465                 host_writew(tmp+i+2,port);                      /* min */
06466                 host_writew(tmp+i+4,port);                      /* max */
06467                 tmp[i+6] = 0x10;                                /* align */
06468                 tmp[i+7] = 0x08;                                /* length */
06469                 i += 7+1;
06470 
06471                 if (irq > 0) {
06472                         tmp[i+0] = (4 << 3) | 3;                        /* IRQ resource */
06473                         host_writew(tmp+i+1,1 << irq);
06474                         tmp[i+3] = 0x09;                                /* HTL=1 LTL=1 */
06475                         i += 3+1;
06476                 }
06477 
06478                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
06479                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
06480                 i += 2;
06481                 /*-------------possible-----------*/
06482                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
06483                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
06484                 i += 2;
06485                 /*-------------compatible---------*/
06486                 tmp[i+0] = 0x79;                                /* END TAG */
06487                 tmp[i+1] = 0x00;
06488                 i += 2;
06489 
06490                 if (!ISAPNP_RegisterSysDev(tmp,i)) {
06491                         //LOG_MSG("ISAPNP register failed\n");
06492                 }
06493         }
06494 }

06498 void BIOS_Destroy(Section* /*sec*/){
06499         ROMBIOS_DumpMemory();
06500         ISA_PNP_FreeAllDevs();
06501         if (test != NULL) {
06502                 delete test;
06503                 test = NULL;
06504         }
06505 }
06506 
06507 void BIOS_OnPowerOn(Section* sec) {
06508         if (test) delete test;
06509         test = new BIOS(control->GetSection("joystick"));
06510 }

06512 void swapInNextDisk(bool pressed);
06513 void swapInNextCD(bool pressed);
06514 
06515 void INT10_OnResetComplete();
06516 void CALLBACK_DeAllocate(Bitu in);
06517 
06518 void MOUSE_Unsetup_DOS(void);
06519 void MOUSE_Unsetup_BIOS(void);
06520 
06521 void BIOS_OnResetComplete(Section *x) {
06522     INT10_OnResetComplete();
06523 
06524     if (biosConfigSeg != 0) {
06525         ROMBIOS_FreeMemory(biosConfigSeg << 4); /* remember it was alloc'd paragraph aligned, then saved >> 4 */
06526         biosConfigSeg = 0;
06527     }
06528 
06529     call_pnp_rp = 0;
06530     if (call_pnp_r != ~0UL) {
06531         CALLBACK_DeAllocate(call_pnp_r);
06532         call_pnp_r = ~0UL;
06533     }
06534 
06535     call_pnp_pp = 0;
06536     if (call_pnp_p != ~0UL) {
06537         CALLBACK_DeAllocate(call_pnp_p);
06538         call_pnp_p = ~0UL;
06539     }
06540 
06541     MOUSE_Unsetup_DOS();
06542     MOUSE_Unsetup_BIOS();
06543 
06544     ISA_PNP_FreeAllSysNodeDevs();
06545 }
06546 
06547 void BIOS_Init() {
06548         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Initializing BIOS");
06549 
06550         /* make sure the array is zeroed */
06551         ISAPNP_SysDevNodeCount = 0;
06552         ISAPNP_SysDevNodeLargest = 0;
06553         for (int i=0;i < MAX_ISA_PNP_SYSDEVNODES;i++) ISAPNP_SysDevNodes[i] = NULL;
06554 
06555         /* make sure CD swap and floppy swap mapper events are available */
06556         MAPPER_AddHandler(swapInNextDisk,MK_f4,MMOD1,"swapimg","SwapFloppy"); /* Originally "Swap Image" but this version does not swap CDs */
06557         MAPPER_AddHandler(swapInNextCD,MK_f3,MMOD1,"swapcd","SwapCD"); /* Variant of "Swap Image" for CDs */
06558 
06559         /* NTS: VM_EVENT_BIOS_INIT this callback must be first. */
06560         AddExitFunction(AddExitFunctionFuncPair(BIOS_Destroy),false);
06561         AddVMEventFunction(VM_EVENT_POWERON,AddVMEventFunctionFuncPair(BIOS_OnPowerOn));
06562         AddVMEventFunction(VM_EVENT_RESET_END,AddVMEventFunctionFuncPair(BIOS_OnResetComplete));
06563 }
06564 
06565 void write_ID_version_string() {
06566         Bitu str_id_at,str_ver_at;
06567         size_t str_id_len,str_ver_len;
06568 
06569         /* NTS: We can't move the version and ID strings, it causes programs like MSD.EXE to lose
06570          *      track of the "IBM compatible blahblahblah" string. Which means that apparently
06571          *      programs looking for this information have the address hardcoded ALTHOUGH
06572          *      experiments show you can move the version string around so long as it's
06573          *      +1 from a paragraph boundary */
06574         /* TODO: *DO* allow dynamic relocation however if the dosbox.conf indicates that the user
06575          *       is not interested in IBM BIOS compatability. Also, it would be really cool if
06576          *       dosbox.conf could override these strings and the user could enter custom BIOS
06577          *       version and ID strings. Heh heh heh.. :) */
06578         str_id_at = 0xFE00E;
06579         str_ver_at = 0xFE061;
06580         str_id_len = strlen(bios_type_string)+1;
06581         str_ver_len = strlen(bios_version_string)+1;
06582         if (!mainline_compatible_bios_mapping) {
06583                 /* need to mark these strings off-limits so dynamic allocation does not overwrite them */
06584                 ROMBIOS_GetMemory(str_id_len+1,"BIOS ID string",1,str_id_at);
06585                 ROMBIOS_GetMemory(str_ver_len+1,"BIOS version string",1,str_ver_at);
06586         }
06587         if (str_id_at != 0) {
06588                 for (size_t i=0;i < str_id_len;i++) phys_writeb(str_id_at+i,bios_type_string[i]);
06589         }
06590         if (str_ver_at != 0) {
06591                 for (size_t i=0;i < str_ver_len;i++) phys_writeb(str_ver_at+i,bios_version_string[i]);
06592         }
06593 }
06594 
06595 extern Bit8u int10_font_08[256 * 8];
06596 
06597 /* NTS: Do not use callbacks! This function is called before CALLBACK_Init() */
06598 void ROMBIOS_Init() {
06599         Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06600         Bitu oi,i;
06601 
06602         // log
06603         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Initializing ROM BIOS");
06604 
06605         oi = section->Get_int("rom bios minimum size"); /* in KB */
06606         oi = (oi + 3) & ~3; /* round to 4KB page */
06607         if (oi > 128) oi = 128;
06608         if (oi == 0) oi = (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping && machine != MCH_PCJR) ? 128 : 64;
06609         if (oi < 8) oi = 8; /* because of some of DOSBox's fixed ROM structures we can only go down to 8KB */
06610         rombios_minimum_size = (oi << 10); /* convert to minimum, using size coming downward from 1MB */
06611 
06612         oi = section->Get_int("rom bios allocation max"); /* in KB */
06613         oi = (oi + 3) & ~3; /* round to 4KB page */
06614         if (oi > 128) oi = 128;
06615         if (oi == 0) oi = (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping && machine != MCH_PCJR) ? 128 : 64;
06616         if (oi < 8) oi = 8; /* because of some of DOSBox's fixed ROM structures we can only go down to 8KB */
06617         oi <<= 10;
06618         if (oi < rombios_minimum_size) oi = rombios_minimum_size;
06619         rombios_minimum_location = 0x100000 - oi; /* convert to minimum, using size coming downward from 1MB */
06620 
06621         /* in mainline compatible, make sure we cover the 0xF0000-0xFFFFF range */
06622         if (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping && rombios_minimum_location > 0xF0000) {
06623                 rombios_minimum_location = 0xF0000;
06624                 rombios_minimum_size = 0x10000;
06625         }
06626 
06627         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_DEBUG)("ROM BIOS range: 0x%05X-0xFFFFF",(int)rombios_minimum_location);
06628         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_DEBUG)("ROM BIOS range according to minimum size: 0x%05X-0xFFFFF",(int)(0x100000 - rombios_minimum_size));
06629 
06630         if (!MEM_map_ROM_physmem(rombios_minimum_location,0xFFFFF)) E_Exit("Unable to map ROM region as ROM");
06631 
06632         /* and the BIOS alias at the top of memory (TODO: what about 486/Pentium emulation where the BIOS at the 4GB top is different
06633          * from the BIOS at the legacy 1MB boundary because of shadowing and/or decompressing from ROM at boot? */
06634         {
06635                 bool MEM_map_ROM_alias_physmem(Bitu start,Bitu end);
06636                 Bit32u MEM_get_address_bits();
06637 
06638                 uint64_t top = (uint64_t)1UL << (uint64_t)MEM_get_address_bits();
06639                 if (top >= ((uint64_t)1UL << (uint64_t)21UL)) { /* 2MB or more */
06640                         unsigned long alias_base,alias_end;
06641 
06642                         alias_base = (unsigned long)top + (unsigned long)rombios_minimum_location - (unsigned long)0x100000UL;
06643                         alias_end = (unsigned long)top - (unsigned long)1UL;
06644 
06645                         LOG(LOG_BIOS,LOG_DEBUG)("ROM BIOS also mapping alias to 0x%08lx-0x%08lx",alias_base,alias_end);
06646                         if (!MEM_map_ROM_alias_physmem(alias_base,alias_end)) E_Exit("Unable to map ROM region as ROM alias");
06647                 }
06648         }
06649 
06650         /* set up allocation */
06651         rombios_alloc.name = "ROM BIOS";
06652         rombios_alloc.topDownAlloc = true;
06653         rombios_alloc.initSetRange(rombios_minimum_location,0xFFFF0 - 1);
06654 
06655         write_ID_version_string();
06656 
06657         /* some structures when enabled are fixed no matter what */
06658         if (!mainline_compatible_bios_mapping && rom_bios_8x8_cga_font) {
06659                 /* line 139, int10_memory.cpp: the 8x8 font at 0xF000:FA6E, first 128 chars.
06660                  * allocate this NOW before other things get in the way */
06661                 if (ROMBIOS_GetMemory(128*8,"BIOS 8x8 font (first 128 chars)",1,0xFFA6E) == 0) {
06662                         LOG_MSG("WARNING: Was not able to mark off 0xFFA6E off-limits for 8x8 font");
06663                 }
06664         }
06665 
06666         /* install the font */
06667         if (rom_bios_8x8_cga_font) {
06668                 for (i=0;i<128*8;i++) {
06669                         phys_writeb(PhysMake(0xf000,0xfa6e)+i,int10_font_08[i]);
06670                 }
06671         }
06672 
06673         if (mainline_compatible_bios_mapping) {
06674                 /* then mark the region 0xE000-0xFFF0 as off-limits.
06675                  * believe it or not, there's this whole range between 0xF3000 and 0xFE000 that remains unused! */
06676                 if (ROMBIOS_GetMemory(0xFFFF0-0xFE000,"BIOS with fixed layout",1,0xFE000) == 0)
06677                         E_Exit("Mainline compat bios mapping: failed to declare entire BIOS area off-limits");
06678         }
06679 
06680     /* we allow dosbox.conf to specify a binary blob to load into ROM BIOS and execute after reset.
06681      * we allow this for both hacker curiosity and automated CPU testing. */
06682     {
06683         std::string path = section->Get_string("call binary on reset");
06684         struct stat st;
06685 
06686         if (!path.empty() && stat(path.c_str(),&st) == 0 && S_ISREG(st.st_mode) && st.st_size <= (128*1024)) {
06687             Bitu base = ROMBIOS_GetMemory(st.st_size,"User reset vector binary",16/*page align*/,0);
06688 
06689             if (base != 0) {
06690                 FILE *fp = fopen(path.c_str(),"rb");
06691 
06692                 if (fp != NULL) {
06693                     /* NTS: Make sure memory base != NULL, and that it fits within 1MB.
06694                      *      memory code allocates a minimum 1MB of memory even if
06695                      *      guest memory is less than 1MB because ROM BIOS emulation
06696                      *      depends on it. */
06697                     assert(GetMemBase() != NULL);
06698                     assert((base+st.st_size) <= 0x100000);
06699                     fread(GetMemBase()+base,st.st_size,1,fp);
06700                     fclose(fp);
06701 
06702                     LOG_MSG("User reset vector binary '%s' loaded at 0x%lx",path.c_str(),(unsigned long)base);
06703                     bios_user_reset_vector_blob = base;
06704                 }
06705                 else {
06706                     LOG_MSG("WARNING: Unable to open file to load user reset vector binary '%s' into ROM BIOS memory",path.c_str());
06707                 }
06708             }
06709             else {
06710                 LOG_MSG("WARNING: Unable to load user reset vector binary '%s' into ROM BIOS memory",path.c_str());
06711             }
06712         }
06713     }
06714 
06715     /* we allow dosbox.conf to specify a binary blob to load into ROM BIOS and execute just before boot.
06716      * we allow this for both hacker curiosity and automated CPU testing. */
06717     {
06718         std::string path = section->Get_string("call binary on boot");
06719         struct stat st;
06720 
06721         if (!path.empty() && stat(path.c_str(),&st) == 0 && S_ISREG(st.st_mode) && st.st_size <= (128*1024)) {
06722             Bitu base = ROMBIOS_GetMemory(st.st_size,"User boot hook binary",16/*page align*/,0);
06723 
06724             if (base != 0) {
06725                 FILE *fp = fopen(path.c_str(),"rb");
06726 
06727                 if (fp != NULL) {
06728                     /* NTS: Make sure memory base != NULL, and that it fits within 1MB.
06729                      *      memory code allocates a minimum 1MB of memory even if
06730                      *      guest memory is less than 1MB because ROM BIOS emulation
06731                      *      depends on it. */
06732                     assert(GetMemBase() != NULL);
06733                     assert((base+st.st_size) <= 0x100000);
06734                     fread(GetMemBase()+base,st.st_size,1,fp);
06735                     fclose(fp);
06736 
06737                     LOG_MSG("User boot hook binary '%s' loaded at 0x%lx",path.c_str(),(unsigned long)base);
06738                     bios_user_boot_hook = base;
06739                 }
06740                 else {
06741                     LOG_MSG("WARNING: Unable to open file to load user boot hook binary '%s' into ROM BIOS memory",path.c_str());
06742                 }
06743             }
06744             else {
06745                 LOG_MSG("WARNING: Unable to load user boot hook binary '%s' into ROM BIOS memory",path.c_str());
06746             }
06747         }
06748     }
